title": "Ajoatao (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ajoatao - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#garlic #potatoes #potato #steamed #sauce #thermomix #grilled #fish #egg #parsley #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This garlic and potato sauce recipe is a translation of a recipe in Salsas y Alinos con Thermomix (Susaeta Ediciones)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 407\n|PortionCalories = 101\n|DatePublished=21st February 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Ajoatao (TM).jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Some like it Hot!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">That includes me \ud83d\ude0b</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Potato|potato]] [[Sauce|sauce]] recipe is a translation of a recipe in '''Salsas y Ali\u00f1os con [[Thermomix]] (Susaeta Ediciones)'''.  It is more like [[garlic]] [[mashed potatoes]], although it is served as a [[sauce]].  It can be served hot or cold.\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 400g [[Potato|potato]]\n| 1 [[free range egg]]\n| 3 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| A few [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]]\n| 50g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 500g water (I would use 750g as using only 500g the water boiled dry)\n| [[Pepper]]\n| [[Salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the water in the bowl for '''12 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1'''.  (You only really need to heat the water for about '''5 minutes''')\n| Peel and wash the [[Potatoes|potatoes]].\n| Cut them into medium sized pieces and place them in the Varoma bowl.\n| [[Steam]] for '''20 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Once cooked, reserve the [[Potatoes|potatoes]], empty the water and dry the bowl.\n| Chop the peeled [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves '''8 seconds / Speed 8'''. ('''4 seconds''' is sufficient)\n| Add a little [[Salt|salt]], a pinch of [[Pepper|pepper]], the [[Saffron|saffron]] and the [[Steamed|steamed]] [[Potatoes|potatoes]].\n| [[Blend]] until you have a thick pur\u00e9e.\n| Add the [[Egg|egg]] and mix for a '''few seconds / Speed 5'''.\n| Pour the [[Oil|oil]] onto the lid, little by little, keeping the [[Thermomix]] at '''Speed 4''', until you have the desired texture.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nYou can use this to accompany any type of [[Fish|fish]], especially those which are [[Grilled|grilled]], barbecued or [[Steamed|steamed]] in the Varoma.  At the same time, it goes well with red [[Meat|meat]], [[Meat|meat]] [[Fondues|fondues]], as an [[Aperitif|aperitif]], combined with other [[Sauces|sauces]]. \n===Variations===\nYou can give it a special touch by adding [[Oregano|oregano]] and [[Parsley|parsley]].  I sprinkled some smoked [[paprika]] over the top.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #potatoes #potato #steamed #sauce #thermomix #grilled #fish #egg #parsley #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

It is heavenly! \n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=31st January 2017\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  10 minutes plus 1 hour chilling time\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes plus 1 hour chilling time\n|CookTime = None\n|TotalCalories = 1864\n|PortionCalories = 310\n|Image = [[Image:Ajoblanco with pears TM recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love the parsley oil</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Delicious</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn alternative version of [[Ajo Blanco Malague\u00f1o (TM)|Ajo Blanco Malague\u00f1o]], an uncooked, chilled [[garlic]] [[soup]].  It is heavenly!\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 150 g [[Almonds|almonds]], skinned\n| 1 kg Conference [[Pears|pears]], peeled, cored and roughly chopped\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, peeled - I used 4 cloves, although I feel it could take more\n| 110g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 25ml [[Sherry|sherry]] vinegar\n| 2g (\u00bc tsp) [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] (you may need less if using [[Stock|stock]])\n| 175g water or [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n}}\n====For garnishing====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| Fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Blanched|blanched]] for 15 seconds, put into iced water, then patted dry\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Pine Nuts|Pine nuts]], [[Toasted|toasted]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Pears|pears]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]], half the [[Salt|salt]] and water or [[Stock|stock]] into the bowl '''1 minute / Speed 5-7-9'''\n| Check for seasoning and add more, [[Salt|salt]], [[Vinegar|vinegar]] and [[Oil|oil]] if necessary\n| If the [[Soup|soup]] is too thick, thin down with a little more water or [[Stock|stock]]\n| [[Blend]] again '''10 seconds / Speed 5'''\n| Chill for a minimum of 1 hour\n| Meanwhile, make [[Parsley|parsley]] [[Oil|oil]] by blending 1 part (by volume) to 3 parts [[Olive oil|olive oil]] (also by volume) until you have a green [[Sauce|sauce]] '''1 minute / Speed 5-7-9'''.  If you are only making a small amount, it would be best to use a [[stick blender]].\n| Once the [[Soup|soup]] has chilled, drizzle a little of the [[Parsley|parsley]] [[Oil|oil]] over it and sprinkle a few [[Pine Nuts|pine nuts]] on the top\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with crusty [[Bread|bread]]\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Translated and adapted for Thermomix from a [http://canalcocina.es/receta/ajoblanco-de-pera Canal Cocina] recipe\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#oliveoil #soup #stock #garlic #parsley #pears #almonds #pinenuts #vinegar #toasted #vegetablestock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This recipe is for the traditional hand-made allioli\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 28\n|PortionCalories = 28\n|DatePublished=12th April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 1\n|Difficulty = 3\n|TotalTime = 30 minutes\n|PrepTime = 30 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Allioli a la Catalana (traditional garlic and oil sauce) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Rosemary's daily dish!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Once you have the hang of this, it's easy</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]])</span></span>\n}}\nAllioli is the traditional [[Spanish]] [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Sauce|sauce]] that is eaten with [[Meat|meat]], [[Fish|fish]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]].\n\nThis recipe is for the traditional hand-made allioli ([[Garlic]] [[mayonnaise]]).  If you don't have 20 minutes of [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]] time available, you might want to take the short-cut and try our [[Allioli a la moderna|garlic sauce recipe]] that uses an electric [[Mixer|mixer]].  However if you have the time and need some therapy, read on\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, peeled\n| A pinch of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| &#189; teaspoon of fresh [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] from &#188; of a large [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 1.5 cups of [[Spanish]] extra virgin [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves to a large round mortar and smash the [[Cloves|cloves]] into a smooth paste\n| Add the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] to the [[Garlic|garlic]] paste\n| Then, drop-by-drop, add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], crushing the paste, turning the mortar as you go\n| Don't add the next drops of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] until the last have been completely amalgamated into the paste\n| After about 20 minutes you should have a [[Sauce|sauce]] the consistency of a very thick [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].\n| If it is too thick, you can add a drop or two of water to thin it out\n}}\n===Servings===\nServings: 12 - Makes 1 cup of alliloli\n===Chef's notes===\nDon't add the [[Oil|oil]] too quickly.\n==See also==\n* A huge variety of [[Garlic mayonnaise recipes|different mayonnaise recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #oliveoil #alliolialacatalana #spanish #mayonnaise #lemonjuice #sauce #fish #mortarandpestle #lemon #mixer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Allioli a la moderna",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Allioli a la moderna a garlic mayonnaise recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#alliolialamoderna #oliveoil #garlic #lemonjuice #foodprocessor #garlicmayonnaise #egg #garlicmayonnaiserecipes #spanish #unusualrecipes #vinegar \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The cheat's way to make allioli (Garlic mayonnaise) using an electric hand mixer or a food processor with a metal blade attachment\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 120\n|PortionCalories = 12\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 10 - Makes about 1 cup\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Allioli a la moderna recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Garlic Mayo!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great stuff Julia, superb with chips, it's like being in Paris, or Madrid!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Allioli a la moderna gently does it.jpg|thumb|300px|right|..little by little]]\nThe cheat's way to make allioli ([[Garlic mayonnaise]]) using an electric hand mixer or a [[food processor]] with a metal blade attachment.\n\nIf you have the time and want to try the authentic method using a pestle and mortar, we have the recipe for [[Allioli a la Catalana]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 small [[free range egg]]\n| 1 cup [[Spanish]] extra virgin [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 3 Cloves of [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]] or fresh [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Break the [[Egg|egg]] into a small mixing bowl\n| Add 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], the crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves and the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] or [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| If using a food processor, tip the contents of the bowl into the food processor \n| At full-speed, mix until the [[Garlic|garlic]] is combined into a paste\n| Little by little (don't rush this stage), add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] whilst blending at high speed\n| Add [[Salt|salt]] to taste - but not too much. My first attempt was ruined because it was too salty.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nIf the allioli is too thick, add a teaspoon of water to loosen it.\n\nIt will probably be too runny if you use a large egg, so if you have no choice of size, use less of the white.  You can always add more if needed; you can't take it out afterwards though!\n\nThis can also be made in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a blade attachment.\n\nIf you add the olive oil too quickly and the mixture separates into an oily mess, try the rescue method recommended by the award-winning Spanish chef, Jos\u00e9 Andr\u00e9s: \"Measure out 1 tablespoon of lukewarm water and add to the mix little by little until you have the creamy sauce you wanted\".\n\nHaving tried the above suggestion a few times to no avail, I would suggest adding another whole fresh egg into the split mixture, maybe a dash of nice vinegar and just blitz for a minute or so.  You'll hear the difference as the curdled mixture starts to coagulate properly.  This ''fix'' has worked for me, every time.\n==See also==\n* A huge variety of [[Garlic mayonnaise recipes|different mayonnaise recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#alliolialamoderna #oliveoil #garlic #lemonjuice #foodprocessor #garlicmayonnaise #egg #garlicmayonnaiserecipes #spanish #unusualrecipes #vinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Almogrote",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Almogrote a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#almogrote #cheese #mortarandpestle #goats #tucanarias #tomatoes #seeds #garlic #oliveoil #unusualrecipes #garlicmayonnaiserecipes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Almogrote is a delicious cheese paste that is a speciality of La Gomera in the Canary Islands\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1631\n|PortionCalories = 163\n|DatePublished=2nd January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 10 - Makes almost 1kg of [[Cheese|cheese]] paste\n|Difficulty = 3\n|TotalTime = 30 minutes\n|PrepTime = 30 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Almogrote recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\nAlmogrote is a delicious cheese paste that is a speciality of  La Gomera in the Canary Islands.  It is traditionally made with [[La Gomera|Queso de la Gomera]], an unpasteurised goats\u2019 cheese, which may be difficult to source outside of the Canaries.  [[TuCanarias]] can supply [[Queso de la Gomera]] though the postage costs may be prohibitive.\n\nThe word \"[[Almogrote]]\" does not even appear in [[Spanish]] dictionaries, although it is probably derived from the word \"almodrote\": a [[Sauce|sauce]] made from [[Oil|oil]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and other ingredients. Almogrote is always made using a [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]] - a basic wooden mortar and pestle.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500 g mature [[Goats|goats]] [[Cheese|cheese]]\n| 4 tablespoons of [[paprika]]\n| 1 whole [[Red chilli pepper|red chilli pepper]] with [[Seeds|seeds]]\n| 1 cup of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 10 [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]]\n| 300g [[tomatoes]], (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Chop the ingredients into small pieces\n| Grind the pieces to a paste using a large wooden [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]].\n}}\n===Type of cheese to use===\nOriginally, in a discussion with another editor, the oft-seen suggestion to use a 'hard' cheese for this recipe was possibly attributed to a (mis)-translation \"Sometimes the Spanish word 'duro' which means 'hard' can also mean 'mature' in cheese terms\", however the following quote was found:\n\n''Si hace falta martillo y escoplo para ello, el queso es el ideal'', [If you need a hammer and chisel for it, the cheese is the ideal (one)].\n\nSo the plot thickens!  If you can shed any further light on this quandary then please do add your thoughts to this, or the discussion page.\n\n===The non-authentic version===\n..and here's what happened when [[Talk:Almogrote|I tried to make the non-authentic version!]]\n==See also==\n* [[Almogrote gomero (TM)]]\n* [[Chilli sauce|Many other chilli sauce recipes]]\n* A huge variety of [[Garlic mayonnaise recipes|different mayonnaise recipes]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A lovely dip for crackers</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Los!  See my other attempt at this - there is a link in the recipe!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#almogrote #cheese #mortarandpestle #goats #tucanarias #tomatoes #seeds #garlic #oliveoil #unusualrecipes #garlicmayonnaiserecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Almogrote gomero (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Almogrote gomero - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tomatoes #garlic #cheese #roasting #stock #oliveoil #almogrote #bread #thermomix #thermomixrecipes #fridge \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This thick sauce originates from the Canary Islands and in particular the small island of Gomera\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 847\n|PortionCalories = 169\n|DatePublished=26th May 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = I like mine with a bit of texture\n|Servings = Serves 5 - Makes about 500ml\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 hour, 55 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 1 hour, 45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Almogrote gomero (TM) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A perfect pitta-dip</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Also good as a vegetable dip</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\nThis thick sauce originates from the Canary Islands and in particular the small island of Gomera.  It is traditional to use a cheese such as a mature [[Queso de la Gomera cheese|La Gomera]], but any strong, hard cheese will be fine.\n\n'''To [[Roast|roast]] the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 6 ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] (about 425g), cut in half\n| 4 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] or pink Himalayan [[Rock salt|rock salt]]\n}}\n'''To make the [[Almogrote|almogrote]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 8 large [[Cloves|cloves]] [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| 1-2 [[Guindilla peppers|guindilla peppers]]\n| 140g hard, mature, strong [[Cheese|cheese]], broken into chunks\n| The [[Roasted tomatoes|roasted tomatoes]], drained (reserve the [[Oil|oil]])\n| 90g [[Stock|stock]] of your choice\n| The reserved [[Olive oil|olive oil]], made up to 120ml\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to its highest setting.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Arrange the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] in a [[Roasting tin|roasting tin]], cut side up.\n| Drizzle the [[Oil|oil]] over them and lightly sprinkle with the [[Salt|salt]].\n| Place in the [[Oven|oven]] for 15 minutes, reduce the heat to 150\u00b0 C (300\u00b0 F - gas 2), [fan oven 130\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour] and continue [[Roasting|roasting]] for a further 1&frac12; hours, by which time the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] should have shrunk to half their original size.\n| Allow the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] to cool thoroughly or even leave them in the [[Fridge|fridge]] overnight.\n| Place the [[Garlic|garlic]], and [[Guindilla peppers|guindilla(s)]] in the TM bowl and process '''10 seconds / Speed 5'''.\n| Scrape down the inside of the bowl and add the [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| Process '''1 minute / Speed 5-10 progressively'''.\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and the [[Stock|stock]] and [[Blend|blend]] at '''Speed 5''' until you have the consistency of a paste.\n| Ensure the '''MC''' has open end upright and slowly pour the [[Oil|oil]] onto the lid of bowl, running at '''Speed 5''' until all the oil has been emulsified.\n| Continue blending until you have the desired consistency - I like mine with a bit of texture although you can make it as smooth as you like.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Boiled potatoes|boiled potatoes]] or papas arrugados, [[Hard boiled eggs|hard boiled eggs]] or simply spread it on [[Bread|bread]] or toast.  It can also be used as a [[Dip|dip]].\n===Recipe source===\n* The recipe is based on one in '''''Canarias - cocina tradicional''''' by Vicente Sanchez Ara\u00f1a (ISBN 9788444120157).  It has been translated, adapted and converted for [[Thermomix]].\n===Chef's notes===\nI doubled the ingredients listed in the original recipe, because I am a pig.  Also the [[Roasting|roasting]] of the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] was my idea, to add extra flavour, but there is no need to do so.\n\n==See also==\n* [[Almogrote]] and [[Talk:Almogrote|Almogrote - the non-authentic version]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tomatoes #garlic #cheese #roasting #stock #oliveoil #almogrote #bread #thermomix #thermomixrecipes #fridge </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

gas 8)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Grease a shallow [[Baking|baking]] dish or [[Casserole|casserole]] with some of the [[Oil|oil]].\n| Using a little more [[Oil|oil]], gently saut\u00e9 the [[Garlic|garlic]] until barely golden, reserving the oil.\n| Arrange a layer of [[Peppers|peppers]] on the bottom of the [[Baking|baking]] dish.\n| Sprinkle some of the [[Garlic|garlic]] over the [[Peppers|peppers]] and follow this with a layer of [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], seasoning between the layers.\n| Continue layering until you have used up the ingredients.\n| Pour the remaining [[Oil|oil]] and the oil in which you saut\u00e9ed the [[Garlic|garlic]] over the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and sprinkle with the [[Oregano|oregano]].\n| [[Bake]] for about 20-25 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Bread|bread]] to mop up the juices.  Can be served hot or cold.\n===Chef's notes===\nTo roast and remove the skins from peppers please follow these [[Roasted red pepper|instructions]].  \n\nYou can buy preserved roasted and de-skinned peppers in jars.  Some are good and others not so.  If you decide to opt for [[Bell peppers#Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa|Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa]], you will need to use quite a few as they are very small.  Sadly, they are rather expensive if bought in the UK.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Asadillo]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Asadillo]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Asadillo]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Asadillo]]\n[[Category:Starters|Asadillo]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Asadillo]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Asadillo]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#asadillo #garlic #peppers #tomatoes #oregano #baking #bread #casserole #vegetables #miseenplace #roastedredpepper </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Basque-style Puy lentils",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "\n<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basque-style Puy lentils recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#oliveoil #onion #lentils #bouquetgarni #basquestylepuylentils #france #parsley #pancetta #butter #boil #duckfat \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=As a keen surfer, we spent 15 years holidaying around Vieux-Boucau-les-Bains, in the Basque region of France. My version of the famous lentil dish.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1516\n|PortionCalories = 252\n|DatePublished=6th July 2016\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  25 minutes\n|CookTime =  1 hour\n|Image = [[Image:Basquestyle Puy lentils recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Worth hunting these down</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Not always easy to find sensibly priced Puy lentils, but it's worth the hunt as they are so much nicer than normal orange lentils.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>}}\n[[Image:Basque-style Puy lentils pre boil.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready to simmer]]\nAs a keen surfer, we spent 15 years holidaying around Vieux-Boucau-les-Bains, in the Basque region of [[France]].\n\nThis is my attempt at replicating the [[Lentil|lentil]] dishes found in this lovely area of [[France]] (and [[Spain]]!)\n\nThis would be made with [[Duck fat|duck fat]] and served with [[Foie gras|foie gras]] or [[Roast|roast]] [[Duck|duck]].  Not having any of the aforementioned to [[Hand|hand]] I'm using [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Butter|butter]] and I shall serve it with half a [[Crispy aromatic duck|crispy aromatic duck]] from our local [[Chinese wholesaler]]. Not entirely [[French]] then, but still delicious and a great basis for recipe customisation.\n\nThis can be made ahead of time and reheated in a [[Conventional oven|conventional oven]] or [[Microwave|microwave]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 225 g [8 oz] [[Puy lentils]]\n| 1 [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and slashed halfway through and studded with 2 [[Clove buds|clove buds]]\n| 1 large [[Carrot|carrot]], peeled and cut into small cubes\n| 160 g [5.5 oz] cubed [[Smoked|smoked]] [[Pancetta|pancetta]]\n| 6 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 4 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Butter|butter]]\n| Big handful of freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| Splash of [[White wine|white wine]] or [[Sherry|sherry]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Rinse the [[Lentils|lentils]] in a [[Sieve|sieve]] under cold running water\n| Pop the [[Lentils|lentils]] in a large pan, well covered with cold water and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]. Use filtered water if you are in a hard water area.\n| Immediately the water boils, remove from the heat and drain in a [[Colander|colander]], discarding the water.\n| Give the [[Saucepan|saucepan]] a wipe round add the [[Lentils|lentils]] and cover with 1 litre [1.24 [[Pints|pints]]] of cold water.\n| Sprinkle in 1 teaspoon of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and add the [[Clove|clove]] studded [[Onion|onion]], the [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]], half of the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] and the chopped [[Carrot|carrot]].\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] uncovered for 15 minutes, skimming any scum from the surface as required.  Check from time to time and top up with [[Boiling|boiling]] water if it's getting low.\n| Remove and drain, discarding the [[Clove|clove]]-studded [[Onion|onion]] and the [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]].\n| Heat a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or [[Wok|wok]] with a generous pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]], half of the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] off half of the [[Pancetta|pancetta]] until it starts to [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add the chopped [[Onion|onion]] and cook gently for 10 minutes.\n| Add the remaining [[olive oil]] and the butter together with the remaining [[Bacon|bacon]] and cook slowly for another 5 minutes.\n| Add the chopped [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for a few minutes.  Once it starts to take the slightest colour, stir in the [[Lentils|lentils]] and [[Carrots|carrots]].\n| Allow the [[Lentils|lentils]] to re-heat, stir in the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]], season and serve.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nI've served this with half a [[Shredded|shredded]] [[Roasted|roasted]] [[Crispy duck|crispy duck]], which cooks from [[Frozen|frozen]] in about 40 minutes.  Delicious!\n===Variations===\nUse [[Duck fat|duck fat]] instead of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] if you can get it.\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#oliveoil #onion #lentils #bouquetgarni #basquestylepuylentils #france #parsley #pancetta #butter #boil #duckfat </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Add some [[Beans|beans]] for body, [[Peppers|peppers]] for richness and [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]], just because you can, you have a complete, gorgeous meal. Try it\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 400 g can of [[Haricot beans|haricot beans]], rinsed many times and then drained.\n| 2 sweet [[Bell peppers|bell peppers]], any colour.\n| 1 [[Fennel bulb|fennel bulb]], sliced finely, green tops reserved, if you are lucky enough to find a seller that retains them!\n| Half an [[Onion|onion]], very thinly sliced.\n| A small handful of freshly chopped [[oregano leaves]].\n| A large handful of freshly chopped [[parsley leaves]].\n| 1 tablespoon of [[olive oil]]\n| [[Sea salt]] & [[freshly ground black pepper]] to taste.\n| A squeeze of fresh [[lemon juice]].\n| 1 teaspoon [[fennel seeds]], bruised in a [[mortar and pestle]].\n| 3 teaspoons of [[sherry vinegar]].\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* [[Roasted red pepper|Roast the bell peppers as shown here]], remove skin and seeds then tear into strips.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the beans, sliced [[fennel]], [[fennel seeds]] and [[onions]] together with the [[roasted pepper]] strips in a serving bowl. Add the [[parsley]], [[oregano]] and reserved [[fennel tops]] if you had any. Toss well.\n| Drizzle with [[sherry vinegar]], [[lemon juice]] and [[olive oil]], Season with salt and pepper and toss again..\n}}\n===Alternatives===\nTry a variety of [[beans]], most beans work very well in a salad like this.  [[Butter beans]], [[chick peas]]. [[kidney beans]] etc.  Dried beans are good too if you remember to prepare them ahead of time.\n\nTry [[cumin seeds]] instead of [[fennel seeds]]\n===Chef's note===\nIf you can't find [[sherry vinegar]], then try harder as it's an invaluable condiment Or use [[red wine vinegar]] with a pinch of sugar!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sherryvinegar #fennelseeds #beansaladwithfennelandroastedpeppers #beans #fennel #oliveoil #onion #lemonjuice #salad #bellpeppers #fennelbulb </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

However, bream in general is a traditional Christmas Eve first course\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2080\n|PortionCalories = 520\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Carp bream\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour, 5 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 50 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Carp bream.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Couldn't find bream locally</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">But this was nice with trout instead</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nStuffed sea [[Bream|bream]], served throughout Spain as a dish for St Valentine's day. Unlike the cornbread typical of the southern United States, broa is made from a mixture of [[Cornmeal|cornmeal]] and [[Wheat|wheat]] or [[Rye flour|rye flour]], and is [[Leavened|leavened]] with [[Yeast|yeast]] rather than [[Baking powder|baking powder]] or [[Baking soda|baking soda]].\n\nThis yeast bread has the wholesome rustic flavour and texture that suitably accompanies soups, especially [[Caldo Verde]], the Portuguese green soup made with tender [[kale]], [[potatoes]], and [[chouri\u00e7o sausages]]. It has a wonderful crunchy crust when freshly baked.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 teaspoons [[Dried active yeast|dried active yeast]]\n| 150 ml (1/4 pint) tepid [[Milk|milk]]\n| 200 ml (7 fl oz) tepid water\n| 200 g [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]]\n| 300 g (10 oz) [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]]\n| 1 level teaspoon of [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the ingredients to your [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]].\n| Set to Whole wheat - Bake rapid [[Panasonic SD253 breadmaker]]\n| Use menu 05 ''Whole wheat rapid bake'' (3 hours) on [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]]\n|* Ideally: 15 min rest / 25 min [[Kneading bread|knead]] / 1:40 min rise / 45 min [[Bake|bake]]\n| Remove and cool on a wire tray once [[Baking|baking]] is complete.\n}}\n===Variations===\nPlease [[Talk:Broa|discuss other bake setting here]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes]]\n[[Category:Portuguese recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#broa #baking #driedactiveyeast #kneadingbread #ryeflour #panasonicsd253breadmaker #kale #bakingpowder #yeast #bake #potatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This version is particularly popular in [[Spain]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| [[Garlic|garlic]] to taste, peeled\n| A handful flat [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| 2 [[Carrots|carrots]], peeled\n| 1 12cm piece of thick [[Mooli|mooli]], peeled\n| 1 [[Parsnip|parsnip]], peeled\n| 1 stick [[Celery|celery]] including leafy part\n| 2 [[Leeks|leeks]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]] (The total of the above should weigh about 820g)\n| 200g [[Salt|salt]]\n| 20g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Chop the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] into chunks, place them into the TM bowl and blitz progressively from '''Speed 7-10''' until the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] are vary finely chopped.\n| Add the [[Salt|salt]] and the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and and set '''30 mins/100\u00ba/Speed 2&frac12;'''.\n| Then blitz progressively from '''Speed 7-10/30 seconds'''. \n| Store in the [[Fridge|fridge]] in a jar or [[Lock&lock box]].\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* Very slightly adapted from a recipe on '''[http://www.forumthermomix.com/index.php?topic=836.0 Forum Thermomix]'''\n===Chef's notes===\nI use about 4 tsps of concentrate to 1 litre of liquid, but you may wish to adjust according to your taste.  \n\nThe [[Salt|salt]] quantity may appear to be massive, but because you only use small amounts at a time, it will not taste over salty.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Vegetable stock concentrate]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Vegetable stock concentrate]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes|Vegetable stock concentrate]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes|Vegetable stock concentrate]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Vegetable stock concentrate]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes|Vegetable stock concentrate]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#vegetables #fridge #oliveoil #thermomix #mooli #onion #garlic #leeks #parsley #carrots #spain </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This vegetarian pesto is made with butternut squash, always available at this festive time\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 810\n|PortionCalories = 202\n|DatePublished=3rd January 2015\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  1 hour\n|Image = [[Image:Butternut squash pisto.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Vegalicious!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Top marks Julia - A lovely vegetarian meal which we really enjoyed making.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nPisto is the [[Spanish]] equivalent of [[Ratatouille|ratatouille]].  This [[Vegetarian|vegetarian]] [[Pesto|pesto]] is made with [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]], always available at this festive time of year.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1.2 kg [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]], peeled and chopped into 2cm pieces - about 800g once prepared\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Old India Taco Seasoning]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| A good pinch of [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 3 medium [[Onions|onions]], peeled and chopped\n| 1 [[Red pepper|red pepper]], deseeded, halved and cut into rings\n| 2 [[Green Indian chillies|green indian chillies]], thinly sliced, deseeded if you wish\n| 1 large [[Sprig of rosemary|sprig of rosemary]], left whole\n| 4 freshly picked [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]]\n| 3 [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]], peeled and thinly sliced\n| 1 teaspoon [[Mexican oregano]]\n| A pinch of [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]]\n| A pinch of freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| 180ml [[Passata|passata]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Port|port]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n}}\n''' to garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 tablespoons [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pop the [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] chunks into a [[Sieve|sieve]] and dust with the [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], set to one side.\n| Add the [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or even a [[Wok|wok]].\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and gently saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] for 15 minutes.\n| Add the sliced [[Red pepper|red pepper]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 10 minutes.\n| Now to liven it up; add the sliced [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], whole [[Sprig of rosemary|sprig of rosemary]] and finally the [[Garlic|garlic]] slices.  [[Stir-fry]] these for a few minutes.\n| Give the [[Sieve|sieve]] of [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] a shake to remove any liquid that may have leached out and add the [[Squash|squash]] to the pan.\n| Very gently saut\u00e9 the [[Squash|squash]] for 20 minutes, turning regularly.\n| After 20 minutes add the [[Passata|passata]], [[Port|port]], [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]], [[Mexican oregano]], and a grate of [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]] and heat for the final 10 minutes.\n| Remove the stem of the [[rosemary]] sprig and serve.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe garnished with [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]]\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you don't have [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and &#189; teaspoon of unsmoked [[Paprika]] will work just as well.\n{{Template:Pisto recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butternutsquash #squash #pinenuts #cuminseeds #bayleaves #sieve #port #onions #nutmeg #butternutsquashpisto #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chanfaina",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chanfaina, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chanfaina #carrots #potatoes #stock #lamb #tomato #onions #porktenderloin #breadcrumbs #meats #saffron \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a stew made with mixed meat. My husband and daughter enjoyed this in a restaurant near to the city of Antequera (Malaga)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4599\n|PortionCalories = 1149\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chanfaina recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n===Recipe review===\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">love the eggs</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Very Spanish, Julia!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a [[Stew|stew]] made with mixed [[Meat|meat]].  My husband and daughter enjoyed this in a restaurant near to the city of [[Antequera]] (M\u00e1laga). There are many variations of this recipe so I have tried to re create it as near as I can to that which they ate. The orginal had [[goat]] instead of [[lamb]], but it is not easy to come by in the UK.  However, our butcher said he can get it for us.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 45 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 kg [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled and cut into slices\n| 2 large [[Carrots|carrots]], peeled and sliced\n| 2 large [[Onions|onions]], peeled and sliced\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, [[Diced|diced]] - we used 2 bulbs\n| 1 kg in total of [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]], [[Pork tenderloin|pork tenderloin]] and [[Shoulder|shoulder]] of [[Lamb|lamb]]\n| 1 [[Red pepper|red pepper]], chopped\n| 1 teaspoon [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]]\n| 2 tablespoons sweet [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]] (Piment\u00f3n de la Vera), or to taste\n| A few [[saffron]] strands, crushed with a [[pestle and mortar]]\n| 1 large [[Tomato|tomato]], skinned\n| 1.3 lites (approx) [[Stock]] or water\n| 200 g [[Long grain rice|long grain rice]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 40 g [[Ground almonds|ground almonds]]\n| 125 ml manzanilla or very [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| Seasoning\n| 2 [[Eggs, hard-boiled|eggs, hard-boiled]] and cut into slices\n| [[Parsley]], chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large deep pan and [[Saute|saute]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and [[Carrots|carrots]] until they are golden.\n| Remove them from the pan and reserve.\n| [[Fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] in the same pan until soft, then add the [[Meats|meats]].\n| Cook until the [[Meats|meats]] are sealed.\n| Add the [[Pepper|pepper]] and cook for a minute or so then stir in the [[Cumin|cumin]], [[Paprika|paprika]] and [[saffron]], cooking for a further 30 seconds.\n| Mix in the [[Tomato|tomato]], and return the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and [[Carrots|carrots]] to the pan and add enough hot [[Stock|stock]] or water to cover.  \n| Add more [[Stock|stock]] or water as needed throughout the cooking process.\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] until about 15 minutes before you think the [[Meat|meat]] will be done, then add the [[Rice|rice]], [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]], [[Almonds|almonds]] and [[Sherry|sherry]]. \n| Cover and cook for a further 15 minutes.\n| Check seasoning and serve, garnished with the [[Egg|egg]] slices and [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nSome variations use just [[pork]] or [[lamb]], but would be a mixture of, for example, [[heart]], [[liver]] and flesh.  The version from C\u00f3rdoba uses [[pork tenderloin]], whole [[chicken]] pieces, [[morcilla]] and [[chorizo]].\n===Chef's notes===\nRemember to make sure the liquid does not evaporate too much or it will stick to the pan.  It should have a thickish consistency though.  By the way, the verdict was that it is very, very similar to that meal in Antequera!\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine|Chanfaina]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chanfaina #carrots #potatoes #stock #lamb #tomato #onions #porktenderloin #breadcrumbs #meats #saffron </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

you have to like [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] though!\n\nIn smaller quantities, this would make a nice [[Starter|starter]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 225 g thinly sliced [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]] \n| 3 large [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] cut into bite sized chunks\n| A handful of [[Cherry tomatoes|cherry tomatoes]]\n| 2 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| [[Sherry vinegar]]\n| 2  [[Shallots|shallots]], peeled and sliced or 4 or 5 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], [[Cut on the diagonal|cut on the diagonal]]\n| [[Extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 100g [[Goats cheese|goats cheese]], (one small round)\n| A big handful of [[herbs]] of your choice\n|* try [[Basil|basil]], [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Mint|mint]] or [[Chervil|chervil]]\n| Crusty [[Bread|bread]] to serve\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Onions|onions]] and [[Herbs|herbs]] to a serving bowl\n| Divide the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] in to two portions.\n| Heat a few tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], add the Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] and a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and [[Fry|fry]] half of the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] over a medium heat until crispy - this won't take very long if the chorizo is thinly sliced.\n| Once crispy, transfer the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] to the serving bowl\n| De-glaze the [[Frying pan|frying pan]] with a tablespoon or so of [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]].  Use this to dress the [[Salad|salad]] and mix well.\n| Season to taste\n| [[Crumble]] the [[Cheese|cheese]] over the [[Salad|salad]] and serve\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chorizoandtomatosalad #chorizo #tomatoes #salad #sherryvinegar #garlic #herbs #chervil #oliveoil #parsley #springonions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I have not tried drying or [[Preserving|preserving]] them in any way, though I guess it would be possible with this recipe. For this reason, I don't bother to get the casings, I just make the [[sausages]] like patties or burgers.\n\nUse these in [[:Special:Whatlinkshere/Chorizo_sausage|any recipe that calls for chorizo sausages]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.5 tablespoons [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n| 1 large [[Dried|dried]] [[Poblano|poblano]] [[Chili|chili]], stalk removed\n| 4 fresh [[Habanero|habanero]] [[Chillies|chillies]], stlaks removed or 3 teaspoons hot [[Chili powder|chili powder]]\n| 675 g (1.5 lb) lean [[Pork|pork]] ([[Pork fillet|pork fillet]] is good here) , chopped coarsely\n| 1 tablespoon fresh [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], chopped\n| 6 [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Paprika powder|paprika powder]] or [[Smoked paprika powder|smoked paprika powder]] if you can find it\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| &#188; teaspoon [[Ground cloves|ground cloves]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Spices|spices]], [[Chillies|chillies]] and the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] to a small [[Blender|blender]] attachment and grind to a paste.  A [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]] will do the job, just takes a bit more work!\n| Add the [[Pork|pork]] and the [[Spice|spice]] paste to a [[Food processor|food processor]] and pulse blend until you have a coarse mix.  Don't overdo this or you will end up with [[Pate|pate]] which is not what you need\n| Roll into [[Sausage|sausage]] shapes or flat patties\n| Preheat the oven to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5)\n| Cook for 20 minutes on a lightly oiled oven tray\n| Verify the [[Meat|meat]] is cooked properly as it is [[Pork|pork]] remember\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot or cold\n\n===Variations===\nAdjust the amount of [[Chili|chili]] to your personal taste.  I like mine quite hot.\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pork #chili #chillies #poblano #porkfillet #groundcinnamon #smokedpaprikapowder #chorizosausages #vinegar #chilipowder #blender </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Meat|meat]] is readily available.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Olive oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n| 1 slice good, stale [[Bread|bread]], cut into pieces\n| 1 bulb [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and chopped\n| 900 g [[Goat|kid]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| Pinch of sweet, [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]]\n| Pinch of [[Dried|dried]] [[Oregano|oregano]] or [[Marjoram|marjoram]]\n| 2 [[Bay leaves|bay C/350 F/ Gas 4\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a small pan and add the [[Bread|bread]] and [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| [[Fry]] until the [[Garlic|garlic]] is slightly [[Brown|brown]] and transfer to a [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]].\n| Sear the kid in the same pan and add to the [[Casserole|casserole]].\n| Mix the [[Paprika|paprika]], [[Oregano|oregano]], [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]] and the seasoning together and then pour it over the [[Meat|meat]].\n| Add the [[White wine|white wine]] and cook (uncovered) at 180 C/350 F/ Gas 4 for about an hour and a half or until the [[Meat|meat]] is tender.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with lots of fresh [[Bread|bread]].\n===Variations===\nKid is difficult to get in UK, so you can (as indeed the [[Spanish]] do) use lean [[Lamb|lamb]] instead.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe dish should still have quite a bit of liquid at the end of the cooking period.  If you find that it evaporates too quickly, cover it with a lid.\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 10:58, 30 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Kid]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Kid]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes|Kid]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Kid]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Kid]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Kid]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Kid]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #bread #sherryvinegar #casserole #oregano #bayleaves #dried #oliveoil #diced #paprika #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Varoma / Speed 2 / 40 minutes'''.\n| Allow to cool and keep in the [[Fridge|fridge]] in an [[Air-tight container|airtight container]].\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you wish to achieve a darker colour, transfer to a small saucepan and reduce for a further 2-3 minutes.  When a recipe calls for [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e use 1 part paste to 1 part water.\n\nThe original suggests around 20g [[Sugar|sugar]], but I feel that would make it far too sweet.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#oliveoil #tomatoes #seeds #tomato #fridge #chinois #sieve #thermomixrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Couscous, pepper and garlic salad a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#couscouspepperandgarlicsalad #garlic #oliveoil #butter #preserved #peppers #tomatojuice #roastedredpeppers #boil #chickenstock #stock \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Roasted peppers, garlic and couscous in a delicious salad\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1244\n|PortionCalories = 311\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 3 hours, 10 minutes (incl. chilling time)\n |PrepTime = 3 hours\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Couscous, red pepper and garlic salad recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tasted authentic</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.25</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I think the roasted peppers made all the difference.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] are [[Roasted|roasted]].  [[Preserved]] [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]] such as [[Bell peppers#Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa|Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa]] are excellent for this recipe and a great time saver.  The recipe has no particular country of origin, but its flavours are a combination of [[Spanish]] and Maghreb\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 bulbs [[Garlic|garlic]], separated into [[Cloves|cloves]] and peeled\n| 80 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 large [[Roasted sweet peppers|red peppers, roasted]] and peeled or [[Preserved|preserved]], and cut into strips\n| 380 ml [[Vegetable|vegetable]] or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 180 g [[Couscous|couscous]]\n| 90 g melted [[Butter|butter]]\n}}\n'''For the dressing'''\n* 125 ml [[Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]] or [[Tomato juice|tomato juice]]\n* 1 tablespoon [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n* 1&frac12; teaspoons [[Harissa|harissa]]\n* 60 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n* 4 tablespoons [[Herbs|herbs]], finely chopped, eg. [[Chives|chives]], flat-leaved [[Parsley|parsley]]\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4) and [[Roast|roast]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] in the [[Oil|oil]] for 25 minutes.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Bring the [[Stock|stock]] to the [[Boil|boil]] and stir in the cousous.\n| Remove from the heat  and allow to stand until it has absorbed the liquid.\n| Return to heat and stir in the [[Butter|butter]].\n| Allow to cool and add the [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and dressing.\n| Chill briefly.\n}}\n'''To make the dressing'''\n# Place all the ingredients in a jar and shake until blended\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#couscouspepperandgarlicsalad #garlic #oliveoil #butter #preserved #peppers #tomatojuice #roastedredpeppers #boil #chickenstock #stock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

Varoma / Speed Spoon / Reverse blade / MC Off'''\n| Remove and strain the [[oil]] reserving it and the [[garlic]]\n| Make the dressing - see below\n| Add the [[Stock|stock]] '''4 minutes / 100\u00b0 C / Speed 1'''\n| Stir in the [[couscous]] '''2 minutes / 100\u00b0 C / Speed 1 / Reverse blade'''\n| Allow to stand until it has absorbed the liquid\n| Stir in the [[Butter|butter]] '''1 minute / 80\u00b0 C / Speed 3 / Reverse blade'''\n| Allow to cool and add the [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and dressing '''1 minute / Speed 3-4 / Reverse blade'''\n| Chill in the fridge for 2-3 hours\n}}\n'''To make the dressing'''\n# After frying the garlic, chop the herbs '''2-3 seconds / Turbo'''\n# Add all the remaining dressing ingredients, making the reserved oil up to 60g '''10 seconds / Speed 4 / Reverse blade'''\n# Empty the bowl and reserve in the same container as the [[garlic]]\n\n===Chefs notes===\nIf using preserved [[Red peppers|peppers]] do not chop beforehand\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #couscous #butter #oliveoil #peppers #preserved #spanish #parsley #stock #herbs #redpeppers </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Add the remaining ingredients, except for the [[Quesitos|quesitos]] '''20 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 1''' (if using [[Milk|milk]] set at '''90\u00b0''').\n| Allow to cool a little '''40 seconds / Speed 7'''.\n| If necessary, repeat the operation.\n| Add the [[Quesitos|quesitos]] '''5 minutes / 90\u00b0 / Speed 5'''.\n| Correct seasoning if necessary and serve sprinkled with the [[Parsley|parsley]] or [[Chives|chives]].\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nI heated the [[oil]] and [[butter]] '''8 minutes / Temp. [[Lemon peel|lemon peel]] and [[Cinnamon stick|cinnamon stick]] 15 secs / Speed 3\u00c2\u00bd.\n| Add the [[Lemon peel|lemon peel]] and the [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]] 11 minutes / 90\u00b0C / Speed 2.\n| Then 2 minutes / Speed 2  without temperature.\n| Pour into heatproof bowls and either [[Blowtorch|blow torch]] the top, or place under the [[Grill|grill]] until well [[Browned|browned]].\n| Allow to reach room temperature before serving.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Lightly adapted from '''[[Thermomix]] TM31:  Imprescindible para su cocina'''\n===Chef's (2014)\n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 45 minutes \n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe [[Spanish]] are very fond of [[Seafood|seafood]] and this [[Thermomix]] recipe is worth a try.\n\n'''For the Varoma basket'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 500g [[Mussels|mussels]]\n| 300g [[Hake|hake]] fillets\n| 200g [[Monkfish|monkfish]] fillets\n| A few strands of [[Saffron|saffron]]\n}}\n'''For the [[Broth|broth]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 300g [[Prawns|prawns]]\n| 30g [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 50g [[Brandy|brandy]]\n| 200g water\n}}\n'''For the [[Sofrito|sofrito]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 50g [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 200g [[Leeks|leeks]]\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| 100g [[Onions|onions]]\n| 200g [[Prawns|prawns]] per person, and sprinkle the [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]] over the top.\n| Cover and reserve.\n| Put the [[Oil|oil]] in the bowl '''3 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Add the heads and shells of the [[Prawns|prawns]] '''3 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 4'''.\n| When the time is up, add the [[Brandy|brandy]] and leave to [[Rest for|rest for]] a few seconds.\n| Add the water '''5 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 2'''.\n| Strain and reserve the [[Stock|stock]].\n| Wash the bowl, add the [[Sofrito|sofrito]] ingredients and chop '''4 seconds / Speed 4'''.\n| Afterwards, program '''5 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 1'''.\n| Add the reserved [[Stock|stock]] and place the Varoma basket over the bowl '''10 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Cut the [[Fish|fish]] into pieces [and remove the shells from the [[Mussels|mussels]]] and add to the bowl, reserving the bodies of the [[Prawns|prawns]] '''30 seconds / Speed 7'''.\n| Add the [[Cream|cream]], season and program '''2 minutes / 80\u00b0 / Speed 5'''.\n| Add more water if you think it is necessary and [[Blend|blend]] for a '''few seconds / Speed 7''', until you have a homogenous mixture and you desired texture.\n| To decorate, place a [[Basil|basil]] leaf in the centre of each bowl, with two or three [[Prawns|prawns]] on the top.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''Thermomix TM31 - Imprescindible para tu cocina''''' which is the book supplied with [[Spanish]] TMXs.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#prawns #mussels #brandy #thermomix #fish #stock #spanish #sofrito #restfor #blend #singlecream </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Duelos y quebrantos (Scrambled eggs with chorizo)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Duelos y quebrantos Scrambled eggs with chorizo) Egg recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#eggs #chorizo #lard #bread #chilliflakes #paprika #bacon #duelosyquebrantosscrambledeggswithchorizo #unusualrecipes #diced #butter \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=\"Duelos y quebrantos\" literally means \"wounds and suffering\" due to the paprika in the chorizo bleeding into the eggs\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2075\n|PortionCalories = 518\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Duelos y quebrantos (Scrambled eggs with chorizo) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Good Morning!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">My favourite breakfast</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\n\"Duelos y quebrantos\" literally means \"wounds and suffering\" due to the [[Paprika|paprika]] in the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] bleeding into the [[Eggs|eggs]].  This recipe is from La Mancha, and it would make an excellent hot breakfast alternative to [[Bacon|bacon]] and eggs.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 225 g spicy (picante) cooking [[Chorizo|chorizo]], thickly sliced\n| 2 tablespoons [[Lard|lard]] or [[Oil|oil]]\n| 4 tablespoons stale [[Bread|bread]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 8 [[Eggs|eggs]], beaten\n| [[Chilli flakes]], to taste, if desired\n| [[Salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Lard|lard]] or [[Oil|oil]] in a pan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] until it starts to go [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add the [[Bread|bread]] cubes and turn them in the [[Oil|oil]] until they are crisp.\n| Carefully stir in the [[Eggs|eggs]] and add the [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]], if using, and a little [[Salt|salt]].\n| Scramble the [[Eggs|eggs]] until they begin to set and remove from the heat.\n| Serve immediately.\n}}\n===Variations===\nUse [[Butter|butter]] instead of [[Oil|oil]] or [[Lard|lard]].  Try it with [[Serrano ham|serrano ham]] instead of [[Chorizo|chorizo]], in which case add a tablespoon [[Paprika|paprika]] to give colour to the [[Eggs|eggs]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Duelos y quebrantos (scrambled eggs with chorizo)]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes|Duelos y quebrantos (scrambled eggs with chorizo)]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Duelos y quebrantos (scrambled eggs with chorizo)]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Duelos y quebrantos (scrambled eggs with chorizo)]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Duelos y quebrantos (scrambled eggs with chorizo)]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Duelos y quebrantos (scrambled eggs with chorizo)]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Duelos y quebrantos (scrambled eggs with chorizo)]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#eggs #chorizo #lard #bread #chilliflakes #paprika #bacon #duelosyquebrantosscrambledeggswithchorizo #unusualrecipes #diced #butter </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ensalada de cebolletas y apio de Moratalla a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#lemonjuice #ensaladadecebolletasyapiodemoratalla #springonions #salad #celery #bread #marinade #cidervinegar #fat #whitepepper #onions \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A spring onion and celery salad from the medieval town of Moratalla in the province of Murcia\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 224\n|PortionCalories = 56\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 4 or 8 as a [[Tapa|tapa]]\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 1 hour\n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Ensalada de cebolletas y apio de Moratalla recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Good for my celery glut</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Neat salad as well.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nA [[Spring onion|spring onion]] and [[Celery|celery]] [[Salad|salad]] from the medieval town of Moratalla in the province of Murcia.  The recipe has been translated and adapted from ''Cocina de la Huerta Murciana'' (ISBN 9788497362436) by Gloria Sanju\u00e1n.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 [[Fat|fat]] [[Spring onions|spring onions]], finely sliced\n| 60 ml [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| [[Salt]], to taste\n| 1 head of [[Celery|celery]], cut into 1 cm chunks\n| 4 large, firm [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], roughly chopped\n| A pinch of [[Ground|ground]] [[White pepper|white pepper]]\n| A pinch of [[Ground cloves|ground cloves]]\n| 90 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Cider vinegar|cider vinegar]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Marinade]] the [[Spring onions|spring onions]], with the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], for about an hour in the [[Refrigerator|refrigerator]].\n| Place the remaining ingredients in a [[Salad|salad]] bowl and when the [[Spring onions|spring onions]] are cold, pour in the spring [[Onions|onions]] with the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGood with [[Bread|bread]] for mopping uo the liquid.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lemonjuice #ensaladadecebolletasyapiodemoratalla #springonions #salad #celery #bread #marinade #cidervinegar #fat #whitepepper #onions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ensalada de coditos, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#ensaladadecoditos #coditos #tuna #cream #mayonnaise #tomatoes #pasta #egg #parsley #tomato #blackolives \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A simple pasta salad with tuna, tomatoes, egg, Cream and mayonnaise\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1529\n|PortionCalories = 382\n|DatePublished=9th March 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Ensalada de coditos recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Any pasta is fine</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.1</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">While a purist would say this has to be made with coditos, any pasta is fine in this salad.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\n\nA simple [[Pasta salad|pasta salad]] with [[Tuna|tuna]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Egg|egg]], [[Cream|Cream]] and [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].   [[Coditos]] are generally used in Mexico, but the combination of the other ingredients is typically [[Spanish]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 300 g [[coditos]] (pasta) - see Variations below\n| 130g tin of [[Tuna|tuna]] in [[Oil|oil]], [[Mashed|mashed]]\n| [[Home-made mayonnaise|Mayonnaise]], using 500 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n|  2 tablespoons of [[single cream]]\n| 500g firm [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], thinly sliced\n| A handful of [[Black olives|black olives]], pitted\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], hard [[Boiled|boiled]], finely chopped or put through a [[Sieve|sieve]]\n| [[Parsley]], finely chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Boil]] the [[coditos]] for about 15 minutes or per packet instructions.\n| Rinse under cold water and drain thoroughly.\n| When the [[Pasta|pasta]] is cold, mix with the [[Tuna|tuna]], [[Cream|Cream]] and [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] and place in the middle of a serving dish.\n| Arrange the [[Tomato|tomato]] slices around the [[Pasta|pasta]] and place the [[Olives|olives]] on top of it.\n| Sprinkle with the [[Hard boiled egg|hard boiled egg]]. and the [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Variations===\n[[Coditos]] are not available in the UK, as far I can ascertain, although it may be found as elbow macaroni.  They are similar in shape to the [[Italian]] [[:Image:Pasta 2006 3.jpg|pipe pasta]] and this type can be used instead.\n[[Elicoidali]] is another fairly close equivalent that can be purchased directly from Waitrose.\n\nI already had some [[homemade garlic mayonnaise]], but had no idea how much would be made from 500 ml of olive oil, however,  3 good tablespoons of mayonnaise seemed just fine.  I also garnished the salad with a little [[smoked paprika]] to add a bit of extra interest.\nMany people like to use [[Cream|Cream]] in this salad because it reduces acidity in the dish due to the [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Pasta salad recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#ensaladadecoditos #coditos #tuna #cream #mayonnaise #tomatoes #pasta #egg #parsley #tomato #blackolives </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
