                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ensaladilla Rusa, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#mayonnaise #garlic #ensaladillarusa #olives #vegetables #capers #potatoes #boil #carrot #beans #potato \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Although called Little Russian Salad, it is a traditional Spanish tapa\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1386\n|PortionCalories = 346\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Ensaladilla rusa sprinkled with piment\u00f3n da La Vera dulce\n |Servings = 4 or more as a tapa\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Ensaladilla rusa.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Spanish? Russian? Salad?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.11</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Whatever its origins, it is a nice eggy salad \ud83e\udd57</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nAlthough called Little Russian [[Salad]], it is a traditional [[Spanish]] tapa.  There are many variations of this recipe so you can make it how you like so long as you use [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and mix with [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]] ([[Carrots|carrots]] and [[Peas|peas]] being the more usual).\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500 g mixed [[Potatoes|potatoes]] - I would suggest half King Edward and half Charlotte\n| 1 large [[Carrot|carrot]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 125 g French or Kenyan [[Beans|beans]], chopped\n| 125 g [[garden peas]], [[Frozen|frozen]]\n| 1-2 [[Chopped red peppers|chopped red peppers]], depending on size\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, crushed\n| [[Mayonnaise]] to taste - or [[Allioli a la moderna|allioli a la moderna]] (in which case leave out the [[Garlic|garlic]])\n| Small handful of green, pitted [[Olives|olives]], chopped, but not too finely\n| 2-3 [[Gherkins|gherkins]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Capers|capers]]\n| 2 [[Hard-boiled eggs|hard-boiled eggs]], roughly chopped\n| 130g tin of [[Tuna|tuna]] in [[Oil|oil]]\n| 4 slices of chopped [[Jam\u00f3n serrano]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Peel and [[Boil|boil]] the King Edwards and once cooked, [[Mash|mash]] them.\n| Scrape the Charlottes, cut into smallish [[Dice|dice]], and [[Boil|boil]] until tender.\n| [[Boil]] or [[Steam|steam]] the [[Carrot|carrot]], [[Beans|beans]], [[Peas and peppers|peas and peppers]].  Try not to over-cook them,  [[Al dente|al dente]] is ideal.\n| In a bowl, mix both types of [[Potato|potato]] with the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and the [[Garlic|garlic]] if using. \n| Add the [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] or ali-oli whilst the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] are still warm.  Do be liberal with it as you want to taste the mayonnaise.  Mix thoroughly.\n| Add the [[Olives|olives]], gherlins and [[Capers|capers]], mixing gently.\n| Serve in small dishes or on a large plate and garnish as desired with the [[Egg|egg]], tune and [[Jam\u00f3n serrano]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nOther suggested ingredients include [[Celery|celery]], \"reineta\" [[Apple|apple]] (Cox's [[Orange|orange]] pippin is about the nearest variety in the UK) and [[Nuts|nuts]].  Whatever you use, should be chopped quite small.  It is not vital to include the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Capers|capers]] and [[Olives|olives]], if disliked.\n\nYou can also have make it with all [[Mashed|mashed]] or all cubed [[Potatoes|potatoes]], in which case, choose the appropriate [[Potato|potato]] type.\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you have the time and patience to make [[Allioli a la Catalana|allioli a la catalana]], then I feel it is better than plain [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].  [[Allioli a la moderna|Allioli a la moderna]] is a perfectly acceptable substitute.  For the picture above, I used [[Not-for-wimps garlic mayonnaise|Not-for-wimps garlic mayonnaise]] which gives the salad a more yellow appearance due to the [[Rapeseed oil|rapeseed oil]] content.\n[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#mayonnaise #garlic #ensaladillarusa #olives #vegetables #capers #potatoes #boil #carrot #beans #potato </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Escalivada (Pepper and Aubergine Salad)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Escalivada (Pepper and Aubergine Salad) a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#grilled #aubergines #vegetables #oliveoil #parsley #grill #salad #roastingredpeppers #greenpeppers #garlic #onions \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A Catalonian roast pepper and aubergine salad. Escalivada means \"cooked in hot ashes\" which is the authentic way to roast the vegetables\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 272\n|PortionCalories = 68\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes incl cooling\n |PrepTime = 35 minutes\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Escalivada recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Good when cold</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I like these in salads</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nA Catalonian roast [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Aubergine|aubergine]] [[Salad|salad]].  Escalivada means \"cooked in hot ashes\" which is the authentic way to roast the [[Vegetables|vegetables]].  However, not everyone has hot ashes to hand, so the following method uses a [[Grill|grill]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 125 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]] or more\n| 4 [[Green peppers|sweet peppers]]\n| 4 [[Aubergines|aubergines]]\n| [[Salt]]\n| [[Parsley]], finely chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n\n'' see [[Roasting red peppers|Roasting peppers]]''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Grill]] the [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Aubergines|aubergines]] until the skins are blackened.  Peel.\n| Remove the [[Seeds|seeds]] and cut into strips. Place strips in a bowl and sprinkle with [[Salt|salt]] and allow to cool. \n| Dress the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and sprinkle with chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTraditionally served with [[Grilled|grilled]] [[Meat|meat]], it also makes an excellent tapa or first course.\n===Variations===\nYou can use any additional [[Grilled|grilled]] or [[Roasted|roasted]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]] you like, especially [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Onions|onions]].\n\nYou may also wish to add Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] to the [[Oil|oil]].\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Aubergines|aubergines]] taste much better if [[Grilled|grilled]] on a barbecue. As fresh peas are only available for a short period of the year, you will probably use frozen ones for this recipe.  Note that the weight given above is for fresh peas, so you should [[defrost]] frozen peas, drain and pat dry before weighing.  Also if they are fairly dry, they will cook better in the oil. --[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 13:58, 6 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Escalivada]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Escalivada]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Escalivada]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Escalivada]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti|Escalivada]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Escalivada]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#grilled #aubergines #vegetables #oliveoil #parsley #grill #salad #roastingredpeppers #greenpeppers #garlic #onions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

Varoma / Speed 3&frac12;'''.\n| Using the spatula, push down the ingredients from the wall of the bowl and the lid.\n| Incorporate the [[defrosted]] [[Spinach|spinach]] and the [[Salt|salt]] '''5 minutes / Temp. title": "Fabada Asturiana",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Fabada Asturiana, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fabadaasturiana #morcilla #beans #garlic #chickenstock #paprika #saffron #parsley #sausages #pork #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A classic bean and sausage stew from the Asturias in Spain. Don't be alarmed by the amount of garlic\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4361\n|PortionCalories = 726\n|DatePublished=19th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 45 minutes plus overnight soak\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes plus overnight soak\n |CookTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Fabada Asturiana recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Sausage in beans</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Looks like sausages in baked beans.  It's WAY better than that.  The more garlic you use, the better it is!baked </span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA classic [[Bean|bean]] and [[Sausage|sausage]] [[Stew|stew]] from the Asturias in Spain.  Don't be alarmed by the amount of [[Garlic|garlic]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 600 g [[Faba beans|faba beans]]\n| 100 ml extra virgin [[Olive oil|olive oil]], or as little as you need to cook the onions and garlic\n| 1-2 bulbs of [[Garlic|garlic]], separated and peeled, but not chopped\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and quartered\n| 1&frac12; [[Litres|litres]] [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 4 [[Chorizo sausages|chorizo sausages]]\n| 2 [[morcilla]] sausages\n| 200 g [[pancetta]] - this should be in a whole piece and not sliced\n| 1&frac12; teaspoons sweet [[Paprika|paprika]], either [[Smoked|smoked]] or unsmoked\n| A few strands of [[Saffron|saffron]], crushed\n| Finely chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the [[Beans|beans]] overnight.  Drain and rinse.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large saucepan and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Onions|onions]] until they are slightly golden.\n| Add the [[Sausages|sausages]], pancetta,  [[Beans|beans]] and [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] to the saucepan.\n| Cook slowly and when it starts to foam, add the [[Paprika|paprika]] and [[Saffron|saffron]].\n| Continue cooking slowly for about two and a half hours, checking regularly that the saucepan is not running out of liquid.  Add more water as and when necessary, making sure that the [[Beans|beans]] are covered at all times.\n| Remove from the heat and let it stand until cool.\n| Remove the [[Sausages|sausages]] and pancetta, cut them into 1 cm pieces and return them to the pan.\n| Reheat and serve in bowls, sprinkled with the [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nIf you particularly like [[morcilla]], you can substitute an extra one for one of the chorizos.  Pieces of [[Pork|pork]] shoulder can be included as well.\n\n===Chef's tip===\nTry to get \"fabas a la granja\" which are obtainable from specialist [[Spanish]] food shops.  If you really cannot get them, then use white [[Kidney|kidney]] or [[Haricot beans|haricot beans]], although their texture is not the same.\n\nPancetta is widely available, but it must be a whole piece.  Substitute it with a piece of streaky [[Bacon|bacon]] if you can only find sliced pancetta.  The chorizos and morcillas should be slightly larger than a thick British sausage.\n\nFor those watching their weight or health, please be warned that this dish is rather fatty.  The [[morcilla]], especially, can shrink to almost half its uncooked size.  Although not authentic, you could grill the sausages first to reduce the amount of fat and drain off the olive oil once the onions and garlic are golden.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Fabada asturiana]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Fabada asturiana]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Fabada asturiana]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Fabada asturiana]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Fabada asturiana]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Fabada asturiana]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Fabada asturiana]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fabadaasturiana #morcilla #beans #garlic #chickenstock #paprika #saffron #parsley #sausages #pork #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Festival of vegetables with vinaigrette (TM)",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Festival of vegetables with vinaigrette a Thermomix egg recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#vegetables #vinaigrette #thermomix #sauce -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1518\n|PortionCalories = 253\n|DatePublished=22nd October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = The new [[Thermomix]] TM5 (2014)\n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 36 minutes \n|PrepTime = 10 minutes \n|CookTime = 26 minutes \n|Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not short on vegetables!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A meal in itself.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nA wonderful [[Vegetable|vegetable]] dish from [[Spain]]\n\n'''For the [[Vinaigrette|vinaigrette]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 100g [[Green peppers|green peppers]]\n| 100g [[Red peppers|red peppers]]\n| 100g [[Onion|onion]]\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], hard-[[Boiled|boiled]]\n| 100g [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 30g [[Vinegar|vinegar]]\n| 1 small bunch of [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped\n| [[Salt]]\n}}\n'''For the bowl'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 600g water\n}}\n'''For the Varoma'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1kg [[Vegetables|vegetables]], cut into slices ([[Aubergines|aubergines]], [[Potatoes|potatoes]], [[Artichokes|artichokes]], [[Carrots|carrots]] etc)\n}}\n'''For the Varoma tray'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 200g [[garden peas]]\n| 300g [[Courgettes|courgettes]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put all the [[Vinaigrette|vinaigrette]] ingredients into the bowl '''4 seconds / Speed 4'''.\n| Remove and reserve.\n| Without washing the bowl, add the water '''6 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 2'''\n| Place all of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] in the Varoma basket (the softer ones in the tray) '''20 minutes / Temp. title": "Four quarters cake (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Four quarters cake - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#butter #thermomix #lemon #flour #bakingpowder #cake #eggs #thermomixrecipes #bake #miseenplace #spain \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Known in Spain as 'Bizcocho cuatro cuartos' it takes its name from the fact that it contains equal parts of the four main ingredients: flour\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1754\n|PortionCalories = 292\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = The new [[Thermomix]] TM5 (2014)\n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 35 minutes \n|PrepTime = 5 minutes \n|CookTime = 30 minutes \n|Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A quarter per saeason</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Unusual!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nKnown in [[Spain]] as 'Bizcocho cuatro cuartos' it takes its name from the fact that it contains equal parts of the the four main ingredients: [[Flour|flour]], [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Butter|butter]] and [[Eggs|eggs]].  It can be made with with various flavourings such as [[Lemon|lemon]], [[Vanilla|vanilla]], [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]] etc.  It is similar to the English Pound [[Cake]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 130g [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| The peel of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 3 [[free range eggs]]\n| 130g [[Butter|butter]] at room temperature\n| 130g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 3 teaspoons [[Baking powder|baking powder]]\n| A pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4) \n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Tip the [[Sugar|sugar]] into the very dry bowl '''20 seconds / Speed 5-10 progressively'''\n| Add the [[Lemon peel|lemon peel]] and again '''20 seconds / Speed 5-10 progressively'''\n| Next, add the [[Eggs|eggs]] '''2 minutes / 37\u00b0 / Speed 3'''\n| Add the [[Butter|butter]] and beat '''30 seconds / Speed 3'''\n| Incorporate the [[Flour|flour]], [[Baking powder|baking powder]] and [[Salt|salt]] '''10 seconds / Speed 2&frac12;'''\n| Finish by folding the mixture delicately with the spatula\n| Pour into a greased and floured [[Cake|cake]] tin and [[Bake|bake]] in the [[Oven|oven]] for about 25-30 minutes\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''[[Thermomix]] TM31 - Imprescindible para tu cocina''''' which is the book supplied with [[Spanish]] TMXs.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butter #thermomix #lemon #flour #bakingpowder #cake #eggs #thermomixrecipes #bake #miseenplace #spain </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

#friedcodwithroastvegetables #peppers #leeks #butter #flour #roasted \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Possibly a weird combination, but my husband gave me a 'Ready, Steady, Cook' type goody bag and 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 1\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Fried cod with roast vegetables recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">That looks nice and spicy</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">You must like your hot sauce!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nPossibly a weird combination, but my husband gave me a 'Ready, Steady, Cook' type goody bag and this is what I came up up with.\n\nThe recipe below is only for one, so increase quantities accordingly for more [[Servings|servings]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Rapeseed oil]]\n| Large pinch Maldon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 250g Mayan Gold [[Potatoes|potatoes]], scrubbed and chopped into 2.5cm chunks (see Chef's notes below)\n| 130g [[Leeks|leeks]] (cleaned and trimmed weight), cut into 5cm chunks\n| 200g [[Red onions|red onions]], peeled and quartered\n| [[Garlic]] cloves, to taste, unpeeled\n| 1 medium [[Red pepper|red pepper]], cut into quarters\n| More [[Oil|oil]]\n| [[Butter]]\n| 170g [[Cod|cod]] steaks, lightly dusted in seasoned [[Flour|flour]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 1 to 2 teaspoons of hot Piment\u00f3n de Murcia, according to taste \n| 150ml [[Fish|fish]] or [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 100ml fino [[Sherry|sherry]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Cover the bottom of a [[Roasting|roasting]] tin with the [[Oil|oil]] and place in the [[Oven|oven]].  \n* Preheat the oven to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4).\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| When the [[Oven|oven]] has reached the required temperature, add the [[Potatoes|potatoes]], [[Leeks|leeks]], [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| After 30 minutes, turn the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and add the [[Peppers|peppers]].\n| [[Roast]] for a further 15 minutes, then turn the [[Peppers|peppers]].\n| Return to the [[Oven|oven]] for 15 minutes longer.\n| Meanwhile, heat a little [[Oil|oil]] and [[Butter|butter]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Fish|fish]] on a high heat for about a minute each side.\n| Remove the [[Fish|fish]] and reserve.\n| Reduce the heat.\n| Add the [[Flour|flour]] and cook it through, stirring constantly for about 4-5 minutes, then add the piment\u00f3n.\n| Cook for a further 30 seconds maximum ([[Paprika|paprika]] will turn [[Bitter|bitter]] if over cooked).\n| The [[Garlic|garlic]] can be squeezed from its skin over the plate, the skin being discarded. \n| Add the [[Stock|stock]] and the [[Sherry|sherry]].\n| Cook for 3 minutes or so to reduce the [[Sherry|sherry]] and cook out the [[Alcohol|alcohol]].\n| Return the [[Fish|fish]] to the pan and gently heat through for a few minutes.\n| Place the [[Fish|fish]] in the middle of a plate or serving dish.\n| Surround with the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and pour over the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nUse any firm [[white fish]] and vary the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] if desired.  However, you should bear in mind that different [[Vegetables|vegetables]] require different [[Cooking times|cooking times]].\n===Chef's notes===\nI used Mayan Gold [[Potatoes|potatoes]] because they look attractive [[Roasted|roasted]] unpeeled and are generally smallish.  Another good [[Potato|potato]] to use is Highland Burgundy Red which is also small.  However, use any suitable potato breed you desire, as long as they are chopped up small.\n\nAs for [[Garlic|garlic]], I would recommend very [[Fat|fat]] [[Cloves|cloves]].  If yours are not very big, add them at the same time as the [[Peppers|peppers]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Cod with roast vegetables]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Cod with roast vegetables]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Cod with roast vegetables]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Cod with roast vegetables]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes|Cod with roast vegetables]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Cod with roast vegetables]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Cod with roast vegetables]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fish #garlic #vegetables #sherry #potatoes #friedcodwithroastvegetables #peppers #leeks #butter #flour #roasted </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Place the drained [[Vegetables|vegetables]] into a serving dish and drizzle the [[Sofrito|sofrito]] over the top.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''Cocina espa\u00f1ola con [[Thermomix]]'''''\n===Chef's notes===\nFollow the [[RSPCA Think Pig Checklist]] to make sure that your [[Pork|pork]] has come from pigs that have been reared to higher welfare standards.\n* http://bit.ly/rspcathinkpig\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#greenbeans #steaming #onions #potatoes #sofrito #asparagus #carrots #thermomix #vegetables #ham #tomatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This could be a tapas dish, a starter, or if you doubled the amount, a main course\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 654\n|PortionCalories = 163\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = thumb|right|Gambas al ajillo, these beauties with garlic shoots\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 10 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Gambas al ajillo.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">More garlic please</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Food for the garlic fiend!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nGambas al ajillo or Garlic prawns.  This could be a [[tapas]] dish, a [[starter]], or if you doubled the amount, a [[main course]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450g (1 lb) fresh peeled [[prawns]]\n| 4 cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], crushed\n| 1 teaspoon hot [[chili flakes]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[smoked paprika]] powder (normal [[paprika powder]] will do)\n| 4 tablespoons [[dry sherry]]\n| 3 tablespoons freshly chopped [[parsley]]\n| Juice of 1 [[lemon]]\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 [[lime]], quartered\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly [[ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut each slice down the centre of the back of each [[prawn]].  This will enable you to remove the bitter black 'backbone' and will allow the [[prawn]] to  curl open when cooked.\n| Add 2 or 3 good glugs of [[olive oil]] to a large frying pan over a medium heat\n| When the oil is hot, but not smoking, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[chili flakes]] and saut\u00e9 for a few minutes so the oil is nicely flavoured. Don't burn the garlic or you will need to start again!\n| Turn up the heat and add the [[sherry]], [[lemon juice]], [[paprika powder]] and the [[prawns]], stirring until the [[prawns]] change colour and curl. This should take about 3 minutes\n| Arrange in a bowl and garnish with the chopped [[parsley]]\n| Season with [[sea salt]] and freshly [[ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with freshly baked [[bread]] and [[lime]] quarters\n[[Image:Boiled chickpeas.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Plain boiled [[chickpeas]] are a great way of adding healthy fibre to this dish]]\nIn a nod towards the recent report that [https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/health-46827426 we are not eating enough lifesaving fibre], we have started to add plain boiled [[chickpeas]] to lots of our meals.\nThis recipe is ideally suited to such an addition.  Just drop a fistfull of cooked chickpeas into the bowl as you serve the garlic prawns.  The bland-nuttiness works extremely well with the garlic oil.\nIt's worth trying, drained, canned [[chickpeas]] would be just as good as freshly cooked chickpeas. \n\n===Variations===\n\nThis can be made will unpeeled [[prawns]] or even [[defrosted]] frozen [[king prawns]].\n==See also==\n* [[Menorcan garlic prawns]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Starters|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Tapas,_mezze_and_antipasti|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#gambasalajillo #prawns #chickpeas #parsley #groundblackpepper #chiliflakes #garlic #lime #paprikapowder #prawn #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Garlic soup",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Garlic soup; a  recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#garlic #eggs #soup #garlicsoup #paprika #herbs #bread #egg #stock #bayleaf #clams \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is the basis of the numerous variations of a spanish hot garlic soup. It is delicious as a winter warmer and helps to fight off colds and flu\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1687\n|PortionCalories = 421\n|DatePublished=6th November 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Garlic Soup.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Garlic, garlic, garlic!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">If you like garlic, you'll love this.  I think Julia likes garlic!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Stewing the garlic and paprika.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Stewing the garlic and paprika]]\nThis is the basis of the numerous variations of a [[Spanish]] hot [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Soup|soup]].  It is delicious as a winter warmer and helps to fight off colds and flu'.  In southern Spain it is sometimes described as Ajo Blanco, not to be confused with cold [[Ajo Blanco Malague\u00f1o|ajo blanco Malague\u00f1o]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2-3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 3 bulbs [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and either left whole, or sliced\n| 1-2 teaspoons [[Smoked|smoked]] sweet [[Paprika|paprika]]\n| 1&frac12; [[Litres|litres]] [[Ham|ham]] or [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 8 slices of French [[Bread|bread]]\n| A few small sprigs of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| 4 [[free range eggs]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a largish saucepan on a medium heat.\n| When hot, add the whole or chopped [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| Once the [[Garlic|garlic]] is golden [[Brown|brown]], remove from heat.  If you are using whole [[Cloves|cloves]], then blend them with a little of the [[Stock|stock]]. Set aside.\n| Return pan to the heat and add the [[Paprika|paprika]], allowing to [[Stew|stew]] for a minute or two.\n| If you have blended the [[Garlic|garlic]], return the mixture to the pan after the [[Paprika|paprika]] has been cooked.   \n| Add the remaining [[Stock|stock]], [[Bread|bread]] slices and the [[Herbs|herbs]].\n| Cover and  allow to [[Simmer|simmer]] for 15-20 minutes.\n| Remove the [[Herbs|herbs]],\n| Beat the [[Eggs|eggs]] and pour some of the [[Soup|soup]] into a bowl.\n| Spoon the beaten [[Egg|egg]] into the bowl and when it has started to solidify, gently pour the contents of the bowl bag into the saucepan,\n| Reheat slightly, but do not [[Boil|boil]],\n| Serve in bowls, being careful not to break up the [[Egg|egg]] too much.\n}}\n===Variations===\nFor extra warmth, use hot [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]] instead of sweet.  I tend to add about 4-5 teaspoons.\n\nUse as much or as little [[Garlic|garlic]] as you like, but you should be able to taste it.\n\nYou can add about 250 g of [[clams]] or [[prawns]], in which case omit the [[eggs]].  Try grating some [[cheese]] over the top of each bowl.  Alternatively, chop 250 g [[serrano ham]] or [[chorizo]] or a mixture of both.  In the Pa\u00eds Vasco (Basque country) they use [[salt cod]], and in Castilla you will sometimes find the soup with chopped, cooked [[morcilla]].  In Sevilla. the [[eggs]] are poached an floated in each bowl on a largish slice of fried bread.  In Catalu\u00f1a you will find the soup with whole chorizos or other sausages. A Madrid version is to include 250 g of chopped [[tomatoes]] and to place bread slices and whole [[eggs]] into a casserole dish, the soup being carefully poured over it once it is cooked.  You then [[bake]] the whole thing in the  oven at 400C/200F/Gas 6 until the eggs are set.  This should take about 5 - 10 minutes. \n===Chef's notes===\nAlthough this does not taste as strongly of [[Garlic|garlic]] as one would imagine, for a much milder version use whole Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] and omit the blending stage.  You can then remove and discard the cloves once the [[Soup|soup]] has finished cooking.  \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #eggs #soup #garlicsoup #paprika #herbs #bread #egg #stock #bayleaf #clams </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]

It is delicious as a winter warmer and helps to fight off colds and flu'\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1724\n|PortionCalories = 431\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Garlic Soup.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Phew!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice, but quite garlicky \ud83d\ude02</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Stewing the garlic and paprika.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Stewing the garlic and paprika]]\nThis is the basis of the numerous variations of a [[Spanish]] hot [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Soup|soup]].  It is delicious as a winter warmer and helps to fight off colds and flu'.  In southern Spain it is sometimes described as Ajo Blanco, not to be confused with cold [[Ajo Blanco Malague\u00f1o|ajo blanco Malague\u00f1o]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 4 bulbs [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and either left whole, or sliced\n| 2 teaspoons [[Smoked|smoked]] sweet [[Paprika|paprika]]\n| 1&frac12; [[Litres|litres]] [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 8 slices of French [[Bread|bread]]\n| A few small sprigs of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| 4 [[free range eggs]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a largish saucepan on a medium heat.\n| When hot, add the whole or chopped [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| Once the [[Garlic|garlic]] is golden [[Brown|brown]], remove from heat.  If you are using whole [[Cloves|cloves]], then blend them with a little of the [[Stock|stock]]. Set aside.\n| Return pan to the heat and add the [[Paprika|paprika]], allowing to [[Stew|stew]] for a minute or two.\n| If you have blended the [[Garlic|garlic]], return the mixture to the pan after the [[Paprika|paprika]] has been cooked.   \n| Add the remaining [[Stock|stock]], [[Bread|bread]] slices and the [[Herbs|herbs]].\n| Cover and  allow to [[Simmer|simmer]] for 15-20 minutes.\n| Remove the [[Herbs|herbs]],\n| Beat the [[Eggs|eggs]] and pour some of the [[Soup|soup]] into a bowl.\n| Spoon the beaten [[Egg|egg]] into the bowl and when it has started to solidify, gently pour the contents of the bowl bag into the saucepan,\n| Reheat slightly, but do not [[Boil|boil]],\n| Serve in bowls, being careful not to break up the [[Egg|egg]] too much.\n}}\n===Variations===\nFor extra warmth, use hot [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]] instead of sweet.  I tend to add about 4-5 teaspoons.\n\nUse as much or as little [[Garlic|garlic]] as you like, but you should be able to taste it.\n\nTry grating some [[cheese]] over the top of each bowl. In Sevilla. the [[eggs]] are poached an floated in each bowl on a largish slice of fried bread.\n\nA Madrid version is to include 250 g of chopped [[tomatoes]] and to place bread slices and whole [[eggs]] into a casserole dish, the soup being carefully poured over it once it is cooked.  You then [[bake]] the whole thing in the  oven at 400C/200F/Gas 6 until the eggs are set.  This should take about 5 - 10 minutes. \n===Chef's notes===\nAlthough this does not taste as strongly of [[Garlic|garlic]] as one would imagine, for a much milder version use whole Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] and omit the blending stage.  You can then remove and discard the [[Cloves|cloves]] once the [[Soup|soup]] has finished cooking.  \n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 01:32, 5 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #paprika #eggs #soup #stock #egg #bread #herbs #litres #simmer #vegetablestock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Gazpacho de remolacha",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Gazpacho de remolacha, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#beetroot #gazpachoderemolacha #cream #gazpacho #vinegar #boil #blender #tomatoes #soup #foodprocessor #sherryvinegar \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This recipe for beetroot gazpacho has been adapted from Enrique Mapelli Lopez' book Gazpachos, Sopas y Ajos Blancos\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 994\n|PortionCalories = 248\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 3 hours\n |PrepTime = 1 hour, 50 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Gazpacho de remolacha recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Great recipe for your roots</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Tasty soup and uses up some of my roots, always have loads spare.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe for [[Beetroot|beetroot]] [[Gazpacho|gazpacho]] has been adapted from Enrique Mapelli L\u00f3pez' book ''Gazpachos, Sopas y Ajos Blancos'' (ISBN 8495948702).\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg uncooked [[Beetroot|beetroot]], skin intact and stalk trimmed to leave about 1cm\n| 2 kg ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], chopped\n| &frac12; a large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, chopped or crushed\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Sherry vinegar]]\n| [[Salt]]\n| 80 ml [[Single cream]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Boil]] the [[Beetroot|beetroot]] in [[Salted|salted]] water, for at least an hour, depending on size, until it is cooked.\n| Peel and cut into pieces.\n| Place in a [[Blender|blender]] or [[Food processor|food processor]] with all the other ingredients except for the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Cream|cream]].\n| Check for seasoning and add a little cold water if the [[Soup|soup]] is too thick.\n| Chill and serve in cups or bowls, drizzled with a little [[Cream|cream]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nIf you cannot get fresh [[Beetroot|beetroot]], you could try it using the pre cooked vacuum-packed stuff or some of the excellent organic beetroot [[Juice|juice]]s now available.  However, avoid like the plague the jarred beetroot in [[Vinegar|vinegar]] as it will make the [[Gazpacho|gazpacho]] taste vile.  If using juice, you may need to thicken it with some [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]].\n===Chef's notes===\nMake sure that the [[Beetroot|beetroot]] skins are intact or you will lose colour and flavour.\n==See also==\n* [[Beetroot recipes|Our favourite beetroot recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beetroot #gazpachoderemolacha #cream #gazpacho #vinegar #boil #blender #tomatoes #soup #foodprocessor #sherryvinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Another good excuse to use your tomato press\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 656\n|PortionCalories = 164\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Gazpacho con mostaza recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love the celery tops</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">They gave this a nice crunch and added colour</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nLight [[Gazpacho|gazpacho]] with [[Mustard|mustard]].  Another good excuse to use your [[tomato press]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg ripe [[Tomatoes, peeled|tomatoes, peeled]]\n| 4 tender [[Celery leaves|celery leaves]], or 1 stick [[Celery|celery]]\n| [[Garlic]], to taste\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Mustard|mustard]], or to taste (see Chef's notes below)\n| 45 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 15 ml [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| 1 litre water, light [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]], or freshly pressed [[Tomato juice|tomato juice]] (shop [[Juice|juice]] is too heavy)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place all of the ingredients except the water/[[Stock|stock]] in a [[Blender|blender]] and process until smooth.\n| Pour into a serving bowl and stir in the water, [[Stock|stock]] or [[Tomato juice|tomato juice]].\n| Refrigerate until chilled and garnish with chopped [[celery]] leaves.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe, garnished with chopped [[celery]] leaves. \n===Chef's notes===\nThis will keep in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for 1 day, but can be [[Frozen|frozen]] for up to 3 months.\n\nRegarding [[Mustard|mustard]].  The [[Spanish]] have phrases for [[French]], English and [[wholegrain]] [[Mustards|mustards]], so I assume that when they say just 'mustard' that it refers to their everyday variety, which apparently is a classic American style [[mustard]].  They also have a brand called 'Louit' who make various mustards, including a American one which is the bright yellow stuff used for hot dogs.  I have never tried American [[mustard]] and understand it is fairly mild.  Personally I would suggest that UK readers try [[English mustard]] if you want something with a little more heat than the American variety.  Of course, you can use any [[mustard]] you like!  I used ground [[mustard]] powder.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes|Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]]\n[[Category:Starters|Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#gazpacholigeroconmostaza #mustard #celery #tomatojuice #stock #mustards #celeryleaves #wholegrain #juice #whitewinevinegar #tomatopress </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It is recommend that you cook goat on the bone\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4730\n|PortionCalories = 1182\n|DatePublished=1st September 2015\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  18-20 hours  (including marinating time and slow stewing the onions)\n|PrepTime =  14 hours (including marinating time and slow stewing the onions)\n|CookTime =  4-6 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Goat stew slow cooker recipe recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Very rustic</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And very good too.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Goat]] is now increasingly available in particular online from UK farms and from Asian grocery shops.  It is recommend that you cook goat on the bone, even for [[Stews|stews]], for better flavour\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1kg [[Goat|goat]] [[Meat|meat]], with bone, chopped into largish chunks (see note below)\n| 2 tablespoons mild Piment\u00f3n de La Vera (or other [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]])\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 4 [[Spanish]] [[Onions|onions]], sliced\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, peeled and chopped\n| 1.2 [[Litres|litres]] hot [[Beef Stock|beef stock]]\n| 500g or more [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]], halved\n| 250ml [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| 2 [[Red peppers|red peppers]], roughly chopped\n| 2 large or 4 small [[Courgettes|courgettes]], sliced\n| 1 large or 2 small [[Aubergines|aubergines]], chopped\n| 15 [[Black olives]]\n| 80g [[Raisins|raisins]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| [[Mint]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Rub the [[Goat|goat]] [[Meat|meat]] with the Piment\u00f3n de La Vera, place in a bowl, cover and  leave overnight or for 12 hours in the [[Fridge|fridge]]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Whilst the [[Goat|goat]] is [[Marinating|marinating]], heat some [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Casserole|casserole]] or [[Frying pan|frying pan]].\n| Add the [[Onions|onions]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] until [[Caramelised|caramelised]] - a pinch each of [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Salt|salt]] will [[Help|help]] with this.  The longer it takes, the better the flavour.\n| Towards the end of the cooking time, add the [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| Pre-heat your [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]] according to the manufacturer's instructions - about 20 minutes.\n| Tip the [[Onion|onion]] mixture into the [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]].\n| Using the same pot or pan that you used for the [[Onions|onions]], heat a little more [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to high.\n| Add the [[Goats|goats]] chunks, a few at a time for just long enough to [[Sear|sear]] the outside.\n| Transfer to the [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]] and add the hot [[Stock|stock]], [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| Cook on 'high' for 2-3 hours\n| Add the [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Courgettes|courgettes]], [[Aubergines|aubergines]], [[Olives|olives]] and [[Raisins|raisins]] and cook for a further 2-3 hours\n| Season to taste and serve, garnished with chopped [[Mint|mint]]\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can use any combination of [[Vegetables|vegetables]], but just make sure that any hard ones, eg [[Carrots|carrots]] are added at the beginning\n===Chef's notes===\nI advise you to get the [[Meat|meat]] chopped by the [[Supplier|supplier]], rather than do it yourself, which I understand can be very tricky to get right\n\nYou can cook this on 'low' if you like.  I have not tested it, but would suggest a total of 8 hours cooking at least.\n\nIf you are not going to be around to add the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] half way through cooking, you can put them all in at the beginning.\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#goat #oliveoil #onions #slowcooker #vegetables #courgettes #mint #garlic #aubergines #redwine #raisins </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

The majority of them are consumed whole, but I had to blitz them due to my husband's forthcoming dental treatment.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#peppercorns #sofrito #sauce #spanish #mushrooms #butter #lemonjuice #stockcube #blanched #cream #garlic </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

taste, peeled \n| 50g [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 150g [[Button mushrooms|button mushrooms]]\n| 25g fino [[Sherry|sherry]] or manzanilla\n| 25g [[milk]]\n| 75g [[Single using [[Cherry|cherry]] ones\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the [[Shallots|shallots]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] to the bowl and chop '''6 seconds / Speed 5'''.\n| Scrape down the inside of Varoma / Speed 1 / MC Off'''.\n| Add the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] '''10 seconds / Speed 5 / MC On'''.\n| Scrape down the inside of the bowl using the spatula.\n| To prepare the Varoma basket for the [[Fish|fish]] by greasing with a little [[Oil|oil]].\n| Place the [[Fish|fish]] in the Varoma.\n| Add the [[Sherry|sherry]], [[Milk|milk]], [[Cream|cream]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to the bowl.\n| Place the Varoma, with the [[Fish|fish]], onto the lid '''14 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Place the [[Fish|fish]] onto a serving dish and pour the [[Sauce|sauce]] over the top.\n| Garnish with the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]] or [[Salad|salad]].\n===Recipe source===\n* Translated and lightly adapted from a recipe on the '''[http://www.recetario.es/recetas/filetes-de-merluza-con-salsa-de-setas/276130 Thermomix Espa\u00f1a website]''' (You will need to register and sign in to see the original recipe).\n===Variations===\nYou can you any firm fleshed [[white fish]] fillets.\n===Chef's notes===\nSome parts of the [[hake]] were quite thick and they came straight out of a cold fridge.  This resulted in adding 5 minutes to the steaming time, in which case add a little extra [[milk]] to the [[sauce]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fish #hake #sherry #tomatoes #shallots #sauce #garlic #singlecream #unusualrecipes #thermomix #cherry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

You will find that morcilla is easy to skin and retain their shape, whereas chorizo is more difficult to skin and will break up in the process.\n| Pulse the [[Morcilla|morcilla]] in a [[Food processor|food processor]], add the [[Chorizo|chorizo]] and 1 beaten [[Egg|egg]] and blend roughly.  Do not allow the mixture to become smooth.\n| Put the other beaten [[Egg|egg]] in a dish and sprinkle some [[Flour|flour]] on a chopping board.\n| Divide the [[Sausage|sausage]] mixture into four and shape into burgers.\n| [[Dip]] each one into the [[Egg|egg]] and then coat lightly with the [[Flour|flour]].\n| Leave to rest in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for at least an hour.\n| Peel and lightly smash some [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves and gently cook in [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]].  Discard the [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| When the burgers have rested, [[Fry|fry]] them in the pan on a low-medium heat until they are cooked through.\n| Meanwhile, slice the [[Molletes antequeranos (Antequera muffins)|molletes]] in half lengthways.\n| Spread the [[Allioli a la moderna|allioli]] on the lid half.\n| When the burgers are ready, place them on the bottom half of the [[Molletes antequeranos (Antequera muffins)|molletes]] and cover them with the [[Lettuce|lettuce]] and the [[Tomato|tomato]], and finally the lid.\n}}\n===Variations===\nTry barbecuing the burgers, in which case add a little Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] to the [[Sausage|sausage]] mixture.  You could also use the mixture to make [[Scotch]] [[Eggs|eggs]] or [[Meat|meat]] balls,\n===Chef's notes===\nI have not specified any seasoning as the [[Sausages|sausages]] are highly seasoned in themselves.  Use either ordinary [[Chorizo|chorizo]] or for more spicyness, choose [[Chorizo|chorizo]] 'picante'.\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 08:15, 22 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Hamburger]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes|Hamburger]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Hamburger]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Hamburger]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Hamburger]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Hamburger]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chorizo #garlic #hamburguesasdechorizoymorcilla #morcilla #flour #egg #sausage #oliveoil #eggs #lettuce #tomato </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Home-made Churros",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Home-made Churros, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#churrera #frozen #homemadechurros #greaseproofpaper #deepfatfryer #flour #icingsugar #boiling #potato #orceserranohams #cuporjug \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A churro is a fried-dough pastry-based snack, sometimes made from potato dough, originated in Spain, and is popular in Latin America, France, Portugal\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 120\n|PortionCalories = 24\n|DatePublished=8th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 5\n|Difficulty = 2\n|ImageComment = Churros and chocolate\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Churros recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">One is enough!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">These are more unhealthy than deep-fried Mars Bars.  Yuk!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA churro is a fried-dough pastry-based snack, sometimes made from [[potato]] dough, originated in Spain, and is popular in Latin America, France, Portugal, the USA, and Spanish-speaking Caribbean islands. It is sometimes referred to as a Spanish doughnut or Mexican doughnut. The snack gets its name from its shape, which resembles the horns of the Churro breed of sheep reared in the Spanish grasslands of Huarocho. There are two types of churros in Spain. One is long and fat and the other, specially popular in Madrid, is thin and knotted (porra). They both are normally eaten for breakfast dipped in hot chocolate (drink).\nThe churro is typically fried to a crunchy consistency and sometimes sprinkled with [[sugar]]. Its surface is ridged due to being piped from a [[churrera]], a syringe with a star-shaped nozzle.\n\nLike [[pretzels]], churros are often sold by street vendors who in many cases will fry them freshly on the street stand and sell them hot. In Spain and Mexico, they are available in cafes for breakfast, although they may be found throughout the day and night as a snack.\n\nVery popular for breakfast, churros are a simple type of doughnut.  They can be made with a [[churrera]], obtainable from [http://www.delicioso.co.uk/ Delicioso] and [[Orce Serrano Hams]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| Measuring in a [[cup or jug]], you need equal volumes of [[Plain flour|plain flour]] and water, so for this recipe measure 500 ml of both\n| Large pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| [[Olive]] or [[Sunflower oil|sunflower oil]]\n| Caster or [[Icing sugar|icing sugar]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the water and [[Salt|salt]] in a saucepan and bring to the [[Boil|boil]].\n| [[Sieve]] the [[Flour|flour]] into a bowl.\n| Add the [[Boiling|boiling]] water to the [[Flour|flour]] and mix thoroughly with a fork.  The mixture should be like a thick paste.\n| Do not worry too much about any lumps as the force on the churrera will disperse them.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large [[Deep frying|deep frying]] or saut\u00e9 pan.\n| Force the mixture into the [[churrera]] as tightly as you can, to reduce the amount of air in the mixture.\n| When the [[Oil|oil]] is almost [[Smoking|smoking]], pipe the dough into the pan, either in a spiral or in longish strips.  \n| Cook until they are a rich golden [[Brown|brown]].  Because they float, you will need to turn them over to ensure even cooking.  This is best done with either [[skewers]] or chopsticks.\n| If they are spiral shaped, cut them into long pieces with scissors.\n| Sprinkle them with [[Sugar|sugar]] if desired\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Churros ready to be frozen.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Churros ready to be frozen\nImage:Cooked, frozen, home-made churros.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Home-made, frozen and cooked churros\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with a cup of thick dark drinking [[Chocolate|chocolate]] into which the churros are dunked.  Unless you have quite a sweet tooth, I would avoid sprinkling them with the [[Sugar|sugar]].\n\nThis recipe makes 10 large churros.  Allow 2-3 per person.\n\n===Variations===\nThe above is a very basic recipe and in my experience the more usual one.  However, sometimes [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and/or [[Eggs|eggs]] are included.\n\nAlthough they would lose their authenticity, you can play around with them and add any flavourings you like.  I have made them with [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Paprika|paprika]] before.\n\n===Chef's tip===\nYou can use a [[deep fat fryer]] to cook the churros, but it is quite difficult to pipe in the mixture if your fryer is a long thin one.  They would probably work better in a round fryer.\n\nAs an alternative to a [[churrera]], it is possible to make them using a [[piping bag]] with a large star-shaped nozzle, although not quite so easy.\n\nChurros can be [[Frozen|frozen]].  Pipe them onto [[greaseproof paper]], or preferably [[Bake-O-Glide]] - it can be quite tricky extracting them from [[greaseproof paper]]. [[Open freeze]] them until they are hard (several hours), then put them into bags.  They should be cooked directly from [[frozen]].  If they are [[frozen]], they are easier to cook in a [[deep fat fryer]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Churros]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Churros]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Cuban recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#churrera #frozen #homemadechurros #greaseproofpaper #deepfatfryer #flour #icingsugar #boiling #potato #orceserranohams #cuporjug </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

You can either make just sausages, just burgers or a mixture of the two\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3408\n|PortionCalories = 106\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Homemade [[Chorizo sausages]]\n |Servings = Servings: 32 - Makes 16 large sausages\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 40 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Homemade chorizo sausages.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Stunning work Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..and for anyone reading this now, Julia (aka Rosemary), is a vegetarian!</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nOur first attempt at making [[Chorizo sausages|chorizo sausages]].  You can either make just [[Sausages|sausages]], just [[Burgers|burgers]] or a mixture of the two\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1kg [[Shoulder of pork|shoulder of pork]] (make sure it is not too lean)\n| 50ml [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]], [[Asturian cider]] or [[Sherry|sherry]]\n| 10g [[Salt|salt]]\n| 25g [[Piment\u00f3n de La Vera]] (dulce or picante or a mixture of the two)\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, crushed\n| 10g [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], [[Ground|ground]]\n| 5g [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]], [[Ground|ground]]\n| 5g [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]] (not [[Ground|ground]])\n| 2 metres [[Sheep|sheep]] casings (if making all [[Sausages|sausages]]) or 1 metre if making half-in half\n}}\n'''In addition, if you are making [[Burgers|burgers]] you will need'''\n* 2-3 beaten [[Eggs|eggs]]\n* [[Flour]]\n* [[Olive oil]]\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Sterlise all [[Equipment|equipment]], including worksurfaces.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Using a medium disk, [[Mince|mince]] the [[Pork|pork]] - twice if making [[Sausages|sausages]] or once if making [[Burgers|burgers]].\n| Place in a bowl with the remaining ingredients and mix well with your hands.\n| Ideally wear some [[Sterilise|sterilised]] latex gloves to do this.\n}}\n'''For the [[Sausages|sausages]]'''\n# Stuff your casings - the [[Sausages|sausages]] should be long-linked and slim, so do not overstuff.\n# Store the [[Sausages|sausages]] in the [[Freezer|freezer]] for at least 24 hours to allow the flavours to blend.\n# As and when you want to eat them, [[de-frost]] in the [[Fridge|fridge]] and [[Bake|bake]] at 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4) for 20 minutes.\n'''For the [[Burgers|burgers]]'''\n# Shape into [[Burgers|burgers]] and [[Dip|dip]] each one into some beaten [[Egg|egg]] and then coat lightly with the [[Flour|flour]].\n# Leave to rest in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for at least an hour.\n# Heat some [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]]. \n# When the [[Burgers|burgers]] have rested, [[Fry|fry]] them in the pan on a low-medium heat until they are cooked through.\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the sausages hot for breakfast or cold a part of a tapa or snack.  The burgers would go well with [[Molletes antequeranos (Antequera muffins)|Molletes antequeranos]] and salad as a [[light lunch]].\n===Variations===\nVary the amount of [[Garlic|garlic]] and Piment\u00f3 de La Vera.  Use [[Fennel seeds|fennel seeds]] instead of [[Cumin|cumin]] and experiment with different [[Herbs|herbs]].\n===Chef's notes===\nEnsure that they are properly cooked.  The [[Sausages|sausages]] can also be consumed cold.  We used locally produced [[Traditionally Farmed Gloucestershire Old Spot Pork|Gloucester Old Spot pork]].\n\nAlthough these are ready 1 1 hour, they need at least 24 hours to be at their best.\n\nFollow the [[RSPCA Think Pig Checklist]] to make sure that your [[Pork|pork]] has come from pigs that have been reared to higher welfare standards.\n* http://bit.ly/rspcathinkpig\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine|Chorizo]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sausages #burgers #ground #garlic #flour #driedoregano #fridge #pork #homemadechorizosausagesandburgers #oliveoil #chorizosausages </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

The sugar should have dissolved by then.\n| Allow to cool, pour into a glass or jug and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] until cold.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nIdeal for when lolling around in the garden on a hot day.\n===Chef's notes===\nIf using [[Almonds|almonds]], do not thow them away when you have [[Strained|strained]] them from the water.  You can re-use them to make [[Ajo Blanco Malague\u00f1o]] - my favourite summertime [[Soup|soup]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Horchata de almendras o chufas]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Horchata de almendras o chufas]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Horchata de almendras o chufas]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Horchata de almendras o chufas]]\n[[Category:Beverages|Horchata de almendras o chufas]]\n[[Category:Drink and beverage recipes|Horchata de almendras o chufas]]\n[[Category:Non-alcoholic beverages|Horchata de almendras o chufas]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#horchatadealmendrasochufas #almonds #tigernuts #powderedcinnamon #fridge #groundalmonds #horchata #strained #nut #cinnamon #spanish </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

powder\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Tip the [[Sugar|sugar]] into the bowl and pulverise at '''Speed 5-10''' progressively.\n| Add the [[Lemon|lemon]] rind and pulverise again at the same some [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]] over it.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''[[Thermomix]] TM31 - Imprescindible para tu cocina''''' which is the book supplied with [[Spanish]] TMXs.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Sugar|sugar]] quantity is to suit [[Spanish]] tastes and may well be too sweet for people in the English speaking world, so I would suggest starting off with about 60-70g.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Drink and beverage recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg The vinegar and the [[herbs]] work really well with liver, especially if its not over cooked.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 50 g (2 oz) [[butter]]\n| 1 [[onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 450 g (1 lb) calves liver, washed, rinsed, trimmed and sliced as thinly as you can\n| 3 tablespoons chopped [[parsley]]\n| 3 tablespoons chopped [[sage]]\n| [[Sea salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 30 ml (2 tablespoons) [[sherry vinegar]] - [[red wine vinegar]] will do , but it's worth getting [[sherry vinegar]] anyway, you won't regret it!\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Fry]] the [[onions]] in the [[butter]] until soft, about 4 minutes\n| Add the liver, [[sage]] and half of the [[parsley]] and season to taste with [[salt]] and [[pepper]]\n| [[Fry]] until [[browned]] and tender, but don't overcook it or it will be as tough as old boots. (It's quite ok to eat liver rare)\n| Reserve the [[liver and onions]] and keep warm\n| Deglaze the pan with the [[sherry vinegar]] by bringing it to the [[boil]] whilst stirring.  Reduce the heat and [[simmer]] for a minute\n| Pour the hot [[sherry]] over the liver and sprinkle with the remaining [[parsley]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe hot\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Offal recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sherryvinegar #parsley #fry #liverwithherbsandsherryvinegar #sage #butter #boil #panfried #redwinevinegar #simmer #onions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Lubina a la sidra (Sea-bass in cider)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Lubina a la sidra (Sea-bass in cider) a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cider #fish #onions #tinfoil #saffron #butter #baking #garlic #bass #flour #bake \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Sea-bass in cider\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1971\n|PortionCalories = 492\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Lubina a la sidra\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 40 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Lubina a la sidra.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love the colour of this.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Thanks Julia</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Ingredients for 2.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ingredients for 2]]\nSea-[[Bass|bass]] in [[Cider|cider]].  Since the 17th century [[cider]] has been commercially produced in north-west Spain (Galicia, Asturias and the Basque country) and they even have special bars called sider\u00edas.  This recipe is a simple version of a dish from the Asturias.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 [[Sea bass|sea bass]] fillets\n| [[Flour]] \n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Butter|butter]] \n| 2 [[Onions|onions]] finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, finely diced (I used 2 bulbs)\n| A few [[saffron]] strands, crushed\n| 500 ml dry [[Cider|cider]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Clean and dry the sea-[[Bass|bass]] fillets and lightly coat them with seasoned [[Flour|flour]].\n| Melt the [[Butter|butter]] in a pan and seal the [[Fish|fish]] until they are golden.\n| Remove from the pan, place in greased [[tin foil]] and put in a [[Baking|baking]] dish. \n| Add the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] to the pan and [[Fry|fry]] until soft, then add the [[saffron]] and half of the [[Cider|cider]].\n| Allow to reduce and then pour it over the [[Fish|fish]], together with the remaining [[Cider|cider]].\n| Wrap the [[tin foil]] loosely and [[Bake|bake]] in the oven for 15 minutes at 180 C/325 F/Gas 4\n}}\n===Variations===\nIt is also traditional to place some peeled and sliced reineta [[Apple|apple]] (use Cox's [[Orange|orange]] pippin in the UK) on top of the [[Fish|fish]] when [[Baking|baking]].  You can also add shellfish and [[Paprika|paprika]].\n===Chef's notes===\nUse Asturian [[cider]] if possible.  You can order it on line from '''[[Delicioso.co.uk|Delicioso]]'''.\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 05:54, 17 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Sea-bass]]\n[[Category:Cooking with beer|Sea-bass]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Sea-bass]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Sea-bass]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Sea-bass]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes|Sea-bass]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Sea-bass]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cider #fish #onions #tinfoil #saffron #butter #baking #garlic #bass #flour #bake </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

http://decoraciondemabel.blogspot.com.es/2013/02/tarta-magica.html, translated/transcibed by Google/[[User:Cakey|Cakey]]\n===Variations===\nSwitch 50g of [[Flour|flour]] for [[Cocoa|cocoa]] for a [[Chocolate|chocolate]] version\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#flour #butter #magiccustardcake #icingsugar #eggwhites #vinegar #vanilla #unusualrecipes #bake #microwave #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I've increased the [[Garlic|garlic]] from a measly 2 [[Cloves|cloves]] in the original recipe to about 6 as I can't imagine any self-respecting Spaniard ever putting just 2 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] in a dish to serve 6 people!\n\nBe bold, vary the [[Vegetable|vegetables]] to match what you have lying around at the time.\n\nThis was a very nice, and very easy vegetable dish, it will be made again.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 400g can peeled [[Plum tomatoes|plum tomatoes]], chopped\n| 1 tablespoon fresh [[Oregano|oregano]] or [[Marjoram|marjoram]], chopped\n| 3 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] plus a little more to dress the dish with\n| 6 [[Fat|fat]] Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] (or to taste), half peeled and crushed, the remaining half peeled and roughly chopped\n| 1 [[Aubergine|aubergine]], sliced\n| 1 [[Sweet bell pepper|sweet bell pepper]] of any colour\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 650g [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled and sliced: Desiree, King Edward, Lady Balfour, Maris Piper, Melody etc.\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to  200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add 1.5  tablespoons of the [[Oil|oil]] to a pan and sizzle the [[Garlic|garlic]] for a minute and then add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Oregano|oregano]], season and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 10 minutes to reduce a little.\n| Toss the [[Aubergine|aubergine]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Onion|onion]] in the remaining [[Oil|oil]], season and arrange in a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] and [[Oven|oven]] [[Roast|roast]] for 10 minutes.\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and arrange the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]] in layers.\n| Pour over the [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]], add a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and a glug of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]. \n| Cover with [[Tin foil|tin foil]] and [[Bake|bake]] for 1 hour, removing the [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]] half way through.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with crusty [[Bread|bread]].\n===Chef's notes===\nNever one to resist playing around, I added 1/2 a glass of [[red wine]] and a big pinch of [[chilli flakes]] to the [[tomato sauce]].\n\nI think that in future I would finish under a grill to really crisp up the potatoes.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #majorcanvegetablebake #oregano #potatoes #oliveoil #onion #aubergine #tomatosauce #vegetarian #bread #sidedish </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Marinated olives",
                "revisions": [
