title": "Panache de verduras (Mixed vegetables)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Panache de verduras (Mixed vegetables) a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#vegetables #garlic #tomatoes #potatoes #oliveoil #panfried #leeks #butter #swisschard #broadbeans #gardenpeas \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Simply means 'mixed vegetables' which would be a Spanish first course, although you may wish to make it as an accompaniment\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3842\n|PortionCalories = 960\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Folk dances of the Basque Country\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Folk dances of the Basque Country.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Veggies and garlic</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Not a thing wrong with that!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nSimply means 'mixed [[Vegetables|vegetables]]' which would be a [[Spanish]] first course, although you may wish to make it as an accompaniment.  In Spain, [[Vegetables|vegetables]] are usually served as a separate course.\n  \nThis recipe is from the Pais Vasco (Basque) region.\n\n\nChoose at least 5 or 6 varieties of [[Vegetables|vegetables]] from the following, depending on what is in season:\n{{RecipeIngredients \n| 1 [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]]\n| 1 white [[Cabbage|cabbage]]\n| 4 [[Carrots|carrots]]\n| 8 [[Artichoke hearts|artichoke hearts]]\n| 8 spears white [[Asparagus|asparagus]]\n| 8 medium [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| 400 g [[garden peas]], shelled\n| 200 g [[Broad beans|broad beans]], shelled\n| 200 g [[French beans]]\n| 4 [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 2 large [[Leeks|leeks]]\n| 2 [[Swiss chard]]\n}} \nAlso:\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Olive oil]] to taste\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Wash your chosen [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and peel if necessary.\n| Slice, chop or shred the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] as appropriate.\n| [[Boil]] or [[Steam|steam]] them in separate saucepans, except for the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] which should be [[Grilled|grilled]].  As some [[Vegetables|vegetables]] take longer than others, you will need to work out which ones need to go on first.\n| Towards the end of the cooking time, put some [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a pan and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] until it is golden.\n| Drain the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and arrange them separately on a large serving plate, or on four individual plates.\n| Drizzle the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Oil|oil]] over the top of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and serve.\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can [[Baked potatoes|bake the potatoes]] if you wish and arrange the other [[Vegetables|vegetables]] around them.\n\nThe amount of [[Oil|oil]] you use will depend on which [[Vegetables|vegetables]] you have chosen, eg. [[Potatoes|potatoes]] will absorb more oil than [[Peas|peas]].\n\nYou can use [[Butter|butter]] instead of [[Oil|oil]].\n===Chef's notes===\nIf for some reason, your [[Vegetables|vegetables]] become cold, you can heat them gently in the [[Microwave|microwave]], but do so before you add the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Garlic|garlic]].\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 07:11, 4 February 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Vegetables mixed]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Vegetables mixed]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Vegetables mixed]]\n[[Category:Starters|Vegetables mixed]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Vegetables mixed]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Vegetables mixed]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#vegetables #garlic #tomatoes #potatoes #oliveoil #panfried #leeks #butter #swisschard #broadbeans #gardenpeas </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

As some [[Vegetables|vegetables]] take longer than others, you will need to work out which ones need to go on first.\n| Towards the end of the cooking time, put some [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a pan and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] until it is golden.\n| Drain the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and arrange them separately on a large serving plate, or on four individual plates.\n| Drizzle the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Oil|oil]] over the top of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and serve.\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can [[Baked potatoes|bake the potatoes]] if you wish and arrange the other [[Vegetables|vegetables]] around them.\n\nThe amount of [[Oil|oil]] you use will depend on which [[Vegetables|vegetables]] you have chosen, eg. title": "Panecillos de pan blanco con poolish de yogur",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Panecillos de pan blanco con poolish de yogur Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#yoghurtpoolish #panecillosdepanblancoconpoolishdeyogur #yeast #bakingtray #flour #baked #dough #steam #bread #toastedsesameseeds #poppyseeds \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=These white rolls are made with yogurt poolish and the recipe has been translated and slightly adapted from Xavier Barriga's excellent book\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1445\n|PortionCalories = 160\n|DatePublished=27th September 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 9 - Makes about 18 small rolls\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Panecillos de pan blanco con poolish de yogur.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Quick and easy</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Easy and quick too. \ud83d\ude0e</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThese white rolls are made with [[Yoghurt poolish|yogurt poolish]] and the recipe has been translated and slightly adapted from Xavier Barriga's excellent book '''Pan''' (ISBN 8425343267).  They are also easy to make as once the ingredients are mixed properly, no kneading is required.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500g strong [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 10g [[Salt|salt]]\n| 225ml tepid water\n| 5g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 200g [[Yoghurt poolish|yogurt poolish]] straight from the [[Fridge|fridge]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Dissolve the [[Yeast|yeast]] in the tepid water.\n| Mix the [[Flour|flour]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Yoghurt poolish|yogurt poolish]].\n| When the [[Yeast|yeast]] has dissolved, mix with the remaining ingredients.\n| Cover, and allow to rest for 15 minutes.\n| Divide the mixture into 50g pieces and shape into round, smooth balls.\n| Place them on greased [[baking tray]]s, leaving a reasonable gap between each one as they will spread.\n| Cover with a damp cloth and leave to prove for about 90 minutes in the warmest part of the kitchen.\n| Preheat the [[Oven|oven]], preferably to 250\u00b0 C (475\u00b0 F - gas 9), or the highest temperature if yours is lower.\n| At the same time, place a [[baking tray]] half full of water at the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]] - this is to generate [[Steam|steam]].\n| Before [[Baking|baking]] the  rolls, spray them lightly with a little water as this helps them to colour on the outside.\n| [[Bake]] for about 12 minutes until the rolls are golden [[Brown|brown]].\n| Cool on a wire rack\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nBecause the rolls are small, cut in half, they would make an excellent base for canap\u00e9s.  However, they were so delicious, they did not last long enough for that!\n===Variations===\nXavier Barriga suggests that you use only 30g of [[Dough|dough]] per roll which would make them very small indeed.  Also, he cuts the tops with a pair of scissors just before you put them in the [[Oven|oven]].  This looks very pretty but whenever I do that, my dough deflates!\n\nYou can sprinkle them with [[Poppy seeds|poppy seeds]] or [[Toasted sesame seeds|toasted sesame seeds]] if you wish.\n===Chef's notes===\nThese are best consumed on the day that they are [[Baked|baked]], so you may wish to reduce the quantity, or [[Freeze|freeze]] any that are not to be eaten immediately.  They will be fine to eat the next day, but they will have lost some of their delicious-ness.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#yoghurtpoolish #panecillosdepanblancoconpoolishdeyogur #yeast #bakingtray #flour #baked #dough #steam #bread #toastedsesameseeds #poppyseeds </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Pan al vapor (Steamed bread) (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pan al vapor (Steamed bread) - A Thermomix recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #steam #bread #knead #soup #steaming #litres #steamer #driedyeast #toasted #yeast \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This bread is made entirely in the Thermomix as it is steam baked in the Varoma\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 668\n|PortionCalories = 66\n|DatePublished=27th September 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - 1 small loaf\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours\n |CookTime = 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pan al vapor (Steamed bread) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tasted fine</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">But it looks anaemic - odd!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis [[Bread|bread]] is made entirely in the [[Thermomix]] as it is [[Steam|steam]] [[Baked|baked]] in the Varoma.  It is meant for [[Toasting|toasting]].\n\nThe recipe comes from '''[http://www.clubcocinafacil.com/masas-bases/PAN-AL-VAPOR_2489.html ClubCocinaFacil]''' - the recipe below has one more rising than the original.  You can also see a video on their website.  It is in Spanish but you will get the general idea.\n\nSee '''Variations''' below for how to convert this recipe for [[Steaming|steaming]] conventionally.\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 150g water\n| 15g fresh or 7g [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 250g [[Strong white bread flour|strong white bread flour]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| [[Oil]] for greasing\n| 1.5 [[Litres|litres]] water (for the Varoma)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the 150g water and the [[Yeast|yeast]] in the bowl 2 minutes / 37\u00ba / Speed 1.\n| Add the [[Flour|flour]] and [[Salt|salt]] and 2 minutes 30 seconds / [[Knead]].\n| Leave to rise in the bowl until almost doubled in size, then 10 seconds / [[Knead]].\n| Shape the [[Dough|dough]] into a ball and put it in an oiled [[Soup|soup]] bowl which will fit into the Varoma.\n| Cover with a [[Tea towel|tea towel]] and leave for about an hour until doubled.\n| Pour the 1.5 [[Litres|litres]] of water into the bowl and place the Varoma, containing the [[Soup|soup]] bowl and [[Dough|dough]] on top of the TM bowl.\n| Cover, and [[Steam|steam]] for 45 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1.\n| Allow to cool and cut into 1cm slices.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nMakes a wonderful [[Bread|bread]] for [[Pa amb tom\u00e0quet]] ([[Pa amb oli]]).\n===Variations===\nThis can also be made in a conventional manner.  Make and [[Knead|knead]] the [[Dough|dough]] according to your usual manner and [[Steam|steam]] in a in a saucepan or [[Steamer|steamer]] on the [[Hob|hob]], until it has the appearance of a [[Suet|suet]] pudding.\n===Chef's notes===\nThis [[Bread|bread]] will seem to be uncooked, but that is how it is.  It is very good [[Toasted|toasted]] and will last for days.\n\nI [[Steamed|steamed]] mine in an enamel pudding basin, which is fine, but the top of the [[Dough|dough]] does touch the Varoma lid towards the end of the [[Steaming|steaming]] time, if using a TM31.  The Varoma basket in the TM5 is deeper, so should not touch the lid if using this version.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #steam #bread #knead #soup #steaming #litres #steamer #driedyeast #toasted #yeast </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pan con Tomate, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pancontomate #toasted #olive #oliveoil #garlic #tomato #ciabatta #sausages #belazu #anchovyfillets #olives \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Either George Bennell or Adam Wells writes: \"We first discovered this traditional Catalonian dish when we visited our olive groves\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 682\n|PortionCalories = 170\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Pan con Tomate (y anchoas)\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 6 minutes\n |PrepTime = 3 minutes\n |CookTime = 3 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pan con Tomate recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not bad</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just needs a bit of cheese with it.</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nEither George Bennell or  Adam Wells writes: \"We first discovered this traditional Catalonian dish when we visited our [[Olive|olive]] groves. We often go early in the morning just as the sun is coming up to see the [[Olives|olives]] on the trees. \n\nMaybe it sounds odd, but with local [[Sausages|sausages]], some strong black [[Coffee|coffee]] and our beautiful olive groves laid out before us this is a pretty sublime dish - and not one that should be restricted to breakfast. A good [[Olive oil|olive oil]] is key - try using our Early Harvest [[Olive]] [[Oil]] from Catalonia.\n\nLeopold Pomes, author of the Theory and Practice of [[Bread]] with [[Tomato]] (1984) claims this was invented by a painter who wanted to combine the colours of the sunset on an edible base. It\u0092s more likely this tasty delicacy was created by an inventive Catalan wanting to use up the previous day\u0092s bread.\"\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 8 slices of [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Ciabatta|ciabatta]] or [[Country bread|country bread]] \n| 2 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and cut in half \n| 2 large ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] cut in quarters \n| [[Belazu]] Early Harvest [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] \n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n|Take a piece of the [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Ciabatta|ciabatta]] and rub the cut edge of the [[Garlic|garlic]] over its surface. Then rub the cut side of a [[Tomato|tomato]] quarter over the toast until it softens with the tomato pulp. Drizzle [[Olive oil|olive oil]] on top and sprinkle with [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]. \n|Repeat with the remaining toast and serve.\n}}\n===Variations===\nGarnish with [[anchovy fillets]].\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/early-harvest.html Belazu Early Harvest Extra Virgin Olive Oil Unfiltered]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Toasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pancontomate #toasted #olive #oliveoil #garlic #tomato #ciabatta #sausages #belazu #anchovyfillets #olives </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Pan de agua (Water bread)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pan de agua (Water bread), Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#flour #dough #bread #bake #yeast #baked #sparklingmineralwater #tomato #boiling #coolingrack #clingfilm \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This recipe is based on one by Xavier Barriga from his book Pan\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1329\n|PortionCalories = 132\n|DatePublished=12th April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - 1 large loaf\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 16 hours10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 hours 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Pan de agua (Water bread) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Strange, but true!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">It worked!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nThis recipe is based on one by Xavier Barriga from his book '''Pan''' (ISBN 8425343267).  My version below uses a different method and also requires you to start this the evening before the day you want to [[Bake|bake]] it.\n\nIt is an extremely wet [[Dough|dough]] (120% hydration) and I would advise you to mix it using a food [[Mixer|mixer]] with a beater or whisk (the mixture is too wet to benefit from using a dough hook).  If you have a Kenwood Chef / Major, the  flexi-beater is ideal.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 10g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 600g [[Sparkling mineral water|sparkling mineral water]]\n| 500g very strong bread [[Flour|flour]], eg Waitrose Very Strong Canadian [[Bread]] [[Flour]]\n| 12g [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Dissolve the [[Yeast|yeast]] in the water.\n| Pour into a bowl and add 250g of the [[Flour|flour]].\n| Mix well, cover in [[Clingfilm|clingfilm]] and leave overnight at room temperature.\n| The following morning add the remaining [[Flour|flour]] and the [[Salt|salt]].\n| Mix for about 5 minutes on the second slowest speed.\n| Cover and leave to rest for 2 hours.\n| Grease a 900g loaf tin with [[Oil|oil]] - [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]] is best as it has a high smokepoint.\n| Pour the [[Dough|dough]] into it (it should come up to about three-quarters of the tin.\n| Allow to prove for 1 hour, covered.\n| Meanwhile, place a tray or pan of [[Boiling|boiling]] water in the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]].\n| Switch on the [[Oven|oven]] to its highest temperature.\n| When the [[Dough|dough]] has finished [[Proving|proving]], sprinkle with [[Flour|flour]], put it in the [[Oven|oven]] and reduce the temperature to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan oven 170\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n| [[Bake]] for 60 minutes.\n| Once [[Baked|baked]], turn out onto a [[Cooling rack|cooling rack]] and allow to cool.\n| If the [[bread]] is a little soft on the bottom, turn it over, place on a baking tray and return to the oven for 10 minutes or so until crisp.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGood toasted and rubbed with [[Garlic|garlic]], [[tomato]] and [[olive oil]].\n===Chef's notes===\nAs this is a wet dough, I would recommend that you line your bread tin with [[Bake-O-Glide]], or something similar.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#flour #dough #bread #bake #yeast #baked #sparklingmineralwater #tomato #boiling #coolingrack #clingfilm </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It is an extremely wet dough (120% hydration\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1329\n|PortionCalories = 132\n|DatePublished=12th April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - 1 large loaf\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 4 hours 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 3 hours 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Pan de agua (Water bread) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wet bread</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Didn't work for me</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThis is an adaptation for [[Thermomix]] from the recipe by Xavier Barriga from his book '''Pan''' (ISBN 8425343267).\n\nIt is an extremely wet [[Dough|dough]] (120% hydration) but the beauty of this is that it does not require [[Kneading|kneading]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 600g [[Mineral water|mineral water]]\n| 10g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]] or 5g [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 500g very strong bread [[Flour|flour]], eg Waitrose Very Strong Canadian [[Bread]] [[Flour]]\n| 12g [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place all of the ingredients, excluding the [[Salt|salt]] into the TM and process for '''10-15 seconds / Speed 6''' until you have a smooth [[Batter|batter]]. \n| Leave to rest in the jug for about 2 hours, by which time it should have risen substantially.\n| Add the [[Salt|salt]] and mix for a '''few seconds / Speed 6''' to ensure that the salt is evenly incorporated.\n| Grease a 900g loaf tin with [[Oil|oil]] - [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]] is best as it has a high smokepoint.\n| Pour the [[Dough|dough]] into it (it should fill about three-quarters of the tin).\n| Allow to prove for 1 hour, covered.\n| Meanwhile, place a tray or pan of [[Boiling|boiling]] water in the bottom of the [[Oven|oven]].\n| Switch on the [[Oven|oven]] to its highest temperature.\n| When the [[Dough|dough]] has finished [[Proving|proving]], sprinkle with [[Flour|flour]], put it in the [[Oven|oven]] and reduce the temperature to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan oven 170\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n| [[Bake]] for 60 minutes.\n| Once [[Baked|baked]], turn out onto a [[Cooling rack|cooling rack]] and allow to cool.\n| If the [[Bread|bread]] is a little soft on the bottom, turn it over, place on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] and return to the [[Oven|oven]] for 10 minutes or so until crisp.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGood [[Toasted|toasted]] and rubbed with [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Tomato|tomato]] and [[Olive oil|olive oil]]. \n===Variations===\nA conventional method of making this bread can be found [[Pan de agua (Water bread)|here]].\n===Chef's notes===\nAs this is a wet [[Dough|dough]] and your tin isn't non-stick, I would recommend that you line your [[Bread|bread]] tin with [[Bake-O-Glide]], or something similar. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #flour #bread #batter #mineralwater #groundnutoil #toasted #driedyeast #thermomix #garlic #yeast </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Pan de pueblo (Village bread)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pan de pueblo (Village bread) a breadmaker recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#bread #dough #flour #semolina #bake #poolish #yeast #kneadingbread #wheat #baking #refrigerated \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This village bread recipe has been adapted from Gastronomia y Cia\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1777\n|PortionCalories = 177\n|DatePublished=4th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Pan de pueblo\n |Servings = Servings: 10 - Makes one loaf\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 4 hours 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 4 hours\n |CookTime = 40 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pan de pueblo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A LOT of effort this</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.9</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..but probably worth all the hard work.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis village bread recipe has been adapted from '''[http://www.gastronomiaycia.com/2009/07/20/pan-de-pueblo/ Gastronom\u00ed\u00e1 y Cia]'''.\n\nPara ver esta receta en castellano, pulsa '''[http://www.gastronomiaycia.com/2009/07/20/pan-de-pueblo/ aqu\u00ed]'''\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 batch of [[Poolish|poolish]]\n| 5g easy [[Bake|bake]] [[Yeast|yeast]] or 10 g fresh yeast\n| 600g white [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]] (half strength - see Variations below)\n| 50g [[Wheat|wheat]] [[Semolina|semolina]], plus a little more for sprinkling \n| 8g [[Salt|salt]]\n| 210ml or more of water\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* If the [[Poolish|poolish]] has been [[Refrigerated|refrigerated]], remove from the [[Fridge|fridge]] an hour or two beforehand and allow to stand at room temperature.  It should be bubbling when it is ready to use.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| If making by [[Hand|hand]], dissolve the fresh [[Yeast|yeast]] in, place in a floured bowl,add the other ingredients and [[Kneading bread|knead]] thoroughly for 10 minutes.\n| Cover with a cloth and allow to rise until it has doubled in size - about 1-2 hours. \n| If using a [[Bread machine|bread machine]], place the ingredients in the pan in the order given in your manufacturer's manual.\n| Set to a basic [[Dough|dough]] programme - in the Panasonic SD-253/254/255, this will take about 2 hours and 20 minutes.  For the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]], this is menu option 16.\n| [[Knock back]] the [[Dough|dough]] on a floured board and shape into two loaves.\n| Place on a [[baking tray]], which has been sprinkled with some [[Semolina|semolina]] and sprinkle some more semolina on top of the loaves.\n| Because the [[Dough|dough]] is soft, allow enough space for each loaf to spread.\n| Cover and leave to rise for a further two hours.\n| Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 250\u00b0 C (475\u00b0 F - gas 9) and place a try of water in the bottom of the oven.  Alternatively, you can spray the [[Bread|bread]] with water 2 or 3 times during its [[Baking|baking]] period.\n| When the [[Oven|oven]] is hot, reduce the temperature slightly and make some cuts in the [[Bread|bread]] (a [[Grignette|grignette]] is best for this). \n| [[Bake]] for 40 minutes or until the [[Bread|bread]] sounds hollow when tapped.\n}}\n===Variations===\nIt is suggested that you use 'half strength' [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]] and if using what we know in the UK as 'strong' bread flour. you may need to add more water.  From something I read, Tesco's own make bread flour is probably the least strong, however, I am going to experiment with a mixture of very strong Canadian flour and [[Italian]] type 00 [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] flour.  I will update this once I have finished playing around.\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you are making the [[Dough|dough]] in a [[Bread maker|bread maker]], I would suggest using half quantities, as the ones given in the above recipe are probably too much for the average machine.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pan de pueblo]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Pan de pueblo]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes|Pan de pueblo]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Pan de pueblo]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Pan de pueblo]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#bread #dough #flour #semolina #bake #poolish #yeast #kneadingbread #wheat #baking #refrigerated </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

Varoma / Speed 2'''.\n| Incorporate the guindillas and [[Blend|blend]] '''40 seconds / Speed 1-9 progressively''', for a smooth [[Sauce|sauce]].  Use a lower speed for less time if you prefer it to have some texture.\n| In the meantime, [[Fry|fry]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] in [[Olive oil|olive oil]], empty them into a dish and pour over the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* Translated and adapted from a recipe by Teregomez on the '''[http://www.recetario.es/node/27056 Thermomix Spain]''' website.  \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potatoes #onion #oliveoil #garlic #sauce #tomatoes #tapa #blend #wine #whitewine #fry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Patatas con ajo y perejil (Potatoes with garlic and parsley)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Patatas con ajo y perejil Potatoes with garlic and parsley Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#potatoes #parsley #garlic #whitewinevinegar #paprika #lemonjuice #winevinegar #bitter #oliveoil #smokedpaprika #panfried \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=There are many recipes for potatoes with garlic and parsley and this simple version comes from Jaen\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 697\n|PortionCalories = 174\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 25 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Patatas con ajo y perejil recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Only problem is it uses lots of oil.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nThere are many recipes for [[Potatoes|potatoes]] with [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Parsley|parsley]] and this simple version comes from Ja\u00e9n.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 900 g [[Potatoes|potatoes]], cut in &frac12; cm slices\n| [[Olive oil]] - sufficient to just cover the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] in a deep pan\n| 4 [[Cloves|cloves]] or more of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and roughly chopped \n| [[Parsley]], chopped\n| 1 tablespoon sweet [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]]\n| 1-2 tablespoons [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] gently and add the [[Potatoes|potatoes]].\n| Allow the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] to [[Stew|stew]] in the [[Oil|oil]] until cooked.  Do not allow them to go [[Brown|brown]].\n| Drain off most of the oil, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Parsley|parsley]] and cook for a further minute or two.\n| At the last moment, stir in the [[Paprika|paprika]] and add a splash or two of the [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]].\n| Do not allow the [[Paprika|paprika]] to cook for too long or it will become [[Bitter|bitter]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe as a [[Tapa|tapa]] with [[Allioli a la moderna|allioli]] or with some [[Salad|salad]] and nice [[Bread|bread]].\n===Variations===\nYou can substitute [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] for the [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]].\n===Chef's notes===\nAdd as much or as little [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Paprika|paprika]] and [[Wine vinegar|wine vinegar]] as you like.  If you are using a lot of garlic, leave the [[Cloves|cloves]] whole. You will achieve a stronger garlic taste by frying the garlic separately and adding it to the potatoes at the last minute.\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 08:45, 11 January 2009 (UTC) \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Potatoes with garlic and parsley]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Potatoes with garlic and parsley]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes|Potatoes with garlic and parsley]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Potatoes with garlic and parsley]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Pot]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Potatoes with garlic and parsley]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potatoes #parsley #garlic #whitewinevinegar #paprika #lemonjuice #winevinegar #bitter #oliveoil #smokedpaprika #panfried </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

teaspoon [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| [[Pepper]]\n| Chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the shells and heads of the [[Prawns|prawns]] in the bowl together with the water '''5 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 4'''.\n| Strain, and reserve the [[Broth|broth]] (the bodies of the [[Prawns|prawns]] will be incorporated at the end of the recipe).\n| Thoroughly wash the bowl and lid.\n| In the bowl, put the [[Sofrito|sofrito]] ingredients and chop '''5 seconds / Speed 4'''.\n| Next, program '''10 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 3&frac12;'''.\n| With the spatula, push down the ingredients on the inside wall of the bow.\n| Fit the [[Butterfly]] on the blades add the rest of the ingredients (excluding the [[Prawns|prawns]]) and the [[Stock|stock]] '''23 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Reverse Blade / Speed Spoon'''.\n| After this time add the bodies of the [[Prawns|prawns]] and leave to rest.\n| Adjust the seasoning and serve, garnished with the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''[[Thermomix]] TM31 - Imprescindible para tu cocina''''' which is the book supplied with [[Spanish]] TMXs\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#prawns #thermomix #parsley #broth #sofrito #spanish #butterfly #stock #dried #bayleaf #garlic </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

pepper|green pepper]], chopped\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 8 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and chopped\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| [[Salt]]\n| 1 kg waxy [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]], washed and [[Oil|oil]], together with the [[Garlic|garlic]], bay leaf and a little [[Salt|salt]].\n| Add the [[Potatoes|potatoes]], chops and [[Chorizo|chorizo]].\n| Cover with water and add the [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nNot all recipes include [[Pork|pork]] so if you wish to leave them out, add some extra [[Chorizo|chorizo]].\n\nFor a spicier version, use hot [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]] and as usual, you can adjust the amount of [[Garlic|garlic]].\n===Chef's notes===\nTry not to let the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] over-cook or they will disintegrate.                 "revisions": [
                    {

style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">(when I made this \ud83d\ude09)</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nLiterally '[[Turkey]] with wet [[Rice|rice]]', ie the rice is cooked together with the other ingredients as opposed to being cooked separately.\n\nThis dish is found throughout Spain, where [[Turkey|turkey]] is eaten all year round and not just at Christmas.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 50 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 800g skinned, chopped [[Turkey|turkey]] breast\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]]\n| 6 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| 2 medium [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled and cubed\n| 1 [[Green pepper|green pepper]]\n| 1 [[Red pepper|red pepper]]\n| Pinch of [[Saffron|saffron]], pounded\n| 340g long-[[Grain|grain]] [[Rice|rice]]\n| [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 1 litre [[Turkey|turkey]] or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| Chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a deep pan.  \n| Season the [[Turkey|turkey]] and stir into the [[Oil|oil]] until [[Browned|browned]].\n| Remove the [[Turkey|turkey]] and place in a bowl.\n| Add the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] to the same pan until golden and mix with the [[Turkey|turkey]] in the bowl.\n| [[Fry]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] until golden and add the [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Saffron|saffron]].\n| When the [[Peppers|peppers]] have started to [[Brown|brown]], add the [[Rice|rice]], stir and cook for a further minute.\n| Finally, add the [[Stock|stock]] and [[Lemon|lemon]], cover, and allow to cook for about 15 minutes, by which time the [[Rice|rice]] should be cooked.\n| Garnish with chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nLike most [[Spanish]] dishes, this would be served on its own, but it would go nicely with a [[Side dish|side dish]] of [[Vegetables|vegetables]] or [[Salad|salad]].\n===Variations===\nUse [[Chicken|chicken]] in place of [[Turkey|turkey]] if you wish.\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 05:52, 15 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Turkey]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Turkey]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Turkey]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Turkey]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes|Turkey]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Turkey]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#turkey #rice #saffron #potatoes #lemon #peppers #parsley #garlic #browned #chickenstock #onions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Pa amb oli",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pa amb oli, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#paamboli #tomato #bread #garlic #ham #hand #grated #plumtomato #tomatoes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Literally 'bread and oil' but also includes tomato and garlic. It is from Majorca and is eaten at any time of the day\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 104\n|PortionCalories = 104\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Majorcan 'tomato bread and oil' \n |Servings = Serves 1\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 5 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Pa amb oli recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Bravo!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great idea, thanks Julia.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nLiterally '[[Bread|bread]] and [[Oil|oil]]' but also includes [[Tomato|tomato]] and [[Garlic|garlic]].  It is from Majorca and is eaten at any time of the day.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 slice of rustic [[Bread|bread]], about 2 cm thick\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] [[Garlic|garlic]], cut in half length ways\n| 1 ripe [[Tomato|tomato]], cut in half\n| [[Extra virgin olive oil]], to taste\n| [[Salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Toast the [[Bread|bread]] until it is golden.\n| Rub the [[Garlic|garlic]] over both sides the toast, so that it is actually [[Grated|grated]].\n| Rub the [[Tomato|tomato]] over one side so that the skin comes away in your [[Hand|hand]].  This will only work with a ripe tomato.\n| Serve on a plate, drizzle with the [[Oil|oil]] and add [[Salt|salt]] to taste.\n}}\n===Variations===\nA similar version comes from Catalu\u00f1a where it is known as '''pa amb tom\u00e0quet'''.  However the Catalans put the [[Oil|oil]] on before the [[Tomato|tomato]].  Sometimes, sliced [[ham]] is added on the top.\n\n===Chef's notes===\nThere are some cheat's methods of making this, especially if you cannot get ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].  Firstly, you can grate the [[Tomato|tomato]] finely and spread it over the toast. or try using a tinned [[Plum tomato|plum tomato]].  Alternatively, use some tinned chopped tomatoes and drain them off thoroughly beforehand.  \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pa amb oli]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Pa amb oli]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Pa amb oli]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Pa amb oli]]\n[[Category:Starters|Pa amb oli]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Pa amb oli]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Pa amb oli]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#paamboli #tomato #bread #garlic #ham #hand #grated #plumtomato #tomatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

title": "Pea and garlic stuffed peppers",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pea and garlic stuffed peppers a French recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#garlic #peaandgarlicstuffedpeppers #peas #oliveoil #bread #peppers #chiliflakes #sherry #onions #seeds #pea \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A tasty tapas, light snack, vegetable accompaniment or a meal in itself\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 783\n|PortionCalories = 195\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 40 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pea and garlic stuffed peppers recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Coincidence!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I'm making a similar dish tonight - stuffed with mozzarella and chorizo</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nA tasty [[Tapas|tapas]], light snack, [[Vegetable|vegetable]] accompaniment or a meal in itself.  This recipe is quick and easy to prepare and very easy to adapt so it suits your personal taste.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 large [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], any colour\n| 4 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]], plus extra for drizzling\n| 150g (5oz) [[Frozen peas|frozen peas]], [[defrosted]]\n| 1 large [[Red onion|red onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 4 [[Cloves|cloves]] of [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 2 tablespoons [[Sherry|sherry]] or [[White wine|white wine]]\n| 150g (5oz) wholemeal [[Bread|bread]], crumbled. \n| Pinch of [[Chili flakes|chili flakes]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Slice off the tops, leaving the stem intact; reserve.\n| With deft knife-work, remove the white membranes and knock out the [[Seeds|seeds]].\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and flavour it with a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n| Slightly crush the [[Peas|peas]] so they can really absorb the [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Oil|oil]].\n| Saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 4 minutes, add the [[Peas|peas]] and saut\u00e9 for a further 4 minutes.\n| Soak the crumbled [[Bread|bread]] in the [[Sherry|sherry]] and then stir into cooked [[Peas|peas]] and [[Onions|onions]].\n| Remove from the heat.\n| Season the insides of the [[Peppers|peppers]] with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and a sprinkling of [[Chili flakes|chili flakes]].\n| Distribute the [[Pea|pea]] mixture between the [[Peppers|peppers]]. Drizzle with a little more [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Replace the tops and [[Bake|bake]] for 25 minutes.\n}}\n===Variations===\nA little finely [[Grated|grated]] [[Parmesan]] mixed in with the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] adds an extra lift to this dish.\n==See also==\n* [[Cheese, peas and garlic stuffed peppers]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #peaandgarlicstuffedpeppers #peas #oliveoil #bread #peppers #chiliflakes #sherry #onions #seeds #pea </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nStuffed [https://www.cookipedia.co.uk/cgi-bin/cc.pl?cftk=2#jump chicken breasts] appear frequently on [[Spanish]] menus and in their cookery books, and whilst  this recipe (created by my husband) is not necessarily typical, it does have Spanish elements.\n\nSurprisingly though, it does not contain [[Garlic|garlic]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 plump [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts, skinned and boned\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 100 g [[Serrano ham]]\n| Half a [[Green pepper|green pepper]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 4 medium [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 4 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], whites only, [[Diced|diced]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Paprika|piment\u00f3n de la Vera]] dulce (sweet [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]])\n| Cocktail sticks\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak some cocktail sticks in hot water.\n| Slit the [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts in half horizontally, but not completely - see [[how to butterfly a chicken breast]].\n| Open the breast and bash with a [[meat mallet]].\n| On one side of each of the open breasts, place a slice of [[Serrano ham]] and rub a dab of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] over the [[Ham|ham]].\n| Place the [[Diced|diced]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]] on top of the [[Ham|ham]].\n| Mix the [[Paprika|paprika]] with the remaining [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and dab over the [[Vegetables|vegetables]].\n| Place a further slice of [[Serrano ham]] on top of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]].\n| Fold the other half of the [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]] and using the cocktail sticks pin the open sides together.\n| Heat some [[Oil|oil]] in a shallow pan and gently [[Fry|fry]] the breasts on both sides until golden.\n| Transfer them to a [[Roasting|roasting]] tin and [[Bake|bake]] in a preheated oven 190 C/375 F/Gas 5 for 25 minutes.  \n| Allow to go completely cold, remove the cocktail  sticks and  cut the breasts into 1&frac12; cm slices.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGoes nicely with small [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]], and [[Salad|salad]].\n\n===Chef's notes===\nThis is quite a healthy dish, but to make it even healthier, you can put them straight into the oven without [[Searing|searing]]. Also you can use a rack in the [[Roasting|roasting]] tin.  However, you will need to lengthen the cooking time.\n\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 15:47, 23 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chicken breasts]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chicken breasts]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chicken breasts]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Chicken breasts]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Chicken breasts]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#diced #vegetables #serranoham #oliveoil #roasting #chicken #ham #newpotatoes #springonions #meatmallet #greenpepper </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe small [[Peppers|peppers]] used to make this dish come from Lodosa in [[Spain]] and are available in jars or tins from [[Spanish food suppliers]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 8 piquillo [[Peppers|peppers]]\n| Chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n'''For the [[Stock|stock]]'''\n* 500g [[Milk|milk]]\n* 100g [[White wine|white wine]]\n* 25g [[Brandy|brandy]]\n* 1 large [[Lobster|lobster]]\n'''For the [[Cream|cream]]'''\n* 50g [[Butter|butter]]\n* 50g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n* 25g [[Flour|flour]]\n* 1 [[Egg yolk|egg yolk]]\n* [[Salt]]\n'''For the [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n* 1 [[Carrot|carrot]], peeled and chopped\n* 1 [[Tomato|tomato]], peeled and [[Seeds|seeds]] removed\n* 100g [[White wine|white wine]]\n* 100g water\n* 1 [[Fish stock|fish stock]] cube\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| To make the [[Stock|stock]], put half of the [[Milk|milk]] and the [[Wine|wine]] into the bowl with the [[Brandy|brandy]] and the head of the [[Lobster|lobster]] '''7 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 4'''.\n| Strain through a fine [[Sieve|sieve]], add the rest of the [[Milk|milk]] and reserve.\n| Wash the bowl and the lid.\n| For the [[Cream|cream]], put the [[Butter|butter]], [[Oil|oil]] and [[Flour|flour]] into the bowl '''3 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 3'''.\n| Add the reserved [[Stock|stock]] '''6 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 3'''.\n| Add the peeled and chopped [[Lobster|lobster]], the [[Egg yolk|egg yolk]] and seasoning '''4 minutes / 80\u00b0 / Speed 1&frac12;'''.\n| If the [[Cream|cream]] is very thick, add a little [[Milk|milk]].\n| Stuff the [[Peppers|peppers]] with the [[Cream|cream]], close them with a [[cocktail stick]] and place them in a [[Baking|baking]] dish.\n| Without washing the bowl add the [[Carrot|carrot]] and [[Tomato|tomato]] '''5 seconds / Speed 5'''.\n| [Scrape down the sides of the bowl] then '''5 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 3&frac12;'''.\n| Add the remaining [[Sauce|sauce]] ingredients '''5 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 4'''.\n| If the [[Sauce|sauce]] isn't smooth enough chop for '''a few seconds / Speeds 5-7-9'''.\n| Finally pour the [[Sauce|sauce]] over the [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Bake|bake]] for 15 minutes at 170\u00b0C.\n| Serve sprinkled with the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''Cocina espa\u00f1ola con Thermomix'''''\n==See also==\n{{Template:Lobster recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sauce #peppers #cream #stock #lobster #tomato #eggyolk #butter #whitewine #carrot #parsley </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

'Enrejado' (lit. gated) refers to the layer of latticed pastry on the top\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 7235\n|PortionCalories = 1808\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 1\n |Image = [[Image:Pimientos enrejados recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Looks fantastic</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">But I can never get the lattice-bit right. Help!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Peppers]] and [[Fish|fish]] encased in [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]].  'Enrejado' (lit. gated) refers to the layer of latticed [[Pastry|pastry]] on the top.  This recipe has been reproduced here in English together with the images (right) by kind permission of '''[http://larecetadelafelicidad.blogspot.com/2009/05/pimientos-enrejados.html SandeeA]'''.\n[[Image:The interior.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The interior]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 200 g [[hake]]\n| 200 g peeled [[Frozen|frozen]] [[Prawns|prawns]] \n| 8 [[Bell peppers#Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa|piquillo peppers]]\n| 2 sheets of [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]]\n}}\n'''For the main [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n* 2 tablespoons [[Flour|flour]]\n* 3 tablespoons warm [[Milk|milk]] or [[Fish stock|fish stock]] or a mixture of both\n* 4 tablespoons [[Sunflower oil|sunflower oil]] or [[Butter|butter]]\n* [[Salt|salt]]\n'''For the [[Pepper|pepper]] [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n* 2 piquillo [[Peppers|peppers]]\n* 2 tablespoons main [[Sauce|sauce]]\n* 200 ml [[Single cream|single cream]]\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Simmer]] the hake and [[Prawns|prawns]] in enough water to cover.\n| Once they are cooked, reserve the [[Stock|stock]] if you are going to use it for the [[Sauce|sauce]]\n| Cut the [[Prawns|prawns]] into small cubes and crumble the hake, removing any skin and [[bones]].\n| To make the [[Sauce|sauce]], heat the [[Sunflower oil|sunflower oil]] in a pan and add the [[Flour|flour]].\n| Cook lightly until the [[Flour|flour]] is golden [[Brown|brown]] and add the [[Milk|milk]] or [[Fish stock|fish stock]], stirring until you have the desired consistency. \n| Remove and reserve two tablespoons of [[Sauce|sauce]] to use for the [[Pepper|pepper]] sauce and season the remainder.\n| Mix in the reserved [[Prawns|prawns]] and hake.\n| To prepare the [[Pepper|pepper]] [[Sauce|sauce]], blend two [[Peppers|peppers]] with the [[Cream|cream]] and the two tablespoons reserved sauce.\n| Fill the [[Peppers|peppers]] with the [[Fish|fish]] mixture.\n| Wrap each [[Pepper|pepper]] in [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]] and using a [[lattice cutter]], cut pieces of [[Pastry|pastry]] to put on top of each wrapped pepper. This can also be done using a sharp knife \u2013 if you have the patience!\n| [[Bake]] at 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6) for 15 minutes, serve with the [[Hot pepper sauce|hot pepper sauce]] ... and enjoy!\n}}\n===Variations===\n[[Peeled prawns]] are used for convenience, but you can use un peeled [[Prawns|prawns]] if you wish and these will give the [[Stock|stock]] more flavour.\n\nYou can flavour the [[Sauce|sauce]] with Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] or finely chopped [[Onion|onion]] before adding the [[Flour|flour]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Pies tarts and flans|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Starters|Pimientos enrejados]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pimientosenrejados #sauce #prawns #flour #peppers #puffpastry #sunfloweroil #fishstock #stock #fish #pastry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 900 g boneless, skinless, [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts, [[Diced|diced]] and seasoned with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, [[Diced|diced]] (I used 3 bulbs)\n| 4 [[Red peppers|red peppers]], [[Roasted|roasted]], skins and [[Seeds|seeds]] removed, and coarsely chopped\n| 1 teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Oregano|oregano]] or 3 teaspoons if fresh\n| 2 400 g tins chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large saucepan to a medium temperature.\n| Add the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces and cook for about 15 minutes to [[Brown|brown]] them.\n| Add the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Stew|stew]] until the onions are beginning to soften - about 5 minutes or so.\n| Increase the heat and add the remaining ingredients.\n| Cook for about 5 minutes, then reduce the heat to medium-low.\n| Continue cooking, uncovered for around 50 minutes, until the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces are tender.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Rice|rice]] or [[Noodles|noodles]], or on its own as a [[Tapa|tapa]].\n===Variations===\nThere are many regional variations of pisto using different [[Vegetables|vegetables]] such as [[Aubergines|aubergines]], [[Courgettes|courgettes]].  Green [[Bacon|bacon]], [[Pork tenderloin|pork tenderloin]] or [[Fish|fish]] is often used instead of [[Chicken|chicken]].  \n===Chef's notes===\nIf you can get nice, ripe, fresh [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], then they are best, but peel them first.\n\nMake sure that the temperature of the [[Oil|oil]] to which you add the [[Chicken|chicken]] is not too hot or it will stick.\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{Template:Pisto recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pisto toledano]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pisto toledano]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Pisto toledano]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Pisto toledano]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Pisto toledano]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Pisto toledano]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Pisto toledano]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pistotoledano #chicken #diced #tomatoes #onions #stew #garlic #oregano #roasted #stewedbraisedorpotroasted #tapa </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

There is plenty of garlic sauce that is wonderful for dipping bread\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 736\n|PortionCalories = 184\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Pollo al ajillo con ma\u00edz y tirabeques\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pollo al ajillo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Great garlic chicken</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Fresh and flavoursome. There is plenty of [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Sauce|sauce]] that is wonderful for dipping [[Bread|bread]].\n \nOriginally, the [[Garlic|garlic]] was the poor man's ingredient and the [[Chicken|chicken]] the rich man's.  Nowadays, with intensive farming, the [[chicken]] is cheaper than the [[Garlic|garlic]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 10 [[Fat|fat]] [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves (unpeeled)\n| &#188; cup [[Spanish]] extra virgin [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 12 [[Chicken|chicken]] wings, halved at the joint\n| 3 springs of freshly picked [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| &#188; cup [[Spanish Manzanilla sherry]] \n| &#188; cup [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Using a cleaver, a small [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or even your bare hands, smash the [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves and split them open. Leave them unpeeled \n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large pan or even a [[Wok|wok]] and saut\u00e9 the [[Garlic|garlic]] over a medium-high heat until it's lightly [[Browned|browned]]. This should take about 3 minutes\n| Add the [[Chicken|chicken]] wings, turn the heat up a little and saut\u00e9 until [[Brown|brown]] all over and properly cooked, another 5 to 10 minutes\n| Add the [[Thyme|thyme]], [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]] and the [[Sherry|sherry]] and [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] and bring back to the boil and immediately reduce the heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] for a minute or so\n| Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Pollo al ajillo simple.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Pollo al ajillo\nImage:Smash the garlic.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Smash the garlic\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nWe had this as a main course with added [[mange tout]], split [[baby sweetcorn]], [[Onion and garlic loaf]] and a [[Sour cream and spring onion dip]]\n===Variations===\nSaut\u00e9 a selection of [[Vegetables|vegetables]] or wild [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] with the [[Chicken|chicken]].  See also [[Pollo en salsa de ajo]].\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#polloalajillo #garlic #chicken #chickenstock #bayleaf #thyme #browned #oliveoil #bread #tapa #fat </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This particular recipe has been translated and lightly adapted from a recipe by '''[http://mispinitosdecocina.blogspot.com/2011/07/muslos-de-pollo-al-ajillo-thermomix.html Sandoa]''' and is licenced under '''[http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-nc-sa/3.0/ CC BY-NC-SA]'''.\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 8 [[Chicken|chicken]] drumsticks (or 4 thighs, cut in half)\n| 100g [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| 50g [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 100g [[Cider|cider]] or [[White wine|white wine]]\n| 80g water with a teaspoon of [[Vegetable|vegetable]] [[Bouillon|bouillon]] powder\n| [[Oregano]]\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| Seasoning\n| 1 large [[Potato|potato]], chopped into small pieces\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Oil|oil]] in the jug to heat for '''8 minutes / Temp Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Meanwhile, peel half of the [[Garlic|garlic]] and when the [[Oil|oil]] has heated add the garlic to the jug without stopping the machine and increase to '''Speed 5''' for a few seconds until chopped.\n| Reduce to '''Speed 1''' and allow to saut\u00e9.\n| Add the [[Chicken|chicken]] and the remaining unpeeled [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves (just cut them through the middle).\n| Set to '''10 Minutes / Temp Varoma / Reverse Blade / Speed Spoon'''.\n| After this time, add the remaining ingredients and programme for '''30 minutes, Temp. Varoma / Reverse Blade / Speed Spoon'''.\n| Should it seem to dry out, add small quantities of water.\n| Serve immediately drizzled with the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nIf desired, [[Steam|steam]] some [[Vegetables|vegetables]] in the Varoma for the last 15-20 minutes of the cooking time and serve with [[Bread|bread]].\n===Chef's Notes===\nYou can peel the [[Garlic|garlic]] in the [[Thermomix]] before starting on the recipe. The following version is Spanish\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 233\n|PortionCalories = 58\n|DatePublished=6th April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4 to 6 people\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 25 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Now that's a lot of garlic!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Delicious!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe is traditionally [[French]], but has now become part of the cuisine of [[Spain]].  The following version is [[Spanish]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 60 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Freshly [[Ground|ground]] [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| &frac12; a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| Several [[Rosemary#Sprigs_of_rosemary|sprigs of fresh rosemary]]\n| 1 bulb [[Garlic|garlic]], cut in half, but not peeled\n| 1 [[Chicken|chicken]] weighing 1.5-2 kg, washed and [[Dried|dried]], [[parson's nose removed]]\n| 4 bulbs [[Garlic|garlic]], separated into [[Cloves|cloves]], but not peeled\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Place a [[Roasting|roasting]] tin containing the [[Oil|oil]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] in the [[Oven|oven]] and preheat to 230\u00b0 C (450\u00b0 F - gas 8).  \n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Lemon|lemon]] half, [[Rosemary|rosemary]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] halves in the cavity of the [[Chicken|chicken]].\n| Reduce the temperature to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5) and [[Brown|brown]] it for about 5 minutes on each of the three sides.  If you use a rack in your roasting tin, do not use it at this stage.\n| After this stage put the [[chicken]] on its rack (if using) in the oven.\n| Cover the [[Chicken|chicken]] with a double layer of [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]] and [[Roast|roast]] for 1&frac14;-1&frac34; hours until done.\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves after one hour.\n| Remove from [[Oven|oven]] and allow to rest, covered, for about 15 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with the [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves which can be squeezed over the [[Chicken|chicken]].  [[Steamed]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]] of your choice and [[Mashed potatoes|mashed potatoes]] would go well with this dish.\n===Variations===\nThere are many variations.  Sometimes, [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces are used and cooked in a pan.  You can use other [[Herbs|herbs]] or replace the [[Oil|oil]] with [[Butter|butter]].  It can be made as a [[Casserole|casserole]], with [[Almond|almond]] slithers.\n===Chef's notes===\nYou do not need to have exactly 40 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]].  It is an estimate only, so just throw in as many as you like.  The [[Garlic|garlic]] will taste sweet and not be at all pungent.\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo]]\n[[Category:French recipes|Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Pollo con 40 dientes de ajo]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pollocon40dientesdeajo #garlic #chicken #lemon #french #almond #vegetables #miseenplace #mashedpotatoes #roast #ground </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Pork and strawberry salad with grilled halloumi cheese",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pork and strawberry salad with grilled halloumi cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#strawberries #oliveoil #basil #halloumi #zest #porkandstrawberrysaladwithgrilledhalloumicheese #fry #salad #juice #lime #spanish \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The idea for this recipe came from Jamie Olivers Jamie at Home. Ive often used fruit in savoury recipes but never with strawberries. They have a..\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=7th August 2016\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  55 minutes\n|PrepTime =  45 minutes\n|CookTime =  10 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 805\n|PortionCalories = 402\n|Image = [[Image:Pork and strawberry salad with grilled halloumi cheese.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Glorious</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I cannot wait for strawberry season to begin again</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThe idea for this recipe came from Jamie Oliver's ''Jamie at Home''.  I've often used [[Fruit|fruit]] in  savoury recipes but never with [[Strawberries|strawberries]].  They have a fantastic flavour and just the right amount of tartness to cut a fatty meat such as [[pork]].\n\nAs it's August, Morrison's (and probably every other supermarket) has [[Strawberries|strawberries]] on special offer - 2 x 400g cartons of British strawberries for \u00a33.00 so what you don't use in this recipe you can enjoy with a dollop of [[Soured cream|soured cream]] as a sweet.\n\n''Most of the preparation time is spent in allowing the cooked ingredients to cool''.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 200g fresh [[strawberries]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]] (or [[Balsamic|balsamic]] glaze)\n| [[Juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]]\n| 1 small [[Basil|basil]] plant (supermarket-type)\n| 5 tablespoons of [[Extra virgin Olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 200g [[Halloumi cheese|halloumi cheese]], sliced to 5mm\n| 10 fresh [[Mint leaves|mint leaves]], finely chopped\n| A small bag of tender [[Salad|salad]] leaves\n| 1 small red onion, peeled and very thinly sliced\n| 120g selection of continental [[Meats|meats]] (eg: Morrisons '[[Spanish]] Platter')\n| [[Salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:The easy way to remove the peduncle from a strawberry.jpg|300px|thumb|right|The easiest way I've found to remove the peduncle (''petiole'') from a strawberry is with a pair of long-nosed pliers\nImage:Morrison's Spanish Platter.jpg|300px|thumb|right|Morrison's Spanish platter (120g - \u00a32)\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pick most of the [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] for 5 minutes in 5 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Allow to cool and drain the [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Sieve|sieve]] and discard the leaves\n| [[Fry]] the sliced [[Halloumi|halloumi]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or [[Griddle|griddle]] tray for 2 minutes a side, moistening the pan with a smear of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Remove the [[Cheese|cheese]] allow to cool, then chop into smaller slices\n| De-hull the [[Strawberries|strawberries]] (my long-nosed plier tip works brilliantly on strawberries that are not over-ripe).  Cut the strawberries into thin slices. \n| When the [[Basil|basil]] infused [[Oil|oil]] has cooled, mix it with the [[Juice|juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Add the [[Strawberries|strawberries]] and the [[Oil|oil]] to a bowl and leave them until you are ready to put the dish together.  Drain and reserve the [[Strawberry|strawberry]]/[[Basil|basil]] oil to use a a final dressing.\n| With the cold sliced [[Halloumi|halloumi]] as a base, build the [[Salad|salad]] in layers with the salad leaves, mint leaves, sliced onions, Spanish meats and the remaining fresh basil leaves. Finally drizzle with the flavoured [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| This dish was fantastic, I loved the idea so much that some more [[Strawberries|strawberries]] have already been bought to go with Sunday's [[Roast pork|roast pork]]!\n}}\n===Variations===\nThis would make a brilliant [[Starter|starter]] and an impressive anti-pasta dish.\n\nMake a spicy version; use [[Hugh's fried halloumi]].\n{{SeeAlso-HalloumiRecipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#strawberries #oliveoil #basil #halloumi #zest #porkandstrawberrysaladwithgrilledhalloumicheese #fry #salad #juice #lime #spanish </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
