title": "Porra Antequerana",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Porra Antequerana, a Spanish tapa recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#ham #tomatoes #paprika #bread #garlic #tuna #eggs #breadcrumbs #porraantequerana #lemonjuice #roasted \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Porra is a member of the gazpacho family, but is not a soup. It is much thicker and is invariably served as a tapa\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1624\n|PortionCalories = 406\n|DatePublished=16th August 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4 - ''Several people as a [[tapa]]''\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Porra Antequerana recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice garlic dip</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.9</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Reminds me of holidays.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nPorra is a member of the [[gazpacho]] family, but is not a [[Soup|soup]].  It is much thicker and is invariably served as a [[tapa]].  \n\nAntequera is about 50 km inland from M\u00e1laga and \"Antequerana\" seems to be the generic name for this dish, but bars and restaurants in that part of Spain sometimes name it after their own particular town or village.  See below for ''La Porra Archidonesa'', a piece of free verse\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250 g stale [[Bread|bread]], made into [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 4 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] \n| 125 ml [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Smoked|smoked]] or unsmoked [[Paprika|paprika]]\n| 250 g ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], skinned - if these are unavailable, weigh the equivalent amount of tinned tomatoes\n| 4 teaspoons [[Wine|wine]] or [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]], or [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| [[Salt]] \n| 2 [[Hard boiled eggs|hard boiled eggs]]\n| 100 g serrano [[Ham|ham]] \n| 1 tin of [[Tuna|tuna]] in [[Oil|oil]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] in water for a few minutes - but see the poem below!.  If you are using tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], the [[Juice|juice]] is excellent for soaking.\n| Squeeze the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] to extract as much liquid from them as you can and put them in a [[Blender|blender]] or [[Food processor|food processor]] with the [[Garlic|garlic]].  Pulse for a few seconds to ensure that the garlic is finely chopped.\n| Add the [[Oil|oil]], [[Paprika|paprika]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Vinegar|vinegar]] or [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]].  Blend thoroughly until the mixture is smooth and thick.  Add [[Salt|salt]] to taste and chill briefly.\n| Meanwhile, chop the [[Ham|ham]] quite finely and drain and [[Mash|mash]] the [[Tuna|tuna]] (if using).  Chop the [[Eggs|eggs]] into smallish pieces.\n| Pour the porra mixture in small bowls and place the [[Ham|ham]], [[Tuna|tuna]] and [[Eggs|eggs]] on top of it in separate places.  Do not mix them in.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with pieces of crusty [[Bread|bread]] and small [[Breadsticks|breadsticks]].  Eat with a fork, not a spoon.\n\n===Variations===\nThere are many, many variations of porra, eg. sometimes a skinned [[Roasted|roasted]] [[Pepper|pepper]] is added or the [[Paprika|paprika]] left out.   However, you must ensure that the proportion of [[Bread|bread]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Oil|oil]] are the same as above and that you do include some [[Garlic|garlic]], even if it is only one [[Clove|clove]].  To make Porra archidonesa, omit the [[paprika]] and add a skinned [[Roasted|roasted]] green [[Pepper|pepper]].\n\n[[Eggs]] and [[Ham|ham]] are always added as a garnish.\n\n===Chef's tip===\nFor extra richness, a dash or two of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] can be added to the surface.\n\nSerrano [[Ham|ham]] is available in most supermarkets, including \"budget\" supermarkets such as Lidl's.  If you are unable to get it, substitute with another sort of dry-cured ham.  Do not use ordinary [[Boiled|boiled]] ham.\n\nWhilst porra is officially a tapa, it would also make an excellent first course.  Do not serve too much though as it is rather filling.\n\n== A poem:  La Porra Archidonesa ==\nby Miguel Salcedo Hierro translated from '''Gazpachos, Sopas y Ajos Blancos''' by Enrique Mapelli L\u00f3pez, Editorial Arguval (M\u00e1laga) ISBN 8495948702\n\nIn a round \u2018dornillo\u2019 <sup>[[#Foot1|1]]</sup>\n\none throws salt and one or two garlics<sup>[[#Foot2|2]]</sup>\n\na large green pepper\n\nand three peeled tomatoes.\n\nAll of this you begin to crush\n\ntogether with smashed pieces of bread;\n\nwithout soaking the latter\n\n-for that is for bad porras-.\n\nto it one adds little by little\n\nlight olive oil\n\nand a large dash of vinegar,\n\nthat is to give it a sharp edge.\n\nOne beats, beats, how one beats ...\n\nAnd we give ourselves a rest\n\nwhen all is merged\n\nwhen all is thickened.\n\nTo the porra of Archidona\n\nwe will go, spoon in hand!\n\n=====''Footnotes''=====\n* <span id=\"Foot1\"><sup>1</sup> A dornillo is a type of wooden bowl\n* <span id=\"Foot2\"><sup>2</sup> I think this means 2 cloves rather than 2 bulbs of garlic\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Porra]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Porra]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Porra]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Porra]]\n[[Category:Starters|Porra]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Porra]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Porra]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#ham #tomatoes #paprika #bread #garlic #tuna #eggs #breadcrumbs #porraantequerana #lemonjuice #roasted </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

= Prueba de cerdo\n |Servings = 4 or 8 as a [[Tapa|tapa]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours\n |CookTime = 40 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pork in vinegar Start this recipe one day in advance\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1317\n|PortionCalories = 329\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 20 minutes plus overnight marinading\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes plus overnight\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Rape en abodo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely monkfish</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The nicest fish, this marinade is not bad either.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nFrom the M\u00e1laga region of Spain, this is a simple recipe for [[Marinated|marinated]] [[Monkfish|monkfish]].  Start this recipe one day in advance.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg [[Monkfish|monkfish]] tail, skinned and cut into medium sized pieces\n| 300 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 300 ml [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| 6 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon sweet [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| &frac14; teaspoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| [[Flour]]\n| Extra [[Oil|oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix all of the ingredients together in a bowl, except for the [[Flour|flour]] and extra [[Oil|oil]].\n| [[Marinate]] overnight in the [[Fridge|fridge]].\n| The next day, drain the [[Fish|fish]] thoroughly and dredge the pieces in [[Flour|flour]].\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a deepish pan, until it is almost [[Smoking|smoking]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Fish|fish]] until it is crisp and golden.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nIt can be served as a [[Tapa|tapa]] or with [[Piperrana andal\u00faz|piperrana andal\u00faz]].\n===Variations===\nAny firm and boneless [[Fish|fish]] such as [[Dogfish|dogfish]] can be used.\n===Chef's notes===\nIt is important that the [[Oil|oil]] is very hot for this recipe.\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 11:54, 30 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Monkfish]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Monkfish]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Monkfish]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes|Monkfish]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Monkfish]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Monkfish]]\n[[Category:Starters|Monkfish]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#flour #fish #monkfish #whitewinevinegar #marinated #fridge #oliveoil #marinate #fry #garlic #smoking </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Saffron|saffron]] and [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] '''5 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 3&frac12;'''.\n| Push the ingredients down into the bowl and scrape the lid.\n| Put the [[Butterfly|butterfly]] on the blades, add the water, [[Spinach|spinach]], a little [[Pepper|pepper]], the [[Stock cube|stock cube]] and the [[Raisins|raisins]] into the bowl '''10 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Reverse Blade / Speed Spoon'''.\n| Drain the [[Spinach|spinach]] and sprinkle the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] over it.\n| Put the [[Spinach|spinach]] into a serving dish and decorate it with some more [[Almonds|almonds]].\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''Cocina espa\u00f1ola con Thermomix'''''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#spinach #almonds #vinegar #breadcrumbs #garlic #raisins #frozen #vegetablestock #oliveoil #stockcube #thermomix </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Salmorejo",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Salmorejo, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#salmorejo #garlic #mayonnaise #porraantequerana #bread #tomatoes #egg #oliveoil #wine #gazpacho #sherryvinegar \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A member of the gazpacho family, salmorejo is similar to porra antequerana but comes from western Andalucia, most notably the province of Cordoba\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1323\n|PortionCalories = 44\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Salmorejo, with lots of ground pepper\n |Servings = Servings: 30 - Makes more than 1.75 litres of salmorejo\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = none\n |Image = [[Image:Salmorejo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tomato glut champion</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Ever wondered what to do with all those tomatoes? \ud83c\udf45\ud83c\udf45\ud83c\udf45</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nA member of the [[Gazpacho|gazpacho]] family, salmorejo is similar to [[Porra Antequerana|porra antequerana]] but comes from western Andaluc\u00eda, most notably the province of C\u00f3rdoba. This is another good excuse to use your [[tomato press]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 whole [[Egg|egg]], plus one yolk\n| 1-2 bulbs [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| 1 litre [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 380 g [[Bread|bread]]\n| 1.2 kg ripe [[Tomatoes, peeled|tomatoes, peeled]]\n| [[Salt]], to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a [[Food processor|food processor]], or using a stick [[Blender|blender]], beat the [[Egg|egg]] and the yolk.\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves and process until the mixture is smooth.\n| Add some [[Oil|oil]], a little at a time, then some [[Bread|bread]] and some of the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n| Keep repeating this process until all of the ingredients have been used.\n| Add [[Salt|salt]] as desired.\n| The salmorejo should have the consistency of soft [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nIt is commonly served as a [[Tapa|tapa]] and like [[Porra Antequerana|porra]], is tradtionally accompanied by chopped, [[Hard-boiled egg|hard-boiled egg]] and [[Serrano ham]].   However, I like to use it as a [[Sauce|sauce]] or a [[Dip|dip]].  Also try it in sandwiches instead of [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].\n===Variations===\nThere are many variations of salmorejo.  You may wish to add a few tablespoons of [[Wine|wine]] or [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]].  I used half olive oil and half [[rapeseed]] oil - not authentic, but nice.  The [[Garlic|garlic]] quantity can be varied to taste.  Initially I made it with 1 bulb, but you can hardly taste it, so be BRAVE!!\n===Chef's notes===\nThe quantity given is rather large and only just fits in the largest bowl of a Magimix.  I would suggest making half or even a quarter of the volume to start with, unless you have a glut of [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] or are addicted to salmorejo.  I have and I am.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Salmorejo]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces|Salmorejo]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Salmorejo]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Salmorejo]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Salmorejo]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Salmorejo]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salmorejo #garlic #mayonnaise #porraantequerana #bread #tomatoes #egg #oliveoil #wine #gazpacho #sherryvinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Salmorejo (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Salmorejo - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tomatoes #ham #garlic #salmorejo #eggs #vinegar #refrigerate #thermomix #breadcrumbs #tapa #serranoham \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a Thermomix recipe, but a non-Thermomix recipe is available here\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 764\n|PortionCalories = 127\n|DatePublished=22nd October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 40 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Salmorejo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A different salad</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice to dip pittas in</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a [[Thermomix]] recipe, but a non-Thermomix recipe is available [[Salmorejo|here]].  It is normally served as a [[Tapa|tapa]], particularly in the C\u00f3rdoba province of [[Spain]].  If [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] are out of season, I make this with tinned ones.\n\n'''To garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 4 [[Hard-boiled eggs|hard-boiled eggs]]\n| 40g [[Serrano ham]]\n| 1 kg ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 2 [[Cloves|cloves]] [[Garlic|garlic]] (or more, taste)\n| 20g [[vinegar]] (white wine or sherry)\n| 110g [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 0.5 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 100g [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n}}\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Eggs|eggs]] into the bowl and chop '''2 seconds / Speed 4'''.  Remove and reserve.\n| Next, put the [[Ham|ham]] in the bowl and press the '''Turbo''' 4 or 5 times.  \n| Check the size and if you want it to be chopped more finely, press the '''Turbo''' 3 or 4 times more.  The time depends on how hard the [[Ham|ham]] is.  Remove from the bowl and reserve.\n| Without washing the bowl, add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Salt|salt]] '''30 seconds / Speed 5'''.\n| Add the [[Bread|bread]] and [[Vinegar|vinegar]] '''30 seconds / Speed 5''' and '''2 minutes / Speed 10'''.  The time will depend on the quality of the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]].\n| Running on '''Speed 5''', a pour the [[Oil|oil]], little by little, onto the lid, without removing the MC, until it has finished emulsifying.\n| Finally, pour the [[Salmorejo|salmorejo]] into a dish and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]], until you are ready to serve.\n| A few minutes before, decorate with the [[Ham|ham]] and the [[Eggs|eggs]].  Serve very cold.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* Translated and adapted from a recipe by [http://www.thermorecetas.com/receta-facil-thermomix-salmorejo/ Thermo Recetras] under [https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-nc-sa/2.5/es/ Creative Commons-CC BY-NC-SA 2.5 ES]\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you wish, you can use 1.5 kg [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and increase the other ingredients in proportion.  \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tomatoes #ham #garlic #salmorejo #eggs #vinegar #refrigerate #thermomix #breadcrumbs #tapa #serranoham </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

It is a perfect [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] for [[Meat|meat]], [[Fish|fish]] or [[Salads|salads]].\n\nIt is served cold. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#thermomix #onion #sauce #balsamicvinegar #herbs #accompaniment #tarragon #blackpepper #fish #oliveoil #oregano </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Salsa Concentrada de Tomate Pera (Concentrated Plum Tomato Sauce) (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->{{#seo:\n|title=Salsa Concentrada de Tomate Pera Thermomix plum sauce recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#onion #sauce #basil #thermomix #oliveoil #plumtomatoes #pizzas #tomato #sieve #sterilisedjars #thermomixrecipes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This Concentrated Plum Tomato Sauce recipe is a translation of a recipe in Salsas y Alinos con Thermomix (Susaeta Ediciones)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 202\n|PortionCalories = 10\n|DatePublished=31st August 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = The new [[Thermomix]] TM5 (2014)\n |Servings = Servings: 20 - Makes 500 ml\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 55 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Easy puree</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Good for excess tomatoes</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n\n<!-- If providing a photo for this recipe:\n 1 remove the Thermomix_recipes_awaiting_image.jpg tag\n 2 remove this message\n 3 remove the ImageComment \"Thermomix TM31 - the ultimate gadget!\"\n 4 replace with a comment if different to the recipe name in the box above the picture\n 5 replace image tag with a unique image name. eg: same as the recipe pagename\n 6 revert the 250px size to 300px\n-->\n\nThis is a translation of a recipe in '''Salsas y Ali\u00f1os con [[Thermomix]] (Susaeta Ediciones)'''\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 1kg very ripe [[Plum tomatoes|plum tomatoes]]\n| &frac12; [[Onion|onion]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 sprig of [[Basil|basil]]\n| 1 sprig of [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| &frac12; teaspoons [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Peel and cut the [[Onion|onion]], put it in the bowl and chop '''5 seconds / Speed 4'''.  Remove from the bowl and reserve.\n| Wash the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], cut them up and place in the bowl '''20 seconds / Speed 4'''.\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Oil|oil]], [[Salt|salt]], [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Basil|basil]].\n| Program '''45 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 2'''.\n| It is advisable to remove the MC so that the [[Sauce|sauce]] evaporates and becomes more concentrated.\n| Afterwards, replace the MC in the lid and [[Blend|blend]] '''1 minute / Speed 6''' so that you get a homogenous [[Sauce|sauce]].\n| Place the mixture in a [[Sieve|sieve]] to drain off any excess water to give it a thicker consistency.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nConcentrated [[Tomato|tomato]] is very suitable for the improvement of the flavour, colour and texture of other [[Sauces|sauces]].  It is also ideal for [[Pizzas|pizzas]].  \n===Chef's notes===\nThis [[Sauce|sauce]] will keep for several months in [[Sterilised jars|sterilised jars]] and kept in a dark, dry place.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#onion #sauce #basil #thermomix #oliveoil #plumtomatoes #pizzas #tomato #sieve #sterilisedjars #thermomixrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Salsa de Cebolla (Onion Sauce) (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

For [[Boiled|boiled]] or [[Steamed|steamed]] vegetables you can add [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] and various [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Spices|spices]] to it such as [[Tarragon|tarragon]], [[Rosemary|rosemary]] or [[Coriander|coriander]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#mustard #tabasco #parsley #chives #thermomix #vegetables #steamed #blend #greekyogurt #sauce #tarragon </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Salsa Romesco",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Salsa Romesco, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#salsaromesco #tomatoes #garlic #salsa #vinegar #peppers #roasting #grilled #ancho #fish #whitewinevinegar \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a nut, pepper, and tomato sauce originally from Tarragona\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4906\n|PortionCalories = 272\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 18 - Makes about 500m\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 1 hour\n |CookTime = 20 minutes \n |Image = [[Image:Salsa Romesco recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Good for my tomato glut</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">We've always got too  many left over. This is an ideal way to use them.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a [[Nut|nut]], [[Pepper|pepper]], and [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] originally from Tarragona.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 [[\u00f1oras]]\n| 100 ml [[Oil|oil]] olive oil\n| 500 g [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], whole or sliced in half\n| 25 g [[Almonds|almonds]], skinned\n| 25 g hazelnuts, skinned\n| 5 slices stale [[French stick]]\n| 1 bulb [[Garlic|garlic]], skins intact\n| 1-2 tablespoons [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| [[Salt|salt]] to taste \n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to Gas 6/200C/400F\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the [[\u00f1oras]] in cold water for about an hour, having removed stalks and [[Seeds|seeds]] if required.\n| Meanwhile place the [[Oil|oil]] into a small [[Roasting|roasting]] tin and place it into a cool oven.  \n| Once the oven has reached temperature, place all of the other ingredients into the tin, except for the [[vinegar]].\n| After about 10 minutes turn the ingredients over and leave to roast for another 10 minutes.  It is a good idea to check the oven regularly to prevent over-cooking or burning.\n| Drain the ingredients into a [[Blender|blender]] or food-processor, having peeled the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Garlic|garlic]], reserving the [[Oil|oil]].\n| Add the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] and [[\u00f1oras]] to the [[Salsa|salsa]] and blend throughly.\n| Add the reserved [[Oil|oil]], little by little until you have the required thickness.  Season to taste. and if necessary, add more oil.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Meat|meat]], [[Fish|fish]] or [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and can also be used as a dressing.\n\n===Variations===\nTraditionally, the [[Nuts|nuts]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Bread|bread]] are [[Grilled|grilled]], but I find that [[Roasting|roasting]] gives a richer flavour.\n\nSome people like to include piquillo [[Peppers|peppers]] to the [[Salsa|salsa]] as they add sweetness.\n\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you cannot find [[\u00f1oras]], [[Ancho|ancho]] [[Peppers|peppers]] can be substituted.\n\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Salsa romesco]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces|Salsa romesco]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Salsa romesco]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Salsa romesco]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salsaromesco #tomatoes #garlic #salsa #vinegar #peppers #roasting #grilled #ancho #fish #whitewinevinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

guindilla [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 150g [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 100g [[Onion|onion]]\n| 2 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| 2 very mature [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 25g [[Vinegar|vinegar]]\n| [[Pepper]]\n| &frac12; teaspoons [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Remove the [[Seeds|seeds]] from the \u00f1oras, peel the [[Garlic|garlic]] and chop the guindilla.\n| Place the [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Hazelnuts|hazelnuts]], [[\u00f1oras]] and guindilla in the bowl.\n| Process '''10 seconds / Speed 6''' and reserve.\n| To make the [[Sofrito|sofrito]], put the [[Onion|onion]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] in the bowl, together with 30g of the [[Oil|oil]].\n| [[Blend]] '''7 seconds / Speed 6''' and then cook '''5 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 1'''.\n| Incorporate the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] followed by the previously reserved mixture of [[Nuts|nuts]], \u00f1oras and guindilla.\n| [[Blend]] '''15 seconds / Speed progressively 5 to 10'''.\n| With the MC in place, pour the remaining 120g [[Olive oil|olive oil]] onto the lid, little by little at '''Speed 4'''.\n| When all the [[Oil|oil]] has fallen into the bowl, add the [[Salt|salt]] and a pinch of [[Pepper|pepper]] with the machine still running for a few seconds and then stop.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n[[Salsa Romesco]] belongs to the traditional cooking of Catalonia; its origin is Tarragona.  It is used as much with [[Fish|fish]] as it is an [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] to barbecued  [[Rabbit|rabbit]].  It is a recipe which [[Dates|dates]] from the 16th century, when, thanks to the discovery of America, when [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] became known in Europe.  This [[Sauce|sauce]] will be tastier if prepared a day in advance.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #tomatoes #thermomix #hazelnuts #blend #vinegar #onion #toasted #almonds #accompaniment #sauce </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Fish]] is very good if cooked in the sauce.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#bread #parsley #garlic #anchovies #sauce #thermomix #roast #whiterice #blend #egg #vinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Slow Roasted Lamb with Allioli",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Slow Roasted Lamb with Allioli a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#potatoes #lambstock #lamb #slowroastedlambwithallioli #garlic #thymeleaves #belazu #sherry #freshlygroundpepper #garlicmayonnaise #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Allioli is the Catalan version of aioli, the delicious Provencal garlic mayonnaise\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 14755\n|PortionCalories = 1844\n|DatePublished=11th March 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 8\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 5 hours\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes\n |CookTime = 4 hours 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Slow Roasted Lamb with Allioli recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Sunday lunch, sorted!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Well, I know what we've got for dinner this weekend!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nAllioli is the Catalan version of a\u00efoli, the delicious Proven\u00e7al [[Garlic mayonnaise|garlic mayonnaise]]. In Catalonia \"all i oli\" is usually served on the side with [[Fish|fish]], [[Meat|meat]] or [[Seafood|seafood]].\n[[Image:Slow Roasted Lamb with Allioli roasted garlic.jpg|thumb|300px|right|[[Half a leg of lamb]], Just out of the oven]]\n\nIf this takes your fancy then here are some more areas that may interest you:\n* A selection of [[Garlic mayonnaise|garlic mayonnaise]] recipes\n* [[:Category:Garlic recipes|Garlic recipes]]\n* Many other [[slow roast recipes]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.8kg whole [[Leg of lamb|leg of lamb]]\n| 6 whole bulbs of [[Garlic|garlic]], papery outer skin removed \n| 2 tablespoons [[Belazu]] Catalonian [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] \n| 4000ml fino (dry) [[Sherry|sherry]] \n| &frac12; x 142ml fresh [[Lamb stock|lamb stock]]\n| [[Salt|salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] \n}}\n'''For the [[Potatoes|potatoes]]:'''\n* 1.15kg Desiree [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled \n* 142ml fresh [[Lamb stock|lamb stock]] \n* 2 teaspoons fresh [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]] \n* [[Salt|salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] \n'''For the allioli:'''\n* 1 large Clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed \n* 1 large [[Egg|egg]], at room temperature \n* 250ml [[Belazu]] Catalonian [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] \n* 1 tablespoon [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] \n* [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] for the [[Lamb|lamb]] in a large pan and [[Brown|brown]] the [[Leg of lamb|leg of lamb]] all over. Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Freshly ground pepper|freshly ground pepper]], put in an oiled [[Roasting|roasting]] tin and [[Roast|roast]] in the middle of the [[Oven|oven]] for 20 minutes.\n| After this time, remove the [[Lamb|lamb]] from the [[Oven|oven]] and reduce the heat to 170\u00b0C, 325\u00b0F, Gas mark 3. Add 310ml of the [[Sherry|sherry]] to the lamb, cover tightly with [[Foil|foil]], and cook on the bottom shelf of the oven for 4 hours, [[Basting|basting]] every 30 minutes with the sherry. Add the 6 [[Garlic|garlic]] bulbs after 2 hours. Check that the sherry is not drying up, and add more if necessary.\n| While you are cooking the [[Lamb|lamb]], make the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and the allioli. Cut the potatoes into very thin rounds, put in a large pan of [[Salted|salted]] water and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]. Drain, place in a shallow oiled [[Oven|oven]] proof dish, season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Freshly ground pepper|freshly ground pepper]], then add the half tub of [[Lamb stock|lamb stock]] and sprinkle over the [[Thyme leaves|thyme leaves]].\n| Place in the oven on the shelf above the lamb for the last 1 hour 30 minues of the cooking time, after which time the potatoes will be golden and will have absorbed all the lamb [[Stock|stock]].\n| While the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] are cooking, make the allioli. Pur\u00e9e the Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] with the [[Egg|egg]] in a [[Food processor|food processor]], then mix the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and tablespoon of [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] together in a jug and slowly pour into the egg mixture with the motor running. Add half a teaspoon of [[Salt|salt]] and some [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] and leave the motor on for a further 10 seconds, then transfer to a bowl, ready to serve. ''[[Mayonnaise|See here for tips]] if you manage to split the mayonnaise.''\n| When the [[Lamb|lamb]] is ready, remove it from the [[Oven|oven]] and transfer to a wooden board. To make the [[Gravy|gravy]], mash the cooked garlic with a potato masher, add the remaining half tub of [[Lamb stock|lamb stock]] to the [[Roasting|roasting]] tin, bring to the [[Boil|boil]], season, strain through a coarse [[sieve]] or [[China cap]] and pour into a bowl, ready to serve. Carve the lamb and serve with the gravy and [[Potatoes|potatoes]], with a healthy dollop of allioli on top.\n}}\n(''Sainsbury\u0092s magazine'')\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/catalonian-arbequina.html Belazu Catalonian Arbequina Extra Virgin Olive Oil]\n===Chef's notes===\nUnfortunately, in common with a lot of the Belazu published recipes, they don't appear to have been very well tested.  I have increased the potato cooking time by 30 minutes and you may still need to finish them off under the grill if you want them crisped up a little.\nDon't be put off a recipe that calls for a leg of lamb because of the high cost.  This recipe can be adjusted for [[Frozen lamb - what great value!|half a leg of lamb and you buy that (frozen)]] for just \u00a36.00! (March 2013).\n==See also==\n* '''[[Meat cooking time calculator Metric|A comprehensive guide to roast meat cooking times]]''' - give the time you want to carve your roast and we'll give you a timed step by step roasting guide\n* [[Slow roast recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potatoes #lambstock #lamb #slowroastedlambwithallioli #garlic #thymeleaves #belazu #sherry #freshlygroundpepper #garlicmayonnaise #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

The mixture should be fairly thick.\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can include [[Paprika|paprika]] and/or finely chopped [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]] if you wish.\n===Servings===\nServings: 18 - Makes about 600 ml\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tomato sauce]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces|Tomato sauce]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Tomato sauce]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Tomato sauce]]\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Prepared foods]]\n[[Category:Vegetables]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #tomato #paprika #sweetpeppers #soffrito #juice #tomatosauce #tomatoes #oliveoil #grated #spanish </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Sopa de ajo prisionera ('Imprisoned' garlic soup)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sopa de ajo prisionera 'Imprisoned' garlic soup) Egg recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#egg #garlic #ham #soup #chickenstock #paprika #puffpastry #garlicsoup #brush #bread #broth \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description='Imprisoned' garlic soup\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4553\n|PortionCalories = 2276\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Lid removed\n |Servings = 2\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Lid removed.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Garlicky doesn't come close \ud83d\ude02</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Lovely if you love the stuff though!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n'Imprisoned' [[Garlic Soup|garlic soup]].  This recipe has been reproduced here in English by kind permission of '''[http://larecetadelafelicidad.blogspot.com/2008/12/sopa-de-ajo-prisionera.html SandeeA]'''.  \nIt is a [[Garlic Soup|garlic soup]] covered with [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]] and is absolutely delicious!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons [[Oil|oil]]\n| 4 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and sliced\n| 7 slices of stale [[Bread|bread]], although fresh can be used\n| 1 level tablespoon [[Paprika|paprika]] \n| 1 litre [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] (made from an [[Onion|onion]], a [[Carrot|carrot]], and a [[Chicken|chicken]] carcass)\n| 100 g small cubes of [[Ham|ham]] (shoulder of [[Jam\u00f3n ib\u00e9rico|Iberian ham]], preferably)\n| [[Salt]] to taste\n| 2 [[free range eggs]]\n| A little beaten [[Egg|egg]]\n| 500g [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 200 C/400 F/Gas 6\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Baked.jpg|Baked\nImage:Addition of beaten egg.jpg|Addition of beaten egg\nImage:Cooked in the stock.jpg|Cooked in the stock\nImage:The paprika and bread have been added.jpg|The paprika and bread have been added\nImage:Frying the garlic.jpg|Frying the garlic\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a pan, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and allow it to turn golden. \n| Add the [[Ham|ham]] cubes and saut\u00e9 them with the [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| Add the slices of [[Bread|bread]] to allow them to colour a little. \n| Add the [[Paprika|paprika]], and immediately afterwards the [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]], so that the [[paprika]] does not become bitter. \n| Allow the [[Soup|soup]] to [[Simmer|simmer]] over a gentle heat for half-an-hour.\n| Check for seasoning and add [[Salt|salt]] if necessary.\n| Take some heat-resistant earthenware [[Soup|soup]] bowls and pour the soup into them.\n| Break an [[Egg|egg]] into each bowl.\n| [[Brush]] the rims and the outside tops of the bowls with a little beaten [[Egg|egg]].\n| Cut circles of [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]], about a centimetre or so larger than the top of the bowls, seal around the rim and [[Brush|brush]] with beaten [[Egg|egg]].\n| You can decorate the pastry if you wish.\n| Put the bowls into the oven for 10-15 minutes until the pastry is golden and has formed a dome over the [[Soup|soup]].\n| By this time, the [[Eggs|eggs]] should be firm, but with a runny yolk.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThe most delicious way to eat this is to break the pastry into the [[Soup|soup]] or cut small pieces away as you eat the soup.  If you do not like pastry, just cut the whole thing off, but you will lose the best of the dish. \n \nAnd enjoy it ... who said that a [[Garlic Soup|garlic soup]] dish cannot be a luxury?\n===Variations===\nIf you are a vegetarian, leave out the [[Ham|ham]] and use [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]] or [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Broth|broth]] instead of [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]].\n\nI adapted the recipe slightly by using 4 whole bulbs of [[Garlic|garlic]], no [[ham]], beaten [[egg]] instead of a whole one and using [[Paprika|Piment\u00f3n de la Vera]] which accounts for the brightness of the colour.  And before anyone asks, yes, I did eat the whole lot myself!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Starters|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#egg #garlic #ham #soup #chickenstock #paprika #puffpastry #garlicsoup #brush #bread #broth </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

stock.jpg|Cooked in the stock\nImage:The paprika and bread have been added.jpg|The paprika and bread have been added\nImage:Frying the garlic.jpg|Frying the garlic\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a pan, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and allow it to turn golden. \n| Saut\u00e9 the [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| Add the slices of [[Bread|bread]] to allow them to colour a little. \n| Add the [[Paprika|paprika]], and immediately afterwards the [[vegetable stock]], so that the [[paprika]] does not become bitter. \n| Allow the [[Soup|soup]] to [[Simmer|simmer]] over a gentle heat for half-an-hour.\n| Preheat the oven to 200 C/400 F/Gas 6\n| Check for seasoning and add [[Salt|salt]] if necessary.\n| Take some heat-resistant earthenware [[Soup|soup]] bowls and pour the soup into them.\n| Break an [[Egg|egg]] into each bowl.\n| [[Brush]] the rims and the outside tops of the bowls with a little beaten [[Egg|egg]].\n| Cut circles of [[Puff pastry|puff pastry]], about a centimetre or so larger than the top of the bowls, seal around the rim and [[Brush|brush]] with beaten [[Egg|egg]].\n| You can decorate the pastry if you wish.\n| Put the bowls into the oven for 10-15 minutes until the pastry is golden and has formed a dome over the [[Soup|soup]].\n| By this time, the [[Eggs|eggs]] should be firm, but with a runny yolk.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThe most delicious way to eat this is to break the pastry into the [[Soup|soup]] or cut small pieces away as you eat the soup.  If you do not like pastry, just cut the whole thing off, but you will lose the best of the dish. And enjoy it ... who said that a [[Garlic Soup|garlic soup]] dish cannot be a luxury?\n\nI adapted the recipe slightly by using 4 whole bulbs of [[Garlic|garlic]], no [[ham]], beaten [[egg]] instead of a whole one and using [[Paprika|Piment\u00f3n de la Vera]] which accounts for the brightness of the colour.  And before anyone asks, yes, I did eat the whole lot myself!\n===Chef's notes===\nI need to find a way to stop the pastry from collapsing.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Starters|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Garlic soup imprisoned]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#egg #soup #garlic #garlicsoup #paprika #puffpastry #vegetablestock #brush #bread #freerangeegg #simmer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sopa de almendras de La Palma a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#potatoes #bayleaf #thyme #almonds #garlic #soup #vegetablestock #tomatoes #sopadealmendrasdelapalma #saffron #onion \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=La Palma is one of the lesser known Canary Islands, but it is famous for being the home of the Isaac Newton Group of telescopes (ING)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2297\n|PortionCalories = 574\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Spanish almonds\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Spanish almonds.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">  <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">True about the volcano, Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">It's erupting, now, as we speak! \ud83d\ude1f</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nLa Palma is one of the lesser known Canary Islands, but it is famous for being the home of the Isaac Newton Group of telescopes (ING).  It also has the world's largest volcanic crater. \n\nTheir main production crop is [[Almonds|almonds]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 250 g unpeeled whole [[Almonds|almonds]]\n| 1 kg firm [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled and cut into small cubes\n| 3-4 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], finely chopped\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped \n| 2 largish [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| A couple of sprigs of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| [[Black pepper]]\n| [[Salt]]\n| A few strands of [[Saffron|saffron]]\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]]\n| Water or [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Grind up the unpeeled [[Almonds|almonds]] in a food processor.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a saucepan, [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onion|onion]] and add the [[Garlic|garlic]] for a minute or two.\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]], [[Thyme|thyme]], [[Pepper|pepper]], [[Salt|salt]], [[Saffron|saffron]] and [[Clove|clove]].\n| Mix well and cook gently for a few minutes.\n| Add the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and stir, followed by the [[Ground almonds|ground almonds]].\n| It is ready when the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] are cooked, but if you find that you need to, top it up with water or [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]] to prevent it sticking and then adjust seasoning accordingly.\n| Remove the [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]], [[Thyme|thyme]] and [[Clove|clove]] before serving.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nAs it is intended to be a thick [[Soup|soup]], it is essential to watch it and stir it.  Do not use too much water - just enough to allow the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] to cook.\n\nTo save time, you could [[Par boil|par boil]] the cubed [[Potato|potato]] before adding it to the [[Soup|soup]].  However, start with potataoes in cold water, so that the cubes are less likely to break up as it is desirable to retain the whole cubes in the finished product.--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 09:54, 6 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Almond soup]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes|Almond soup]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes|Almond soup]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Almond soup]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Almond soup]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Almond soup]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potatoes #bayleaf #thyme #almonds #garlic #soup #vegetablestock #tomatoes #sopadealmendrasdelapalma #saffron #onion </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Spanish Thermomix bread - A Thermomix recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #butter #yeast #bread #browning #strongflour #thermomix #thermomixrecipes #spanish #bake #flour \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a basic bread recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2293\n|PortionCalories = 229\n|DatePublished=31st August 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = The new [[Thermomix]] TM5 (2014)\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - Makes a 1kg loaf\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 2 hours 45 minutes \n|PrepTime = 2 hours 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 30 minutes \n|Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Bread (and butter) recipe</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Standard fare (but to a good standard)</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a basic Thermomix [[Bread|bread]] recipe.\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 350g water (see Chef's notes below)\n| &frac12; teaspoons [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 40g fresh [[Bread|bread]] [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 600g [[Strong flour|strong flour]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Salt|salt]] (see Chef's notes below)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the water and the [[Sugar|sugar]] into the bowl '''2 minutes / 37\u00b0 / Speed 2'''\n| Add the [[Yeast|yeast]], mix for a few seconds, incorporate the [[Flour|flour]] and [[Salt|salt]] '''15-20 seconds / Speed 6'''\n| Next, [[Knead|knead]] '''3 minutes / Speed Dough'''\n| Remove the [[Dough|dough]] with oiled hands.\n| Shape as desired and leave to rise until double in size, covering it so that it does not form a crust\n| [[Bake]] for 25-30 minutes at 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\u00b0 \n| If you see that it is [[Browning|browning]] too much, reduce the temperature to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), Fan 180\u00b0 C \n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''Thermomix TM31 - Imprescindible para tu cocina''''' which is the book supplied with [[Spanish]] TMXs\n===Chef's notes===\nHaving made this [[dough]] this morning, I found it very hard to shape.  This is due to the recipe having only 58% hydration, ie not enough water, so next time, I will try it with 400g water.  Spanish [[butter]] is usually unsalted, so if you use salted [[butter]], I would reduce the [[salt]] quantity in the [[dough]].  However, in general the '''bread''' was good, crusty on the outside, with a nice, soft, but twisted looking crumb.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #butter #yeast #bread #browning #strongflour #thermomix #thermomixrecipes #spanish #bake #flour </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

In Spain, they seem to be eaten much more than they are in the UK\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2491\n|PortionCalories = 622\n|DatePublished=19th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 4 as a [[Main course|main course]] or 8 as a snack or first course\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Stewed quails recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not sure</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Still can't get my head round this!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThis recipe is based on a combination of [[Spanish]] recipes for [[quail]].  In [[Spain]], they seem to be eaten much more than they are in the UK.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 tablespoons [[Oil|oil]]\n| 8 oven-ready [[quails]]\n| 8 rashers of streaky [[Bacon|bacon]]\n| 3 medium [[Onions|onions]], peeled and [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, chopped\n| 2 teaspoons [[Dried oregano|dried oregano]]\n| 150 ml [[Dry cider|dry cider]] or [[White wine|white wine]]\n| 1 litre hot [[Vegetable|vegetable]] or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]], or enough to cover\n| Seasoning\n| Parsley to garnich, coarsely chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a saucepan.\n| Wrap a rasher of [[Bacon|bacon]] around each [[quail]] and add to the pan with the [[Onion|onion]].\n| Cook until all sides of the [[quails]] are beginning to [[Brown|brown]], the stir in the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Oregano|oregano]].\n| Cook for a few minutes until the [[Garlic|garlic]] is golden.\n| Add the [[Cider|cider]] or [[Wine|wine]], the [[Stock|stock]] and seasoning.\n| Cover, and [[Simmer|simmer]] for about 45 minutes until the quails are cooked.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGarnish with the [[parsley]] and serve with [[Fried potatoes|fried potatoes]] and/or [[Salad|salad]].\n===Chef's notes===\nWe added 1 bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] for 2 quails, but vary the quantity as desired.  We used back [[bacon]] which is too short really and fell off the [[quails]] as they were browning.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Game recipes|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Starters|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine|Quails stewed]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #stewedquails #bacon #quails #quail #cider #oregano #friedpotatoes #onion #wine #drycider </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Here in the\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 296\n|PortionCalories = 37\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 8 - Makes one jar of [[Sun-dried tomatoes]]\n|Difficulty = 1\n|ImageComment = Oven-dried cherry tomatoes - done\n|TotalTime = 7 hours 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 7 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Sun-dried tomatoes at home 1.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Who knew you could do this?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">What a brilliant idea, and it works so well.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n==Sun-dried tomatoes, without the sun==\n\n[[Sun-dried tomatoes]] are a great item to have in the [[refrigerator]] as they have a long shelf-life and a small amount can lift almost any dish.\n\nHere in the UK we seem to get very little sun so we have to resort to other methods.\n\nMaking [[Sun-dried tomatoes]] without the sun is an ideal task for a slow Aga.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 16 large, good flavoured [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] or 32 cherry tomatoes\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Caster sugar|caster sugar]]\n| A few sprigs of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 500ml of [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| Sea [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to it's lowest setting. About 100\u00b0 C (225\u00b0 F - gas &frac14;), Aga: 'simmering oven'\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| With a sharp knife, cut the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] in half.\n| Lay them out on [[baking tray]]s, lined with greaseproof paper, sprinkle with sugar and drizzle them with a little [[Olive|olive]] [[Oil|oil]].\n| Pick the [[thyme]] leaves off and sprinkle over the [[tomatoes]], if you have lots of thyme you can lay the sprigs amongst the tomatoes for extra flavour.\n| Place them in the oven for about 7 hours, or until most of the moisture has been removed - check them every hour or so as you don't want them to be crispy!\n| Remove them and leave them to cool\n| Sprinkle a [[Sterilised|sterilised]] jar with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and add the sprigs of [[Thyme|thyme]].\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and cover with [[Olive|olive]] [[Oil|oil]].\n| They should keep for 6 months if refrigerated and always covered with [[Oil|oil]].\n}}\n===Variations===\n\nAdd a tablespoon of [[Chili|chili]] flakes if you like them spicy.\n\n==See also==\n* '''[[Oven-dried tomatoes]]\n===FOOD POISONING===\n\nDon't add [[Garlic|garlic]] as some recipes suggest because there is a '''very real danger of botulism''' as it is an anaerobic toxin (one that develops in an air-free environment - read: [[Talk:Garlic olive oil]].\n\nIf you want to be really scared, [http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Botulism read what Wikipedia has to say on botulism].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Pickles and preserves]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Dehydrated]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tomatoes #thyme #olive #bakingtray #sterilised #sundriedtomatorecipe #garlic #refrigerator #blackpepper #castersugar #dehydrated </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

a [[Lemon|lemon]], or [[Vinegar|vinegar]]\n| 25g water\n| [[Salt]], to taste\n| 300g [[Oil|oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Chop the [[Gherkins|gherkins]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Capers|capers]] and [[Parsley|parsley]] in the bowl '''3-4 seconds / Speed 4-5'''.\n| Remove and reserve.\n| Chop the [[Hard boiled egg|hard boiled egg]] '''4 seconds / Speed 4'''.\n| Remove and reserve.\n| Without washing it, put the raw [[Egg|egg]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], water and [[Salt|salt]] into the bowl '''10 seconds / Speed 4'''.\n| With the MC in place on the lid program '''Speed 4''' and pour the [[Oil|oil]] on the lid, little by little.\n| Once the [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] has been made, add the chopped [[Pickles|pickles]] [and the [[Egg|egg]]] and mix well with the spatula.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''[[Thermomix]] TM31 - Imprescindible para tu cocina''''' which is the book supplied with [[Spanish]] TMXs.\n==See also==\n* [[Tartare Sauce (TM)]]\n* [[Quick tartare sauce]]\n* [[Tartare sauce (Mrs Beeton's)]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#egg #onions #spanish #gherkins #parsley #capers #thermomix #hardboiledegg #pickled #quicktartaresauce #juice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Tarta tres chocolates (TM)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tarta tres chocolates a Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chocolate #royalcuajada #cream #doublecream #fridge #biscuit #butter #favouriterecipes #spatula #frozen #refrigerate \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a three chocolate dessert set upon a biscuit base made in a Thermomix \n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 8855\n|PortionCalories = 1106\n|DatePublished=7th April 2015\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 8-10\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  35 minutes plus setting time\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes plus setting time\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Tarta tres chocolates TM recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Chocolate pie.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Meh!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a three [[Chocolate|chocolate]] [[Dessert|dessert]] set upon a [[Biscuit|biscuit]] base\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n}}\n====For the base:====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 small packet of biscuits (I used about 200g of plain Digestives, but the original was made with [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]] biscuits)\n| 100g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 20g [[Milk|milk]]\n}}\n====For the 1st layer:====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 150g plain, [[Dark chocolate|dark chocolate]]\n| 70g [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 250g [[Milk|milk]]\n| 250g [[Double Cream|double cream]]\n| 1 sachet [[Royal cuajada|cuajada]]\n}}\n====For the 2nd layer:====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 150g [[Milk|milk]] [[Chocolate|chocolate]]\n| 50g [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 250g [[Milk|milk]]\n| 250g [[Double Cream|double cream]]\n| 1 sachet [[Royal cuajada|cuajada]]\n}}\n====For the 3rd layer:====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 150g white [[Chocolate|chocolate]]\n| 25g [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 250g [[Milk|milk]]\n| 250g [[Double Cream|double cream]]\n| 1 sachet [[Royal cuajada|cuajada]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====For the base:====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Crush the biscuits 20 seconds / Speed 5-7-10\n| Add the [[Butter|butter]] in pieces, and the [[Milk|milk]] '''2 minutes / 70 degrees / Speed 3''' (you will need to scrape down the inside of the bowl at some stage)\n| Grease a loose bottomed tin, and line it with the mixture, smoothing it down, then place in the [[Fridge|fridge]]\n}}\n====For the 1st layer:====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Break the plain [[Chocolate|chocolate]] into pieces and place in the bowl with the [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Milk|milk]], [[Cream|cream]] and [[Royal cuajada|cuajada]] '''7 minutes / 90 degrees / Speed 5''' (I found that in my cold British kitchen, it needed an extra minute)\n| Tip onto the [[Biscuit|biscuit]] base and put in the [[Fridge|fridge]] until it has set\n}}\n====For the 2nd layer:====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Without washing the bowl, break the [[Milk|milk]] [[Chocolate|chocolate]] into pieces and place in the bowl with the [[Sugar|sugar]], milk, [[Cream|cream]] and [[Royal cuajada|cuajada]] '''7 minutes / 90 degrees / Speed 5''' (again, an extra minute may be required)\n| Drag a fork over the top of the previous layer to make ridges to [[Help|help]] the following layer stick and not run.\n| Tip the [[Milk|milk]] [[Chocolate|chocolate]] mixture into the tin, carefully spreading it evenly (without prodding) using a [[Spatula|spatula]] or reverse side of a spoon.  Take it to the [[Fridge|fridge]] again to set.\n}}\n====For the 3rd layer:====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Makes more ridges over the 2nd layer, wash the bowl well so that the colours do not mix.\n| Break the white [[Chocolate|chocolate]] into pieces and place in the bowl with the [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Milk|milk]], [[Cream|cream]] and [[Royal cuajada|cuajada]] '''7 minutes / 90 degrees / Speed 5'''.\n| Tip into the tin and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for several hours.\n| Once chilled un-mould it from the tin.\n| It can be [[Frozen|frozen]] whole, but do not cut beforehand or it may become gooey.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Recipe reproduced here with permission of La Juani de Ana Sevilla under Creative Commons (Save Creative) licence [http://www.juanideanasevilla.com/2011/07/tarta-tres-chocolates.html Tarta tres chocolates]\n===Chef's notes===\nThe original recipe is made in a [[Heart|heart]]-shaped tin, but if you don\u0092t have one, I would suggest using an 8 or 9 inch (20 or 23 cms) round tin or a 7 or 8 inch (18 or 20cm) square one. It just depends on how tall you want it. I used a 7 inch (18cm) round one which was too small so had to bin some of the mixture. Line with [[Bake-O-Glide]] if you like, then no need to grease.\n\nThe [[Chocolate|chocolate]] I used was that with the highest percentage of [[Cocoa|cocoa]] solids I could get.\n\nThe [[Royal cuajada|cuajada]] can be obtained from [[R Garcia & Sons]] in London.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chocolate #royalcuajada #cream #doublecream #fridge #biscuit #butter #favouriterecipes #spatula #frozen #refrigerate </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Terrina al jerez (Sherry terrine)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Terrina al jerez (Sherry terrine) a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#terrine #chicken #veal #foil #bread #lard #serranoham #roasting #pork #salami #salad \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This veal and chicken terrine is a garlicky adaptation of a recipe from Simone and Ines Ortega's book The Book of Tapas\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3704\n|PortionCalories = 168\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 22 - Makes 1 kg pat\u00e9\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime =  14 hours 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 14 hours 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Terrina al jerez (Sherry terrine) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Served with garlic bread I notice</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice to see that a leopard(ess) doesn't change her spots \ud83d\ude02</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\nThis [[Veal|veal]] and [[Chicken|chicken]] [[Terrine|terrine]] is a garlicky adaptation of a recipe from Simone and In\u00e9s Ortega's book '''The Book of [[Tapas]]''' (ISBN 0714856134).  Unlike like the [[Terrines|terrines]] I have made before, this one uses [[Lard|lard]], rather than solid [[Pork|pork]] [[Fat|fat]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Oil]]\n| 400 g boneless, skinless [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts or thighs\n| 500 g [[Veal|veal]], [[Minced|minced]]\n| 100 g [[Lard|lard]], softened, plus some extra\n| 2 tablespoons [[breadcrumbs]]\n| 3 bulbs [[Garlic, crushed|garlic, crushed]]\n| 2 [[Eggs|eggs]], beaten\n| 120 ml [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| Seasoning\n| 150 g [[Serrano ham]], in one piece then cut into small strips\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180C/gas 4.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat some [[Oil|oil]] in a non-stick [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and [[Brown|brown]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts on each side for 2 minutes.\n| Transfer to a small [[Roasting|roasting]] tin and [[Roast|roast]] for 12 minutes, or until cooked.\n| Remove from tin and allow to cool.\n| Meanwhile, mix together the remaining ingredients, except of the [[Serrano ham]].\n| When the [[Chicken|chicken]] has cooled, chop it roughly and add to the [[Veal|veal]] mixture.\n| Reduce the [[Oven|oven]] temperature to 160\u00b0 C (325\u00b0 F - gas 3).\n| Line a 1 kg [[Bread|bread]] pan or [[Terrine|terrine]] with [[Foil|foil]] and grease the foil with the extra [[Lard|lard]].\n| Starting with the [[Veal|veal]] and [[Chicken|chicken]] mixture, fill the [[Terrine|terrine]] by layering alternately with the [[Serrano ham]], ending with the veal.\n|  Cover the top of the [[Terrine|terrine]] with double-thickness of [[Tin foil|tin foil]], making a lengthways pleat to allow the [[Steam|steam]] to rise.\n|  Place the tin into a large [[Roasting|roasting]] tin and fill it with hot water so that it comes half-way up the side of the [[Bread|bread]] tin. Add further water as and when it is necessary\n| Cook for about two and a quarter hours, allowing an extra 15 minutes if the mixture has been [[Refrigerated|refrigerated]]. The [[Terrine|terrine]] is cooked when it has contracted from the sides of the tin and the [[Juice|juice]] runs yellow, when tested with a skewer.\n| Remove from [[Oven|oven]] and whilst it is still hot, place several cans, eg [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], horizontally and evenly on top of the [[Foil|foil]], to press the [[Terrine|terrine]]. Leave until completely cold.\n| Chill for several hours or overnight, still weighted down.\n| Remove the weights and [[Foil|foil]] and turn out onto clean foil.\n| Wrap the [[Foil|foil]] around it and leave the p\u00e2t\u00e9 until it has been cold for at least 24 hours before cutting.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with nice [[Bread|bread]], [[Salad|salad]] and a good strong [[Cheese|cheese]]. \n===Variations===\nExperiment with various types of [[Meat|meat]] such as [[Pork|pork]], [[Game|game]] and [[Salami|salami]] and try [[Wine|wine]], [[Calvados]] or [[Cider|cider]] instead of [[Sherry|sherry]].\n===Chef's notes===\nThis [[Terrine|terrine]] is very delicate, so be careful when slicing it.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Veal recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Steamed]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#terrine #chicken #veal #foil #bread #lard #serranoham #roasting #pork #salami #salad </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

Removing seeds can be a bit of a chore so I did not bother. title": "Tomate frito (TM)",

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tomate frito - A Thermomix recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tomatoes #carrots #garlic #thermomix #spanish #onion #sofrito #basilleaves #steaming #thermomixrecipes #tomatosauce \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A basic Spanish tomato sauce\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 302\n|PortionCalories = 10\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = The new [[Thermomix]] TM5 (2014) \n|Servings = Servings: 28 - Makes about 1kg\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 50 minutes \n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:The new (2014) Thermomix TM5.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Good sauce</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice with pasta</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nA basic [[Spanish]] [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 50g [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 2 [[Cloves|cloves]] [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| 100g [[Onion|onion]]\n| 100g [[Carrots|carrots]] (optional)\n| 1kg tinned, chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 30g [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| A few [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Pour the [[Oil|oil]] into the bowl '''3 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Onion|onion]] and [[Carrots|carrots]] '''10 seconds / Speed 5''' [push down ingredients in the bowl] then '''7 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 3&frac12;'''.\n| Push down the ingredients in the bowl and put the internal [[Steaming|steaming]] basket on the lid to avoid splashes.\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and the remaining ingredients '''30 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| If you want it thicker, you can cook it for '''5-10 minutes''' longer, so that the liquid evaporates.  If using [[Basil|basil]], do not add it until the last few minutes.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* This is a translation of a recipe in '''''[[Thermomix]] TM31 - Imprescindible para tu cocina''''' which is the book supplied with [[Spanish]] TMXs.\n===Variations===\nYou can use fresh [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], but they must be very red and ripe.  Make a cut into them and drain off all the liquid, by pressing them with your hands.  You will have to blitz them very well at '''Speed 6-7''', until you have a pur\u00e9e.  Take them out and reserve to add to the [[Sofrito|sofrito]] once it is made, because if they are blended together, they will lose their lovely red colour.\n\nIf, once the whole [[Sauce|sauce]] has finished cooking, you want to blitz the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] more, do not do this whilst the sauce is hot.  Wait until it has cooled a little and blitz at '''Speed 7''', but remember that by doing this you will get more of an [[Orange|orange]] colour.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tomatoes #carrots #garlic #thermomix #spanish #onion #sofrito #basilleaves #steaming #thermomixrecipes #tomatosauce </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon sweet [[Paprika|paprika]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]]\n| A pinch of [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| A pinch of [[Ground cloves|ground cloves]]\n| 1 guindilla [[Pepper|pepper]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Put the [[Oil|oil]] in the bowl '''5 minutes / Temp Varoma / Speed Spoon'''.\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Green pepper|green pepper]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] '''15 minutes / Temp Varoma / Reverse Blade / Speed Spoon / MC Off'''. \n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] '''45 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 1'''.\n| Add the remaining ingredients '''60 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 1''', until you have a thick pur\u00e9e.\n| Allow to cool slightly and blitz '''1 minute / Speed 5-10 progressively'''.\n| To thicken it, if necessary, cook for a further '''10-20 minutes / 90\u00b0 / Speed 3 / MC Off'''.\n| Pour into [[Sterilised jars|sterilised jars]] or a clean [[Lock and Lock boxes|Lock&Lock]] container.\n| Allow to cool and cover well.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* Lightly adapted from a PepeKitchen recipe at '''[http://www.directoalpaladar.com/recetas-de-salsas-y-guarniciones/receta-de-ketchup-casero Directo al Paladar]'''\n===Chef's notes===\nI used 1 whole bulb of [[garlic]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #tomatoes #thermomix #greenpepper #onion #cidervinegar #groundcloves #boiledorsimmered #tomatoketchup #paprika #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                "revisions": [
