                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tortas de aceite de oliva, romero y tomillo a breadmaker recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tortasdeaceitedeolivaromeroytomillo #rosemary #flour #bake #dough #thyme #driedthyme #driedyeast #walnut #yeast #whitebread \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I bought some of these and fell in love with them. They are thin biscuit-type affairs and are mostly sweetened\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 482\n|PortionCalories = 120\n|DatePublished=19th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Tortas de aceite de oliva, romero y tomillo\n |Servings = Serves 4 - Makes 16 crackers\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Tortas de aceite de oliva, romero y tomillo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">The Herbs then?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.9</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">\ud83d\ude09\ud83d\ude00\ud83d\ude0b</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nI bought some of these and fell in love with them.  They are thin biscuit-type affairs and are mostly sweetened.  However, '''[http://www.inesrosales.com/ Ines Rosales]''' of Seville also make them with rosemary and thyme and it is this variety which I attempt to reproduce here.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 50 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of [[Dried thyme|dried thyme]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of [[Dried|dried]] [[Rosemary|rosemary]]\n| 130 g [[White bread|white bread]] [[Flour|flour]] \n| 50 g wholemeal [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]]\n| 10 g fresh [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 80 g tepid water\n| &frac12; a teaspoon of [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| [[Sea salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] and allow the [[Thyme|thyme]] and [[Rosemary|rosemary]] to infuse gently/\n| Allow to get cool completely.\n| Pour into a bowl and add all of the remaining ingredients, except for the [[Salt|salt]].\n| Knead gently and allow to rise until doubled. \n| Shape the [[Dough|dough]] into little balls about the size of a [[Walnut|walnut]], and roll them out thinly. \n| Sprinkle with [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Bake|bake]] at 160\u00b0 C (325\u00b0 F - gas 3) until golden.\n}}\n===Variations===\nYou can make the [[Dough|dough]] in a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] if you wish, in which case use 5g easy-[[Bake|bake]] [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortasdeaceitedeolivaromeroytomillo #rosemary #flour #bake #dough #thyme #driedthyme #driedyeast #walnut #yeast #whitebread </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Yum!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nI like [[Tortilla Espa\u00f1ola|Tortilla espa\u00f1ola]] and I like [[Batatas harras]] (Lebanese [[Spiced potatoes|spiced potatoes]]), so decided to combine the two.  This is a [[Tortilla Espa\u00f1ola|Spanish omelette]] with [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Coriander|coriander]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 130 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 kg [[Potatoes|potatoes]], preferably ones which are not floury, eg Cara, Nadine, peeled and sliced\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], peeled and sliced\n| 2 bulbs [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 4 [[Chillies|chillies]], finely chopped\n| 70 g [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], finely chopped \n| 8 large [[Eggs|eggs]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]] to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a medium sized, deepish [[Frying pan|frying pan]] at a medium temperarure.\n| When hot, add the [[Potatoes|potatoes]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Chillies|chillies]].\n| Cover and reduce the heat, stirring from time to time until the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] are cooked and slightly [[Browned|browned]] (about 20 minutes).\n| Meanwhile, beat the [[Egg|egg]] and seasonings thoroughly in a bowl.\n| Drain off most of the excess [[Oil|oil]] and add the [[Potato|potato]] mixture to the [[Eggs|eggs]] and stir in the [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]].\n| Pour the whole lot back into the pan - there should be enough [[Oil|oil]] left to coat the bottom of the pan.\n| Increase the heat to medium again and cook the [[Omelette|omelette]] until the bottom and sides have set.\n| Turn out the [[Omelette|omelette]] onto a plate and slide it back into the pan upside down, so that the other side can be cooked. Alternatively, you can simply leave the omlette in the pan and place it under the [[Grill|grill]] until the top has set.\n| Once cooked, turn it out onto a plate and leave to cool. It is best served at room temperature.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Salad|salad]] or in a [[Baguette|baguette]].\n===Variations===\nUse as much or as little as you like of the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Chillies|chillies]] and [[Coriander|coriander]].  Add other [[Spices|spices]] if you wish.\n\n{{OmeletteRecipes}}\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Potato recipes|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Tortilla 'batatas harras']]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortillabatatasharras #chillies #garlic #potatoes #corianderleaves #onions #omelette #coriander #eggs #diced #egg </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Tortilla capuchina",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tortilla capuchina, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tortilla #asparagus #tortillacapuchina #potatoes #onion #tapa #breadcrumbs #eggs #parsley #garlic #potato \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This summery tortilla originates from La Mancha in Spain\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1150\n|PortionCalories = 287\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 4 or 8 as a [[Tapa|tapa]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Tortilla capuchina.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Great when local asparagus is out</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">June, up here in Norfolk, every other stall has fresh asparagus for sale.  This is a great way top use it.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis summery [[Tortilla|tortilla]] originates from La Mancha in [[Spain]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 400 g fresh green [[Asparagus|asparagus]] spears, trimmed and cut into 2.5 cm pieces\n| 8 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 350 g [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled and cut into smallish [[Dice|dice]]\n| [[Salt]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], thinly sliced\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 100 g fresh [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 8 [[Eggs|eggs]], beaten\n| 2 tablespoons chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Boil]] the [[Asparagus|asparagus]] for 5 minutes until just tender.\n| Drain, plunge into cold water and drain again.\n| Meanwhile, heat the [[Oil|oil]] to medium in a large-ish [[Frying pan|frying pan]].\n| Add the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and [[Salt|salt]] to taste.\n| Cook for about 10 minutes, turning regularly so that they do not [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] and cook for a further 5 minutes.\n| Stir in the [[Asparagus|asparagus]] and [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] and saut\u00e9 for 3 minutes.\n| Remove from the heat and drain off any excess [[Oil|oil]], reserving 1-2 tablespoons of the oil.\n| Mix the [[Eggs|eggs]], [[Parsley|parsley]] and a little more [[Salt|salt]] in a bowl.\n| Pour the [[Asparagus|asparagus]] and [[Potato|potato]] mixture into the same bowl.\n| Wipe the [[Frying pan|frying pan]] with [[Kitchen towel|kitchen towel]] and return it to the heat with the reserved [[Oil|oil]].\n| Pour the [[Egg|egg]] mixture into the pan and spread it evenly without stirring.\n| Cook for about 3 minutes until the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] is nearly set.\n| Flip the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] face downwards onto a plate and slide it back into the [[Frying pan|frying pan]] so that the other side will cook.\n| Keep the pan on the heat for a further couple of minutes, by which time the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] should be ready.\n| Cut into [[Wedges|wedges]] and serve warm (not hot).\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Salad|salad]] and [[Bread|bread]] or as a [[Tapa|tapa]] with some [[Olives|olives]].\n===Variations===\nAs asparagus has such a short season in the UK, you only have a few options if you want to make this at any time of the year.  Never having eaten tinned asparagus, I neither recommend nor decry it.  However I have eaten the white [[Asparagus#Esp\u00e1rrago de Navarra|Esp\u00e1rrago de Navarra]] which is available throughout the year in jars.  It tends to be much thicker than English asparagus so may need to be sliced, rather than cut into lengths.  It has an excellent flavour, although any resulting tortilla would not be as colourful as those made with the green variety.\n\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tortilla #asparagus #tortillacapuchina #potatoes #onion #tapa #breadcrumbs #eggs #parsley #garlic #potato </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tostas, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tostas #bread #oliveoil #bake #garlic #frenchloaf #tortilla #grilled #olive #brush #tomato \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Tostas are slices of bread which are brushed with oil and baked in the oven\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2120\n|PortionCalories = 530\n|DatePublished=28th July 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 16 minutes plus cooling time\n |PrepTime = 4 minutes\n |CookTime = 12 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Tostas.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Toast!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Be sure to make this with nice bread.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]])</span></span>\n}}\nTostas are slices of [[Bread|bread]] which are brushed with [[Oil|oil]] and [[Baked|baked]] in the [[Oven|oven]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 long loaf of [[Bread|bread]], [[Sliced on the diagonal|sliced on the diagonal]], 15 mm thick\n| [[Olive oil]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Brush]] the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] on each [[Bread|bread]] slice on one side only, making sure that you use enough [[Oil|oil]] to coat them properly. \n| Arrange, side by side on a shallow [[baking tray]] and [[Bake|bake]] for 6 minutes.\n| Turn the tray round in the [[Oven|oven]] and [[Bake|bake]] for a further 6 minutes.\n| Allow to cool.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe rubbed with [[Garlic|garlic]] or melt some [[Cheese|cheese]] on top of them.  [[Ham]] and [[Tomato|tomato]] are also used as toppings.  If your tostas are smallish, then you can make various [[Tapas|tapas]] by, for example, taking a slice of [[Tortilla|tortilla]] and an [[Olive|olive]], and skewering them to a tosta with a [[cocktail stick]].\n===Variations===\nYou can use [[Garlic|garlic]]-infused [[Olive oil|olive oil]] if you wish.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe length and width of your loaf will determine the number and size of the slices.  The [[Bread|bread]] in the image above was a normal [[French loaf]] - for bigger slices, you will need something rather wider.  Tostas will keep in an airtight container such as a [[Lock&Lock boxes|Lock&Lock bowl]].  I tried making these with ciabatta, but the resulting tostas turned our so hard that I almost broke my teeth on them, so stick to something with a similar texture to a [[French loaf]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tostas]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Tostas]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes|Tostas]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Tostas]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Tostas]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Tostas]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tostas #bread #oliveoil #bake #garlic #frenchloaf #tortilla #grilled #olive #brush #tomato </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=An authentic meat paella recipe from PaellaWorld\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#paella #rice #bomba #bayleaves #paellaworld #paprika #spain #redpepper #parsley #gardenpeas #tomatoes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An authentic paella recipe from someone who should know!  Dominic Green from PaellaWorld.co.uk\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2974\n|PortionCalories = 743\n|DatePublished=7th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:PaellaWorld_Cooking_paella.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\n\"Hola, Traditional Valencian [[Paella]] in my opinion is best eaten outdoors and even better with friends. In [[Spain]] many family members and friends come together to eat [[Paella]] at home, on the beach, in restaurants and at Fiesta time as anytime is a good time to eat Paella. Here are some Paella recipes to [[Help|help]] you on your Paella journey. Happy eats,  buena comida, buenos amigos (Good food, good friends) gracias.\"\n\n''Dominic Green'': [[Paella World]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 4 [[Chicken thighs]] or 3 chopped [[Chicken breasts|chicken breasts]]\n| 225g [[Chorizo]] sausage ring (sliced)\n| 400g [[Rabbit]] (Optional)\n| 1 medium [[Onion]] (Chopped)\n| Half [[Red pepper|red pepper]] (Chopped)\n| 200g chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 2 [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]] (crushed and chopped)\n| 4 strands of [[Saffron]] (if available)\n| Half  teaspoon of [[Paella]] Colourant\n| Half teaspoon of [[Paprika]] Dulce\n| 300g [[Bomba]] [[Rice]]\n| 100g [[Frozen]] [[Garden peas|garden peas]]\n| Small tin of [[Black olives|black olives]]\n| 250ml of [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 75 ml [[White wine|white wine]] (optional)\n| Water (if required)\n| 2 [[Bay leaves]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n| Chopped Fresh [[Parsley]]\n| [[Lemon wedges]] to garnish\n}}\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| In your [[Paella]] pan (38cm to 42cm recommended) pour in around 2 tablespoons of [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] and set heat to medium to high.\n| Add [[Chicken|chicken]] and [[Rabbit|rabbit]] (optional) and cook until [[Browned|browned]].\n| Add the sliced [[Chorizo|chorizo]] ring, [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Red pepper|red pepper]] and cook for 3 minutes until [[Onions|onions]] are starting to soften.\n| Add the [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], half tin of [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Wine|wine]], [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]. Then add [[Paprika]] Dulce, [[Paella]] Colourant, [[Saffron]] (Grind up the strands with a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]] to start the flavour flowing), [[Garden peas|garden peas]] and stir round (the smell from this should be amazing!).\n| Sprinkle the [[Bomba]] [[Rice]] evenly around the pan, stir in and bring back up to [[Boil|boil]] and turn down the heat to [[Simmer|simmer]] (add water if [[Rice|rice]] soaks up the liquid quickly).\n| Cook for a further 20 minutes or until the [[Bomba]] [[Rice]] is soft to bite. Keep stirring throughout so the [[Rice|rice]] does not stick to the bottom of the pan (Although in [[Spain]] Traditional [[Paella]] is cooked to stick to the bottom of the pan so the choice is yours?).\n| Add the [[Black olives|black olives]], remove the [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]] and stir in the fresh chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n| Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]]. Take off the heat and cover for 5 minutes to let all the ingredients truly infuse together.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Lemon wedges|lemon wedges]] and tuck in for a fantastic treat for you and your guests!!\n===Recipe source===\n* ''Dominic Green'' from [http://www.paellaworld.co.uk Paella World]: [[Paella World]] has kindly given Cookipedia permission to use this recipe.  [[Paella World]] can supply any specialist [[paella]] ingredients.\n===Chef's notes===\nEat the [[Meat|meat]] you like and take out the [[Meat|meat]] you don't like.\n\nAdd half teaspoon of hot [[Paprika|paprika]] if you like a bit of heat in your food. It also enhances the favours in the dish.\n\nDouble the amounts above if cooking for 8 and so on.\n===Paella recipes===\n* '''[[Paella alicantina]]'''\n* '''[[Vegetarian paella]]'''\n* '''Another [[Vegetarian paella (2)|Vegetarian paella]]\n* '''[[Traditional seafood paella]]'''\n* '''[[Traditional meat paella]]'''\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I can see why he's smiling</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Quite a big pan that.  Not sure if I've got one that large in my cupboards!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Game recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#paella #rice #bomba #bayleaves #paellaworld #paprika #spain #redpepper #parsley #gardenpeas #tomatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Traditional seafood paella",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Another authentic seafood paella recipe, this one from PaellaWorld\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#paella #rice #seafood #bomba #bayleaves #lemonwedges #paellaworld #paprika #onion #onions #langoustines \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An authentic paella recipe from Dominic Green from PaellaWorld.co.uk\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2049\n|PortionCalories = 512\n|DatePublished=7th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:PaellaWorld_Cooking_paella.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">That's a big pan</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Even Lakeland hasn't got one that big \ud83d\ude03</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n\"Hola, Traditional Valencian [[Paella]] in my opinion is best eaten outdoors and even better with friends. In [[Spain]] many family members and friends come together to eat [[Paella]] at home, on the beach, in restaurants and at Fiesta time as anytime is a good time to eat Paella. Here are some Paella recipes to [[Help|help]] you on your Paella journey. Happy eats,  buena comida, buenos amigos (Good food, good friends) gracias.\"\n\n''Dominic Green'': [[Paella World]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 200g [[Prawns]] (400g if using unpeeled)\n| 200g [[Mussels]]\n| 100g [[Squid]] rings\n| 200g [[Clams]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion]] (Chopped)\n| Half [[Red pepper|red pepper]] (Chopped)\n| 200g chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 2 [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]]\n| 4 strands of [[Saffron]] (if available)\n| Half  teaspoon of [[Paella]] Colourant\n| Half teaspoon of [[Paprika]] Dulce\n| 300g [[Bomba]] [[Rice]]\n| 100g [[Frozen]] [[Garden peas|garden peas]]\n| Small tin of [[Black olives|black olives]]\n| 250ml of [[Vegetable|vegetable]] or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 125ml [[Glass|glass]] of [[White wine|white wine]] (optional)\n| Water (if required)\n| 2 [[Bay leaves]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n| Chopped Fresh [[Parsley]]\n| [[Lemon wedges]] to garnish\n}}\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Chop the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Onion]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]]\n| In your [[Paella]] pan (38cm to 42cm recommended) pour in around 2 tablespoons of [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] and set heat to medium to high. Add [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Red pepper|red pepper]] and cook for 3 minutes until [[Onions|onions]] are starting to soften.\n| Add the [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], half tin of [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Wine|wine]], [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]. \n| Then add [[Paprika]] Dulce, [[Paella]] Colourant, [[Saffron]] (Grind up the strands with a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]] to start the flavour flowing), [[Garden peas|garden peas]] and stir round (the smell from this should be amazing!).\n|  Sprinkle the [[Bomba]] [[Rice]] evenly around the pan, stir in and bring back up to [[Boiling|boiling]] and turn down the heat to [[Simmer|simmer]] (add water if [[Rice|rice]] soaks up the liquid quickly).\n| Cook for a further 20 minutes or until the [[Rice|rice]] is soft to bite. Keep stirring throughout so the [[Bomba]] [[Rice]] does not stick to the bottom of the pan (Although in [[Spain]] Traditional [[Paella]] is cooked to stick to the bottom of the pan so the choice is yours?).\n| You can add the [[Seafood|seafood]] to the pan at this point and cook for a further 5 minutes but I prefer to cook the [[Seafood|seafood]] in a separate pan in [[White wine|white wine]] until all the [[Mussels|mussels]] and [[Clams|clams]] have opened (but discard any ones that do not open) then add this to the [[Bomba]] [[Rice]] and stir in with the [[Black olives|black olives]], remove the [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]] and stir in the fresh chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n| Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]]. Take off the heat and cover for 5 minutes to let all the ingredients truly infuse together.   Serve with [[Lemon wedges|lemon wedges]] and tuck in for a fantastic treat for you and your guests!!\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Lemon wedges|lemon wedges]] and tuck in for a fantastic treat for you and your guests!!\n===Recipe source===\n\n* ''Dominic Green'' from [http://www.paellaworld.co.uk Paella World]: [[Paella World]] has kindly given Cookipedia permission to use this recipe.  [[Paella World]] can supply any specialist paella ingredients.\n===Chef's notes===\nHad any [[Seafood|seafood]] you like\u0085 [[Scallops|scallops]], [[Crab|crab]], [[Octopus]], [[Langoustines]] or even [[Lobster|lobster]] as an example and take out the [[Seafood|seafood]] you don\u0092t like.\n\nAdd half teaspoon of hot [[Paprika|paprika]] if you like a bit of heat in your food. It also enhances the favours in the dish.\n\nI usually buy 6 to 8 big [[Prawns|prawns]] or [[Langoustines|langoustines]] to lay on top of the finished dish for excellent presentation which is guaranteed to impress your guests!\n\nDouble the amounts above if cooking for 8 and so on.\n===Paella recipes===\n* '''[[Paella alicantina]]'''\n* '''[[Vegetarian paella]]'''\n* '''Another [[Vegetarian paella (2)|Vegetarian paella]]\n* '''[[Traditional seafood paella]]'''\n* '''[[Traditional meat paella]]'''\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#paella #rice #seafood #bomba #bayleaves #lemonwedges #paellaworld #paprika #onion #onions #langoustines </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Tray-baked butternut squash pisto",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tray-baked butternut squash pisto recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#butternutsquash #traybakedbutternutsquashpisto #oliveoil #pinenuts #bananashallots #ratatouille #toasted #port #cuminseeds #clovesofgarlic #sherryvinegar \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Pisto is the Spanish equivalent of ratatouille. This tray-baked squash pisto is almost a sweet and sour dish, tempered with the sherry vinegar\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1051\n|PortionCalories = 262\n|DatePublished=11th January 2015\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Tray-baked butternut squash pisto.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I-Spy ciabatta!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Superb recipe, thanks Julia.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe was going to be cooked in a pan only but in the end it made far more sense to tray-bake it.  The sugary squash and port, combined with the sherry vinegar make this a sweet and sour dish.\n[[Image:Tray-baked butternut squash pisto oven ready.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready for the oven]]\n\n''Pisto is the [[Spanish]] equivalent of [[Ratatouille|ratatouille]].''\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1.2 kg [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]], peeled and chopped into 2cm pieces - about 800g once prepared\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Old India Taco Seasoning]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| A good pinch of [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 5 [[banana shallots]], peeled and roughly sliced\n| 3 [[Sweet peppers]] of any colour, deseeded, halved and cut into rings\n| 1 [[Indian green chillies|Green Indian chili]], thinly sliced, deseeded if you wish\n| 1 large [[Sprig of rosemary|sprig of rosemary]], left whole\n| 4 freshly picked [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]]\n| 5 [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]], peeled and smashed\n| 1 teaspoon dried [[Mexican oregano]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of dried [[epazote]]\n| 1 teaspoon of whole [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]]\n| A pinch of freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| 5cm [2\"] [[cinnamon]] bark\n| A handful of [[green beans]] or other vegetables of choice\n| 180ml [[Passata|passata]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Port|port]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n}}\n''' to garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 tablespoons [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat your [[oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Pop the [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] chunks into a [[Lock and Lock box]], add the [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], shake like mad to mix and set to one side.\n| Add the [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] and all of the [[olive oil]] to a large [[Frying pan]] \n| Gently saut\u00e9 the [[Shallots]] for 15 minutes, adding the whole smashed garlic for the last 5 minutes\n| Pour the Shallots, garlic and oil into a large [[oven tray]]\n| As we're going to add the vegetables next, it's handy to toss them in the pan or wok to soak up all the remaining olive oil.\n| [[Sieve|Sieve]] the [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] pieces (or pop them into a salad spinner) to remove any liquid that may have leached out.\n| Add the sweet peppers, and all of the herbs and spices to the oven tray and mix really well\n| Cover this with a layer of [[tin-foil]] and bake in the oven for 1 hour\n| After one hour, remove the foil, add the passata, port, sherry vinegar and green beans, mix well and bake, uncovered for 15 minutes.\n| Remove the bay leaves, rosemary sprig and cinnamon and serve.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe garnished with [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]]\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you don't have [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and &#189; teaspoon of unsmoked [[Paprika]] will work just as well.\n{{Template:Pisto recipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butternutsquash #traybakedbutternutsquashpisto #oliveoil #pinenuts #bananashallots #ratatouille #toasted #port #cuminseeds #clovesofgarlic #sherryvinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Tuna and bean salad with fennel and roasted peppers",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Tuna and bean salad with fennel and roasted peppers a Barbecue recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#sherryvinegar #fennel #beans #onion #fennelseeds #tunaandbeansaladwithfennelandroastedpeppers #lemonjuice #oreganoleaves #aniseed #chickpeas #fish \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=If you have not tried finely sliced fennel bulbs in a salad, you are missing out on a subtle, almost onion like crunch\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1357\n|PortionCalories = 339\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Ready for the tuna\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes (incl [[roasting the peppers]]\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Bean_salad_with_fennel_&_roasted_peppers_recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Glorious</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Absolutely glorious</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nIf you have not tried finely sliced [[Fennel|fennel]] bulbs in a [[Salad|salad]], you are missing out on a subtle, almost [[Onion|onion]]-like crunch with very slight [[Aniseed|aniseed]] overtones. Brilliant with [[Fish|fish]]. Add some [[Beans|beans]] for body, [[Peppers|peppers]] for richness and [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]], just because you can, you have a complete, gorgeous meal. Try it\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 400 g can of [[Haricot beans|haricot beans]], rinsed many times and then drained.\n| 2 sweet [[Bell peppers|bell peppers]], any colour.\n| 1 [[Fennel bulb|fennel bulb]], sliced finely, green tops reserved, if you are lucky enough to find a seller that retains them!\n| Half an [[Onion|onion]], very thinly sliced.\n| A small handful of freshly chopped [[oregano leaves]].\n| A large handful of freshly chopped [[parsley leaves]].\n| [[Sea salt]] to taste.\n| 2 fresh [[tuna]] steaks sliced in half to make 4 thin steaks , (about 100 g each) so they cook quickly. \n| 4 tablespoons of [[extra virgin olive oil]].\n| A squeeze of fresh [[lemon juice]].\n| 1 teaspoon [[fennel seeds]], crushed in a [[mortar and pestle]].\n| 3 teaspoons of [[sherry vinegar]].\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat a barbecue or oven griddle.\n# [[Roasted red pepper|Roast the bell peppers as shown here]], remove skin and seeds then tear into strips.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n|Cover the beans in fresh water, no salt, and warm them through, remove from the heat and leave in the cooking water.\n| Place the [[fennel seeds]], sliced [[fennel]] and [[onions]] together with the roasted pepper strips and oregano in a serving bowl. Add half of the parsley and reserved fennel tops if you had any. Toss well.\n| Brush the tuna steaks with olive oil and season with salt.\n| Sear on a hot griddle for 1 minutes a side.  Remove and rest, covered, for 4 minutes. \n| Meanwhile, drain the beans and add to the salad bowl.\n| Drizzle with [[sherry vinegar]], [[lemon juice]] and the remaining [[olive oil]].\n| Serve the tuna on individual plates, laid over the salad, sprinkled with the remaining chopped herbs.\n}}\n===Alternatives===\nTry a variety of [[beans]], most beans work very well in a salad like this.  [[Butter beans]], [[chick peas]]. [[kidney beans]] etc.  Dried beans are good too if you remember to prepare them ahead of time.\n===Chef's note===\nIf you can't find [[sherry vinegar]], then try harder as it's an invaluable condiment Or use [[red wine vinegar]] with a pinch of sugar!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sherryvinegar #fennel #beans #onion #fennelseeds #tunaandbeansaladwithfennelandroastedpeppers #lemonjuice #oreganoleaves #aniseed #chickpeas #fish </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Turkey breasts with rice, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#rice #oliveoil #turkeybreastswithrice #turkey #ham #garlic #chives #spanish #preserved #roastedredpeppers #salad \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I refuse to cook turkey at Christmas prefering to treat it just the same as any other meat and serve it when I want to\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 983\n|PortionCalories = 491\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  30 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Turkey breasts with rice recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Turkey is lovely</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just make sure you buy British \ud83d\ude9c</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nI refuse to cook [[Turkey|turkey]] at Christmas prefering to treat it just the same as any other [[Meat|meat]] and serve it when I want to.  In the UK, it is gradually becoming easier to find turkey outside of the big cities all year round and the number of available recipes is increasing.  In this [[Spanish]] recipe it is served with Bomba [[Rice|rice]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 120g Bomba [[Rice|rice]] \n| 240ml hot water\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Chives]], snipped\n| 40g cooked [[Ham|ham]], chopped\n| 4 [[Preserved|preserved]], [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]], cut into strips\n| 150g [[Frozen|frozen]] [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]], cooked\n| 300g [[Turkey|turkey]] breast fillets\n| A further 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Salt]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a saucepan, lightly saut\u00e9 the [[Garlic|garlic]] and then stir in the [[Rice|rice]], cooking until the rice [[Grains|grains]] start to appear translucent.\n| Add the hot water and a little [[Salt|salt]].\n| Cover, and allow to [[Simmer|simmer]] gently for 20 minutes.\n| Remove from the heat and fluff up with a fork to allow the [[Steam|steam]] to evaporate. \n| Mix with the [[Chives|chives]], [[Ham|ham]], [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Corn|corn]].\n| Whilst the [[Rice|rice]] is cooking [[Brush|brush]] the [[Turkey|turkey]] fillets lightly with the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and saut\u00e9 on both sides until properly cooked.  \n| Remove from the pan and season.\n| Serve with the warm [[Rice|rice]] [[Salad|salad]].\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#rice #oliveoil #turkeybreastswithrice #turkey #ham #garlic #chives #spanish #preserved #roastedredpeppers #salad </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Vegetarian paella, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#vegetarianpaella #simmer #saffron #broadbeans #onion #greenpepper #dop #rice #tomatoes #mushrooms #aubergine \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A vegetarian version of the traditional paella valenciana\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1247\n|PortionCalories = 311\n|DatePublished=7th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Vegetarian paella, with roasted garlic garnish\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Vegetarian paella recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I LOVE the garlic bulb</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Clever old Julia!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nA vegetarian version of the traditional [[Paella|paella]] valenciana.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], chopped\n| [[Garlic]], to taste. finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 1 [[Green pepper|green pepper]], chopped\n| 1 [[Aubergine|aubergine]], sliced, sprinkled with a little [[Salt|salt]] and drained\n| 125 g [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], sliced\n| 100 g [[Garden peas]]\n| 100 g fine [[Green beans|green beans]]\n| 100 g small [[Broad beans|broad beans]]\n| 500 ml [[Paella rice|paella rice]]\n| 2 tins [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], drained or [[tomate frito]], to taste \n| 1 ltre warm or hot water or [[Vegetable stock|vegetable stock]]\n| A few strands of [[Saffron|saffron]], crushed and dissolved in a little warm water\n| 4-6 [[Artichoke hearts|artichoke hearts]]\n| 1 jar [[Preserved|preserved]] [[Red peppers|red peppers]], cut inti strips\n| [[Parsley]], finely chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or a [[Paellera|paellera]].\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Green pepper|green pepper]] and and allow to soften and colour slightly.\n| [[Dice]] the [[Aubergine|aubergine]] and add to pan, allowing to saut\u00e9 for a couple of minutes. \n| Add the [[Peas|peas]], fine [[Beans|beans]], [[Broad beans|broad beans]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] over a medium heat for a few minutes.\n| Stir in the [[Rice|rice]] and saut\u00e9 for a minute or two. \n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and mix well, stirring the [[Rice|rice]] at the bottom to make sure that it does not stick.\n| Stir in the water and the [[Saffron|saffron]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] uncovered over a low heat.\n| When nearly done add the [[Artichoke hearts|artichoke hearts]] and strips of [[Red pepper|red pepper]]. \n| When it is cooked, cover and allow to stand for about 5 minutes before serving.\n| Garnish with the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nUse any [[Vegetables|vegetables]] you like, in any quantities.\n===Chef's notes===\nIt is best to use proper [[Paella rice|paella rice]], eg Bah\u00eda or Bomba ([[DOP]] Valencia).  I think you can get this in Waitrose and Tesco.\n\nJars of [[Preserved|preserved]] [[Peppers|peppers]] such as '''[[Bell peppers#Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa|Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa]]''' ([[DOP]] Navarra) can be obtained from delicatessens.  In the absence of [[Spanish]] ones, Lidl sells a fairly respectable Turkish alternative.\n===See also===\n* Another [[Vegetarian paella (2)|Vegetarian paella]] recipe\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Paella vegetarian]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Paella vegetarian]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Paella vegetarian]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Paella vegetarian]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Paella vegetarian]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Paella vegetarian]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#vegetarianpaella #simmer #saffron #broadbeans #onion #greenpepper #dop #rice #tomatoes #mushrooms #aubergine </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Vegetarian paella (2)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Another authentic vegetarian paella recipe, this one from PaellaWorld\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#paella #rice #paellaworld #paprika #bayleaves #bomba #tomatoes #gardenpeas #courgette #saffron #parsley \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An authentic paella recipe from someone who should know!  Dominic Green from PaellaWorld.co.uk\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1206\n|PortionCalories = 301\n|DatePublished=7th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:PaellaWorld_Cooking_paella.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love the picture</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I already feel that I'm transported to a Spanish market square!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\n\"Hola, Traditional Valencian [[Paella]] in my opinion is best eaten outdoors and even better with friends. In [[Spain]] many family members and friends come together to eat [[Paella]] at home, on the beach, in restaurants and at Fiesta time as anytime is a good time to eat Paella. Here are some Paella recipes to [[Help|help]] you on your Paella journey. Happy eats,  buena comida, buenos amigos (Good food, good friends) gracias.\"\n\n''Dominic Green'': [[Paella World]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 8 [[Green beans|green beans]] (Chopped)\n| 150g [[Asparagus]] spears (ends trimmed)\n| 1 [[Courgette|courgette]] (Sliced)\n| 1 medium [[Carrot]] ([[Diced]])\n| 1 medium [[Onion]] (Chopped)\n| Half [[Red pepper|red pepper]] (Chopped)\n| 200g chopped tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 2 [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]]\n| 4 strands of [[Saffron]] (if available)\n| Half teaspoon of [[Paella]] Colourant\n| Half teaspoon of [[Paprika]] Dulce\n| 300g [[Bomba]] [[Rice]]\n| 100g [[Frozen]] [[Garden peas|garden peas]]\n| Small tin of [[Black olives|black olives]]\n| 250ml of [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| 125ml of [[White wine|white wine]] (optional)\n| Water (if required)\n| 2 [[Bay leaves]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n| Chopped Fresh [[Parsley]]\n| [[Lemon wedges]] to garnish\n}}\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Chop the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Onion]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]].\n| In your [[Paella]] pan (38cm to 42cm recommended) pour in around 2 tablespoons of [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] and set heat to medium to high.\n| Add [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Red pepper|red pepper]], [[Carrot|carrot]], [[Green beans|green beans]] and cook for 3  minutes until [[Onions|onions]] are starting to soften.\n| Add the [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], [[Asparagus|asparagus]], [[Courgette|courgette]], half tin of [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Wine|wine]], [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] and bring to the [[Boil|boil]].\n| Then add [[Paprika]] Dulce, [[Paella]] Colourant, [[Saffron]] (Grind up the strands with a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]] to start the flavour flowing), [[Garden peas|garden peas]] and stir round (the smell from this should be amazing!).\n| Sprinkle the [[Bomba]] [[Rice]] evenly around the pan, stir in and bring back up to [[Boiling|boiling]] and turn down the heat to [[Simmer|simmer]] ( add water if [[Rice|rice]] soaks up the liquid quickly).\n| Cook for a further 20 minutes or until the [[Rice|rice]] is soft to bite. Keep stirring throughout so the [[Bomba]] [[Rice]] does not stick to the bottom of the pan (Although in [[Spain]] Traditional [[Paella]] is cooked to stick to the bottom of the pan so the choice is yours).\n| Add the [[Black olives|black olives]], remove the [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]] and stir in the fresh chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]. Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n| Take off the heat and cover for 5 minutes to let all the ingredients truly infuse together.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Lemon wedges|lemon wedges]] and tuck in for a fantastic treat for you and your guests!!\n===Recipe source===\n* ''Dominic Green'' from [http://www.paellaworld.co.uk Paella World]: [[Paella World]] has kindly given Cookipedia permission to use this recipe.  [[Paella World]] can supply any specialist [[paella]] ingredients.\n===Chef's notes===\nExperiment and add [[Vegetables|vegetables]] you like\u0085.[[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] or [[Artichoke hearts|artichoke hearts]] as an example and take out those you don\u0092t.\n\nAdd half teaspoon of hot [[Paprika|paprika]] if you like a bit of heat in your food. It also enhances the favours in the dish.\n\nUse of [[Meat|meat]] substitute eg [[Veggie|veggie]] [[Sausages|sausages]] can be added.\n\nDouble the amounts above if cooking for 8 and so on.\n==See also==\n* Another [[Vegetarian paella]] recipe\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#paella #rice #paellaworld #paprika #bayleaves #bomba #tomatoes #gardenpeas #courgette #saffron #parsley </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Wahaca frijoles Mexican recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chorizo #beans #wahacafrijoles #blackbeans #sourcream #onion #coriander #butter #lancashirecheese #garlic #tortilla \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Wahaca serve two versions of friioles negros (black beans) at their restaurants. \"Tommi\" Miers published this recipe when asked by a blogger\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 731\n|PortionCalories = 182\n|DatePublished=27th August 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  5 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Wahaca frijoles recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tex Mex tasty</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice and easy way to get your Mexican fix!  Best with Queso Fresco cheese</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Wahaca]] serve two versions of frijoles negros (''[[Black beans|black beans]]'') at their restaurants.  When a blogger asked Thomasina ''\"Tommi\"'' Miers if she could have the recipe, this is what Tommi kindly published.\n\nThe base recipe is the same, the toppings are the variation: crumbled [[Chorizo|chorizo]] or [[Lancashire cheese]] and [[Sour cream|sour cream]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 400g cooked [[Black beans|black beans]]\n| \u00bd [[Red chilli|red chilli]]\n| 2 stems of [[Coriander|coriander]]\n| 50g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 small white [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped\n| 2 [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]], finely chopped\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Cook the [[Onion|onion]] in the [[Butter|butter]] until soft then add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and cook for a further minute. \n| Drain the [[Beans|beans]] reserving the cooking liquid.\n| Add the cooked [[Beans|beans]] with a little of their cooking liquid and whiz in the [[Food processor|food processor]].\n| Remove to a bowl and season to taste.\n| Allow to cool and serve with finely chopped [[Shallots|shallots]], a garnish of [[Coriander|coriander]] and a crumbling of [[Chorizo|chorizo]]. \n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nCrumbled [[Chorizo|chorizo]] ''or'' [[Grated|grated]] [[Lancashire]] and [[Sour cream|sour cream]], a bowl of [[Tortilla|tortilla]] crisps and a cold [[Beer|beer]]!\n===Recipe source===\n\n* http://www.wahaca.co.uk/2009/08/frijoles-recipe/\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chorizo #beans #wahacafrijoles #blackbeans #sourcream #onion #coriander #butter #lancashirecheese #garlic #tortilla </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Yellow rice (Spanish)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Yellow rice (Spanish), Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#onion #chickenstock #rice #saffronstrands #garlic #saffron #chillies #longgrainrice #jalepenochilislices #boiledorsimmered #coriander \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Saffron give this dish a sunny tint and a distinct aroma\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 796\n|PortionCalories = 132\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes \n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Yellow rice (Mexican) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Sunny rice!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">With a very subtle aroma.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Yellow rice (Mexican) ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Yellow rice - The ingredients]]\n[[Saffron]] give this dish a sunny tint and a distinct aroma.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 200g (7 oz) [[long grain rice]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[vegetable oil]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of [[saffron strands]]\n| 1 small [[onion]], finely chopped\n| 2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, crushed\n| 475 ml (16 fl oz) good [[chicken stock]]\n| 50 g (2 oz) pickled [[jalepeno chili slices]]\n| sea [[salt]]\n| Fresh [[coriander leaves]], chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a sieve, rinse the [[rice]] for a few minutes under cold running water  to remove excess starch.  The water should run clear once done\n| Heat the oil in a pan and fry the [[onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 4 minutes until soft and translucent\n| Mix the rice into the [[onion]] mix and stir well to coat all of the rice\n| Drop in the [[saffron strands]]\n| Add the [[chicken stock]], bring to the boil and [[simmer]], covered, for 25 minutes or until the rice has absorbed all of the liquid.  A sheet or so of [[tin-foil]] under the pan lid helps to make a good seal\n| Add extra water if the [[rice]] dries out before it's cooked\n| Add the chopped [[chillies]] and add [[salt]] to taste\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe in a large bowl, garnished with [[coriander]] leaves\n===Variations===\nServe cold as a salad.\n\nIf you don't want to add [[chillies]], try some sliced [[roasted red peppers]] instead.\n===Chef's note===\nIf you don't have [[saffron]], use a teaspoon of [[turmeric powder]] and add when you add the rice to the oil.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Rice]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Rice]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#onion #chickenstock #rice #saffronstrands #garlic #saffron #chillies #longgrainrice #jalepenochilislices #boiledorsimmered #coriander </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It uses the whole [[Carrots|carrots]] whereas if made in a [[Juicer|juicer]] the pulp will be wasted.\n\nThis is a translation of a recipe in '''Thermomix TM31 Imprescindible para tu cocina''', which is the book you receive when buying a [[Thermomix]] in [[Spain]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 350g [[Carrots|carrots]], peeled\n| 1 [[Lemon|lemon]], peeled, pith and [[Seeds|seeds]] removed\n| 100g [[Sugar|sugar]] (see Chef's notes below)\n| 500g water (approx)\n| 6 or 8 ice cubes\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Chop the [[Carrots|carrots]] '''5 seconds / Speed 5'''.\n| Add the [[Lemon|lemon]], [[Sugar|sugar]], water and ice cubes and set for '''3 minutes / Speed 10'''.\n| If it is not smooth enough for you, repeat the operation for a little longer.\n| Add the basket to the bowl to strain it, hold it down with the spatula and pour into a jug filled with ice.\n| If it is well blended, there is no need to strain it.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Sugar|sugar]] content is high and can be cut down.  I found the [[Juice|juice]] to be very sweet and feel that 60g is sufficient.  However, I did not pour mine over a jug of ice, which would have made it less sweet.\n\nYou might need ear plugs when processing at '''Speed 10'''!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Drink and beverage recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#carrots #juice #thermomix #lemon #juicer #seeds #carrot #spain </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
